 <hr>
  <h3 align="center">Xhosa Bible: Isaiah</h3> 
 <p><a name="an_1:1">1:1</a> Umbono kaIsaya unyana ka-Amotsi, awawubonayo ngokusingisele kuYuda neYerusalem, ngemihla yoUziya, noYotam, noAhazi,  noHezekiya, ookumkani bakwaYuda.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:2">1:2</a> Yivani, mazulu; bekani indlebe, hlabathi, ngokuba kuthetha uYehova. Uthi, Ndikhulise abantwana ndabondla, besuka bakreqa kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:3">1:3</a> Inkomo iyamazi umniniyo, ne-esile liyawazi umkhombe wesitali senkosi yalo; ke yena uSirayeli akazi, abantu bam abaqiqi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:4">1:4</a> Hayi, luhlanga lonayo, bantu banobugwenxa, mbewu yabenza ububi, nyana bonakalisayo! Bamshiyile uYehova, bamgibile oyiNgcwele kaSirayeli, babuyela emva.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:5">1:5</a> Yini na ukuba nimane ukubethwa, nimane ukukwandisa ukutyeka?  Yonke intloko iyafa, yonke intliziyo inobulwelwe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:6">1:6</a> kuthabathele enkwalini yonyawo, kwesa entloko, akukho ndawo iphilileyo; ziinduma, nemivumbo, namanxeba amatsha:  akacudiswanga, akabotshwanga, akathanjiswanga ngaoli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:7">1:7</a> Kusenkangala elizweni lenu, imizi yenu itshiswe ngomlilo,  umhlaba wenu udliwa ngabasemzini phambi kwenu, uyinkangala njengokubhukuqwa kwabasemzini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:8">1:8</a> Isele ke intombi enguZiyon, njengexhobongo esidiliyeni,  njengephempe entsimini yemixoxozi, njengomzi ongqingiweyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:9">1:9</a> Koko uYehova wemikhosi wasisalisela intwana esindileyo,  singe saba njengeSodom, singe safana neGomora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:10">1:10</a> Liveni ilizwi likaYehova, baphathi baseSodom; wubekeleni indlebe umyalelo kaThixo wethu, bantu baseGomora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:11">1:11</a> Yeyani na kum le mibingelelo yenu mininzi kangaka? utsho uYehova. Ndidikiwe ngamadini anyukayo eenkunzi zeegusha,  namanqatha amathole atyetyisiweyo; negazi leenkunzi ezintsha,  neleemvana, neleebhokhwe, andilinanzile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:12">1:12</a> Xa niza kubonakala ebusweni bam, ngubani na okufunileyo oko esandleni senu, ukugqusha iintendelezo zam?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:13">1:13</a> Nize ningaphindi nizise mnikelo wakudla ukhohlakeleyo;  isiqhumiso silisikizi kum; ukuthwasa kwenyanga, nesabatha,  nokumema intlanganiso, ubutshinga kunye nengqungquthela,  andinakubuthwala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:14">1:14</a> Ukuthwasa kweenyanga zenu, namaxesha enu amisiweyo,  umphefumlo wam uwathiyile; asuka aba bubunzima kum; ndidiniwe kukuwathwala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:15">1:15</a> Ekoluleni kwenu izandla zenu, ndiya kuwafihla amehlo am kuni; nokuba nandise ukuthandaza, andiyi kuva; izandla zenu zizele ngamagazi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:16">1:16</a> Zihlambeni, ziqaqambiseni; susani ububi beentlondi zenu phambi kwamehlo am;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:17">1:17</a> yekani ukwenza ububi; fundani ukwenza okulungileyo;  khathalelani ukugweba; lulekani isibhovubhovu; gwebani ityala lenkedama; lithetheni ityala lomhlolokazi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:18">1:18</a> Khanize sibonisane, utsho uYehova; nokuba izono zenu zide zavela zanjengengubo ebomvu, zoba mhlophe njengekhephu; nokuba zide zayingqombela njengebala elibomvu, zovela zinjengoboya begusha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:19">1:19</a> Ukuba nithe navuma naphulaphula, nodla izinto ezilungileyo zelizwe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:20">1:20</a> ukuba nithe anavuma, naba neenkani, nodliwa likrele; kuba umlomo kaYehova uthethile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:21">1:21</a> Yoo! Utheni na ukuba lihenyukazi umzi lo, ubunyanisile;  ubuzele kokusesikweni; ubulungisa bebulala kuwo; ke ngoku ngabancinithi!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:22">1:22</a> Isilivere yakho isuke yaba ligwebu; iwayini yakho entle ingxengelelwe ngamanzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:23">1:23</a> Abathetheli bakho baziinjubaqa, ngamadlelana namasela;  bathanda izicengo bonke bephela, basukela imivuzo; ityala lenkedama abaligwebi, netyala lomhlolokazi alinakufika kubo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:24">1:24</a> Ngako oko itsho iNkosi, uYehova wemikhosi, imbalasane yakwaSirayeli, ukuthi, Yeha! Ndiya kuzithuthuzela kubabandezeli bam, ndiziphindezelele ezintshabeni zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:25">1:25</a> Ndosibuyisela phezu kwakho isandla sam, ndikunyibilikise ngokufezekileyo njengegolide, likhutshwe igwebu lakho, ndisuse yonke intsila yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:26">1:26</a> Ndobabuyisa abagwebi bakho njengokwasekuqaleni,  namaphakathi akho njengokwamatanci. Emveni koko kuya kuthiwa,  Wena ungumzi wobulungisa, uyinqaba enyanisileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:27">1:27</a> IZiyon iya kukhululwa ngokusesikweni, nabaguquki bayo ngobulungisa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:28">1:28</a> ukwaphulwa kwabakreqi naboni kube kunye, bapheliswe abamshiyayo uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:29">1:29</a> Ngokuba baya kudana yimiterebhinti ebeniyinqwenela, nibe neentloni yimiyezo ebeniyinyula;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:30">1:30</a> kuba niya kuba njengomterebhinti omagqabi omayo,  nanjengomyezo ongenamanzi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:31">1:31</a> nenjengele ibe yingxubuwa, nomsebenzi wayo ube yintlantsi,  kutshe kuphele kokubini kunye, kungabikho ucimayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:1">2:1</a> Ilizwi awalibonayo uIsaya unyana ka-Amotsi, ngokusingisele kuYuda neYerusalem.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:2">2:2</a> Ke kaloku kuya kuthi ekupheleni kwemihla, intaba yendlu kaYehova ivelele ezincotsheni zazo iintaba, izongamele iinduli,  zibe ngumsinga ukuya kuyo zonke iintlanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:3">2:3</a> Kuya kuhamba izizwe ezininzi, zithi, Yizani, sinyuke siye entabeni kaYehova, endlwini kaThixo kaYakobi; asiyalele iindlela zakhe, sihambe ngomendo wakhe. Kuba kuya kuphuma umyalelo eZiyon, nelizwi likaYehova eYerusalem.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:4">2:4</a> Uya kugweba phakathi kweentlanga, ohlwaye izizwe ezininzi;  ziwakhande amakrele azo abe ngamakhuba, nezikhali zazo zibe zizitshetshe zeediliya; uhlanga lungaphakamiseli uhlanga ikrele, nezizwe zingaphindi zifunde ukulwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:5">2:5</a> Ndlu kaYakobi, yizani, sihambe ekukhanyeni kukaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:6">2:6</a> Kuba ubalahlile abantu bakho, indlu kaYakobi; ngokuba bezele zizinto zasempumalanga, bengamatola njengamaFilisti, bebambene ngezandla nabantwana bezinye iintlanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:7">2:7</a> Ilizwe labo lizele yisilivere negolide; abunakuphela ubuncwane babo. Ilizwe labo lizele ngamahashe; azinakuphela iinqwelo zabo zokulwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:8">2:8</a> Ilizwe labo lizele zizithixo ezingeni; baqubuda kumsebenzi wezandla zabo, kwinto eyenziwe yiminwe yabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:9">2:9</a> Ophantsi uyagoba, nendoda ephakamileyo ithotyelwe phantsi,  ungabaxoleli ke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:10">2:10</a> Ngena eweni, uziselele eluthulini, ngenxa yokoyika uYehova,  nangenxa yozuko lobungangamsha bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:11">2:11</a> Amehlo aqwayingileyo esintu othotywa, noqhankqalazo lwamadoda lusibekeke; nguYehova yedwa owoba yingxonde ngaloo mini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:12">2:12</a> Kuba uYehova wemikhosi unemini eyozongamela izinto zonke ezinekratshi, ezinoqhankqalazo; nezinto zonke ezizinyusileyo zithotywe nezinto zonke ezisinyusileyo zithotywe ke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:13">2:13</a> Woyongamela imisedare yonke yaseLebhanon, emide,  ezinyusileyo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:14">2:14</a> nezonke ezinde, neenduli zonke ezizinyusileyo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:15">2:15</a> neenqaba zonke eziphakamileyo, neendonga zonke ezinqatyisiweyo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:16">2:16</a> neenqanawa zonke zaseTarshishe, nezinto zonke ezibonakala zinqweneleka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:17">2:17</a> Kosibekeka ukuzidla kwaba baphantsi, kuthotywe ukuqhankqalaza kwamadoda aphakamileyo. NguYehova yedwa owoba yingxonde ngaloo mini;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:18">2:18</a> izithixo ezingeni zothi shwaka zonke ziphela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:19">2:19</a> Bongena emiqolombeni yamawa nasemingxunyeni yomhlaba ngenxa yokoyika uYehova, nangenxa yozuko lobungangamsha bakhe,  ekuphakameni kwakhe ukuba angcangcazelise ilizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:20">2:20</a> Ngaloo mini umntu uya kuziphosa ezintukwini nasemalulwaneni izithixo zakhe ezingeni zesilivere, nezithixo zakhe ezingeni zegolide, abamenzelayo ukuze aqubude kuzo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:21">2:21</a> ukuze angene ezimfanteni zamawa nasemiqhokrweni yeengxondorha, ngenxa yokoyika uYehova, nangenxa yozuko lobungangamsha bakhe, ekuphakameni kwakhe ukuba angcangcazelise ilizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:22">2:22</a> Khanimyeke umntu omphefumlo usemathatheni akhe; ngokuba kuthiwa, Uyintoni na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:1">3:1</a> Ngokuba uyabona, iNkosi, uYehova wemikhosi, isusa eYerusalem nakwaYuda isixhaso nenkxaso, sonke isixhaso sesonka kwanesixhaso samanzi:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:2">3:2</a> igorha nendoda yokulwa, umgwebi nomprofeti, umvumisi nendoda enkulu,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:3">3:3</a> umthetheli wamashumi amahlanu, nobekekileyo, nomphakathi,  nesilumko esinobungcibi, nengqondi yokukhwitsa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:4">3:4</a> Ndobanika abathetheli abangabantwana, nabafekethi babalawule;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:5">3:5</a> bakhandanisane abantu ulowo nalowo, ulowo nalowa. Baya kusunduzana umntwana nendoda enkulu, ubuvuvu nabazukileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:6">3:6</a> Xa umntu aya kuthi abambelele kumzalwana wakhe endlwini kayise, athi, Unengubo wena, masiphathwe nguwe, oku kukhahleleka kube sesandleni sakho:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:7">3:7</a> wophimisela ngaloo mini athi, Andingebi mphilisi, endlwini yam kungekho sonka, kungekho ngubo; aninakundenza umphathi wabantu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:8">3:8</a> Ngokuba ikhahlelekile iYerusalem, awile amaYuda; ngokuba iilwimi zabo neentlondi zabo zichase uYehova, ukuba bawaphikise amehlo obuqaqawuli bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:9">3:9</a> Imbonakalo yobuso babo iyangqina ngabo, bayaxixela izono zabo njengeSodom, abakhanyeli. Yeha umphefumlo wabo, ngokuba beziphethe kakubi kwabona!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:10">3:10</a> Yithi kumalungisa, kuya kulunga kuwo; ngokuba isiqhamo sezenzo zawo aya kusidla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:11">3:11</a> Yeha ongendawo! Kuya kuba kubi kuye; ngokuba ukuphatha kwezandla zakhe kuya kwenziwa kuye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:12">3:12</a> Abantu bam bakhandaniswa ngabantwana, balawulwa ngabafazi.  Bantu bam, abakhokeli benu ngabandwendwisi, bayigqukile indlela yomendo wenu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:13">3:13</a> Usukile wema uYehova ukuba athethe ityala; umi ukuba agwebe ebantwini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:14">3:14</a> UYehova uya kungena ematyaleni namadoda amakhulu abantu bakhe, nabathetheli babo; esithi, Ke nina nisigqibile isidiliya; okuphangwe kusizana kusezindlwini zenu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:15">3:15</a> Ninani na, ukuba nibatyumze nje abantu bam, nibusile ubuso beentsizana? itsho iNkosi, uYehova wemikhosi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:16">3:16</a> Kananjalo uthi ke uYehova, Ngenxa enokuba zizidla iintombi zaseZiyon, zihamba zolule iintamo, zitshawula ngamehlo, zihamba zicothoza ukuhamba kwazo, zisenza isigampe esisezinyaweni zazo:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:17">3:17</a> ngako oko iNkosi yolujaduka ukakayi lweentombi zaseZiyon,  uYehova azihlube ubunkazana bazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:18">3:18</a> Ngaloo mini iNkosi yozisusa izihombo zemixokelelwane,  nesangqawe, nentsimbi yomqala,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:19">3:19</a> namajikazi, neewatsha, nezigqubuthelo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:20">3:20</a> neembasa, neenxaxhazo, neenqwemesha, namahlala okujoja,  namakhubalo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:21">3:21</a> nemisesane, namakhonkco empumlo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:22">3:22</a> nezambatho ezinqabileyo, neengubo zokwaleka ezingaphezulu,  neetyali, neengxowa zemali,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:23">3:23</a> nezipili, neeqhiya zelinen entle, neenkontsho, neengubo zokwaleka ezikrelekrele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:24">3:24</a> Kothi esikhundleni sobulawu ibe kukuvunda, esikhundleni sombhinqo ibe yintambo; esikhundleni seempothe ibe yimpempethe,  esikhundleni sengubo engwabungwabu ibe sisikhaka esirhwexayo;  ibe ngumtshiso esikhundleni sobunzwakazi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:25">3:25</a> Amadoda akho aya kuwa likrele, namagorha akho yimfazwe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:26">3:26</a> ancwine enze isijwili amasango ayo, ithi yona ikhutshululwe, ihlale phantsi emhlabeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:1">4:1</a> Abafazi abasixhenxe bobambelela ndodeni-nye ngaloo mini,  besithi, Sodla esethu isonka, sambathe ezethu iingubo; kodwa masibizwe ngegama lakho, ukususe ukungcikiveka kwethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:2">4:2</a> Ngaloo mini isithole sikaYehova siya kuba yinto enobukhazikhazi enobuqaqawuli, isiqhamo selizwe sibe yingangamsha nesihombo kwabasindileyo bakwaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:3">4:3</a> Wothi oshiyekileyo eZiyon, noseleyo eYerusalem, kuthiwe ungcwele, bonke ababhalelwe ebomini eYerusalem;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:4">4:4</a> yakuba ithe iNkosi yakuhlamba ukungcola kweentombi zaseZiyon, yawahlanza amagazi aseYerusalem phakathi kwayo ngomoya ogwebayo, nangomoya olulophu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:5">4:5</a> Wodala ke uYehova phezu kweendawo zonke zeentaba zeZiyon,  naphezu kweentlanganiso zayo, ilifu elingumsi emini,  nokudangazela komlilo ebusuku. Kuba phezu kobuqaqawuli obo bonke, kuya kubakho isigubungelo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:6">4:6</a> sibe ngumnquba ongumthunzi emini, ekubaleleni, sibe yindawo yokuzimela nokusithela esiphangweni nasemvuleni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:1">5:1</a> Intanda yam makhe ndiyivumele ingoma yentanda yam,  ngesidiliya sayo. Intanda yam ibe inesidiliya endulini echumayo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:2">5:2</a> yasigaba, yawemba amatye, yasityala imidiliya yohlobo, yakha inyango phakathi kwaso, yaxhola kuso umkhombe wokukhongozela iwayini. Yalinda ukuba sivelise iidiliya ezizizo; ke sona savelisa iidiliya ezingezizo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:3">5:3</a> Kaloku ke, bemi baseYerusalem, nani madoda akwaYuda,  khanahlule phakathi kwam nesidiliya sam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:4">5:4</a> Kube kusekho ntoni na eyenziwayo esidiliyeni sam,  endingayenzanga ke kuso? Kube kungani na ukuba ndikulinde ukuba sivelise iidiliya ezizizo, sisuke sivelise ezingezizo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:5">5:5</a> Kaloku ke makhe ndinazise into endiya kusenza yona isidiliya sam. Ndiza kususa uthango lwaso, sibe lidlelo; ndiya kuluchitha udonga lwaso, sibe yingqushu; ndisijece kuphele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:6">5:6</a> Asiyi kuthenwa, asiyi kuhlakulwa; siya kumila ubobo namakhakakhaka; ndiwawisele umthetho amafu, ukuba angani mvula phezu kwaso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:7">5:7</a> Kuba isidiliya sikaYehova wemikhosi yindlu kaSirayeli;  namadoda akwaYuda sisityalo sokumyolisa. Walinda ukuba kubekho okusesikweni, nanku ikukudywida; walinda ukuba kubekho ubulungisa, nanko ikukukhalisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:8">5:8</a> Yeha, abahlomela indlu kwindlu, abasondeza intsimi kwintsimi, kude kungabikho ndawo, nihlale nedwa phakathi kwelizwe!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:9">5:9</a> Ezindlebeni zam uthi uYehova wemikhosi, Inyaniso, izindlu ezininzi ziya kuba ngamanxuwa, ezinkulu, ezintle zingabi namhlali.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:10">5:10</a> Kuba ishumi leendima zesidiliya liya kwenza ibhate ibe nye,  nehomere yembewu yenze iefa yodwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:11">5:11</a> Yeha, abavuka kusasa, besukela isiselo esinxilisayo;  balibale kude kube lungcwalazi, ide ibatshise iwayini!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:12">5:12</a> Ibe luhadi nomrhubhe, ingqongqo nogwali, newayini, emgidini wabo; ke wona umsebenzi kaYehova abawubeki, nezenzo zezandla zakhe abaziboni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:13">5:13</a> Ngako oko abantu bam bayafuduswa bengazi, nabazukileyo kubo baba ngabafo bendlala, ingxokolo yabo itshiswa linxano.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:14">5:14</a> Ngako oko elabafileyo lizandisile, lakhame ngokungenamlinganiso; buhlile ubungangamela babo, nengxokozelo yabo, nengxolo yabo, nabadlamkileyo kubo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:15">5:15</a> Bayasibekeka abantu abaphantsi, athotywe amadoda aphakamileyo, athotywe amehlo abazidlayo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:16">5:16</a> ke yena uYehova wemikhosi uyaziphakamisa ngogwebo,  azingcwalise uThixo oyiNgcwele ngobulungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:17">5:17</a> Kodla iimvana apho, kunge kusedlelweni lazo; abasemathanga badlise emanxuweni ezityebi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:18">5:18</a> Yeha, abatsala ubugwenxa ngeentambo zenkohlakalo, nesono bange basitsala ngomqokozo wenqwelo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:19">5:19</a> abathi, Makasingxamise asikhawulezise isenzo sakhe, ukuze sibone; malisondele lize icebo loyiNgcwele kaSirayeli, ukuze sazi!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:20">5:20</a> Yeha, abathi okubi kulungile, okulungileyo kubi; abamisa ubumnyama endaweni yokukhanya, ukukhanya endaweni yobumnyama;  abamisa ubukrakra endaweni yobumnandi, ubumnandi endaweni yobukrakra!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:21">5:21</a> Yeha, abalumkileyo kwawabo amehlo, abanengqondo kokwabo ukubona!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:22">5:22</a> Yeha, abangamagorha okusela iwayini; abangamadoda akrotele ukuphithikeza isiselo esinxilisayo; abagwebela abangendawo,  besekeleze isicengo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:23">5:23</a> ubulungisa bamalungisa babususe kuwo!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:24">5:24</a> Ngako oko, njengokuba ulwimi lomlilo luzidla iindiza,  nesikhotha esomileyo sibohla edangatyeni: kwangokunjalo ingcambu yabo iya kuba njengento evundileyo, nentyantyambo yabo inyuke njengothuli; kuba besilahlile isiyalo sikaYehova wemikhosi, bayigiba intetho yoyiNgcwele kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:25">5:25</a> Ngenxa yoko uyavutha umsindo kaYehova kubantu bakhe;  usolule phezu kwabo isandla sakhe, uyababetha; zagungqa iintaba, izidumbu zabo zanjengenkunkuma phakathi kwezitrato.  Kuko konke oko, awubuyi umsindo wakhe, isandla sakhe sisolukile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:26">5:26</a> Uzinyusela ibhanile iintlanga zakude, azenzele ikhwelo eziphelweni zehlabathi; nanzo zisiza zikhawuleza ngamendu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:27">5:27</a> Akukho utyhafileyo, akukho ukhubekayo kuzo; azozeli,  azilali, umbhinqo wamanqe azo awuthukululeki, umtya weembadada zazo awuqhawuki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:28">5:28</a> Iintolo zazo zitsolile, nezaphetha zazo zonke zityediwe;  amanqina amahashe azo kuthiwa anjengeqhwitha, neevili zazo zinjengesaqhwithi. Ukubharhula kwazo kunjengengonyamakazi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:29">5:29</a> zibharhula njengeengonyama ezintsha, zigqume, ziyibambe inyamakazi, zimke nayo, kungabikho uhlangulayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:30">5:30</a> Zogquma phezu kwabo ngaloo mini, ngathi kukugquma kolwandle; babheke emhlabeni, nanko kumnyama yimbandezelo,  nokukhanya kumnyama emafini phezu kwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:1">6:1</a> Ngomnyaka wokufa kokumkani u-Uziya, ndayibona iNkosi ihleli etroneni ende enyukileyo; amasondo eengubo zayo ezirholayo azalisa itempile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:2">6:2</a> Kumi iiserafi ngaphezu kwayo, iyileyo inamaphiko amathandathu, ngamabini ifihle ubuso bayo, ngamabini ifihle iinyawo zayo, ngamabini iphaphazela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:3">6:3</a> Iyileyo idanduluke kuleyo isithi. Uyingcwele, uyingcwele,  uyingcwele uYehova wemikhosi; buzalise ihlabathi lonke ubuqaqawuli bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:4">6:4</a> Yadidizela imigubasi yeminyango lilizwi lowadandulukayo;  yaye indlu izele ngumsi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:5">6:5</a> Ndathi, Athi ke mna! Ngokuba ndithe shwaka, ngokuba ndiyindoda emlomo uyinqambi; ndihleli phakathi kwabantu abamilomo iyinqambi; ngokuba amehlo am abone ukumkani, uYehova wemikhosi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:6">6:6</a> Yaphaphazela yeza kum enye yeeserafi, iphethe ilahle elivuthayo, elithabathe ngesithabatho esibingelelweni;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:7">6:7</a> yalifikisa emlonyeni wam, yathi, Yabona, eli lahle lifikile nje emlonyeni wakho, bususiwe ubugwenxa bakho, nesono sakho sicanyagushelwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:8">6:8</a> Ndeva izwi leNkosi, lisithi, Ndothuma bani na? Ngubani na owosiyela?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:9">6:9</a> Ndathi, Ndikho, thuma mna. Yathi, Yiya, uthi kubo aba bantu,  Yivani, ukuva oku niya kuva, ningaqondi; qiqani, ukubona oku niya kubona, ningaqiqi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:10">6:10</a> Yityebise intliziyo yaba bantu, neendlebe zabo zenze zithi nkqi, namehlo abo uwavingce; hleze babone ngamehlo abo, beve ngeendlebe zabo, baqonde ngentliziyo yabo, babuye, baze baphiliswe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:11">6:11</a> Ndathi, Kube mzuzu ungakanani na, Nkosi? Yathi, Kude kuye kuchithwa imizi, ingabi nabemi, nezindlu zingabi namntu,  utshabalale umhlaba kube senkangala;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:12">6:12</a> uYehova amse kude umntu, abe maninzi amanxuwa phakathi kwelizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:13">6:13</a> Kuya kuthi, ukuba kusekho isahlulo seshumi khona, sibuye naso sibe yinto yokutshayelwa; njengomterebhinti nanjengomoki,  othi ekuwisweni kwawo kushiyeke isiphunzi; yimbewu engcwele ke isiphunzi eso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:1">7:1</a> Ke kaloku kwathi, ngemihla ka-Ahazi unyana kaYotam, unyana kaUziya, ukumkani wakwaYuda, wenyuka uRetsin ukumkani wama-Aram, enoPeka unyana kaRemaliya, ukumkani wakwaSirayeli,  weza eYerusalem, ukuba alwe nayo; akaba nako ke ukulwa nayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:2">7:2</a> Kwaxelwa kwindlu kaDavide, kwathiwa, Ama-Aram athelele kwabelakwaEfrayim. Yadidizela intliziyo yakhe nentliziyo yabantu bakhe, njengokudidizela kwemithi yehlathi phambi komoya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:3">7:3</a> Wathi uYehova kuIsaya, Khawuphume uye umkhawulele uAhazi,  wena noMasalela-obuya unyana wakho, ekupheleni komjelo wechibi lasentla, emendweni ongasentsimini yomxovuli weengubo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:4">7:4</a> uthi kuye, Gcinisa, uzole, ungoyiki, ingathambi intliziyo yakho ngenxa yezo zikhondo zibini zezikhuni eziqhumayo,  ekuvutheni komsindo kaRetsin nama-Aram, nonyana kaRemaliya;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:5">7:5</a> ngenxa enokuba ama-Aram namaEfrayim nonyana kaRemaliya becebile ububi ngawe, besithi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:6">7:6</a> Masinyuke siye kwelakwaYuda, silikruqule, silinqike libe lelethu, simise ukumkani phakathi kwalo, unyana kaTabhele;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:7">7:7</a> itsho iNkosi uYehova, ukuthi, Loo nto ayiyi kuma, ayiyi kubakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:8">7:8</a> Ngokuba intloko yama-Aram yiDamasko, intloko yeDamasko nguRetsin; kuya kuthi iseyiminyaka emashumi mathandathu anamihlanu, aqotywe amaEfrayim, angabi bantu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:9">7:9</a> Intloko yamaEfrayim kukwaSamari, intloko yakwaSamari ngunyana kaRemaliya. Ukuba nithe anakholwa, inene, aniyi kuqiniseka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:10">7:10</a> Waqokela uYehova, wathetha kuAhazi, esithi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:11">7:11</a> Zicelele umqondiso kuYehova uThixo wakho; cela ubhekise enzulwini kwelabafileyo, mhlawumbi ubhekise enyangweni phezulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:12">7:12</a> Wathi uAhazi, Andiyi kucela, andiyi kumlinga uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:13">7:13</a> Wathi yena, Khanive, ndlu kaDavide; kuyinto encinane na kuni ukudinisa abantu, ukuda oku nidinise noThixo wam?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:14">7:14</a> Ngako oko iya kuninika umqondiso ngokwayo iNkosi: uyabona,  intombi le iya kumitha, izale unyana, imthiye igama elinguImanuweli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:15">7:15</a> Uya kudla amasi nobusi, ade akwazi ukulahla okubi, anyule okulungileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:16">7:16</a> Kuba, engekakwazi umntwana lowo ukulahla okubi, anyule okulungileyo, woba selushiyiwe loo mhlaba, ukumkani bawo babini bakukruqulayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:17">7:17</a> UYehova uya kukuzisela wena nabantu bakho, nendlu kayihlo,  imihla ekungazanga kubekho ingangayo, kususela kwimini wemka ngayo uEfrayim kwaYuda; ngukumkani waseAsiriya ke lowo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:18">7:18</a> Kothi ngaloo mini uYehova ayenzele ikhwelo impukane esekupheleni kwemijelo yoMnayile waseYiputa, nenyosi esezweni laseAsiriya;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:19">7:19</a> zize, ziphumle zonke ziphela ezihlanjeni eziphakathi kwamaxandeka, nasezimfanteni zeengxondorha, nasezintangweni zonke zemiqaqoba, nasemadlelweni onke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:20">7:20</a> Ngaloo mini iNkosi iya kuguya ngesitshetshe esiqeshiweyo selasezinxwemeni zoMlambo, ngokumkani waseAsiriya, intloko noboya beenyawo; siphephethe neendevu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:21">7:21</a> Kothi ngaloo mini umntu aphilise ithokazi lenkomo neemazi zezimvu zibe mbini;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:22">7:22</a> kuthi ngokwehlisa kwazo kakhulu adle amasi; ngokuba baya kudla amasi nobusi bonke abo baseleyo phakathi kwelizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:23">7:23</a> Kothi ngaloo mini zonke iindawo ezazinewaka lemidiliya elimelwe liwaka leesilivere, zibe zezobobo namakhakakhaka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:24">7:24</a> Kuya kuyiwa khona neentolo nezaphetha; ngokuba lonke ilizwe liya kuba lubobo namakhakakhaka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:25">7:25</a> Zonke iintaba ebezigatywa ngamagaba, akuyi kuya kuzo,  ngokoyika ubobo namakhakakhaka; loba lelokugxothela iinkomo,  nokunyashwa ziigusha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:1">8:1</a> Wathi uYehova kum, Thabatha icwecwe elikhulu, ubhale kulo ngenkxola yabantu, uthi, NgoMaxhoba ayakhawuleza iinto eziphangiweyo zingxamile,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:2">8:2</a> Ndathabathela amangqina anyanisileyo, ooUriya umbingeleli,  noZekariya unyana kaYebherekiya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:3">8:3</a> Ndasondela kumprofetikazi, wamitha, wazala unyana. Wathi uYehova kum, Yithi igama lakhe nguMaxhoba ayakhawuleza iinto eziphangiweyo zingxamile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:4">8:4</a> Ngokuba, engekakwazi umntwana lo ukuthi, Bawo, nokuthi, Ma,  ubutyebi baseDamasko namaxhoba akwaSamari aya kuthwalelwa phambi kokumkani waseAsiriya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:5">8:5</a> Waqokela uYehova, wabuya wathetha kum, esithi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:6">8:6</a> Ngenxa enokuba abo bantu bewacekisa amanzi aseShilowa, la ahamba kuhle, benze imihlali noRetsin nonyana kaRemaliya:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:7">8:7</a> ngako oko, yabona, iNkosi inyusela phezu kwakho amanzi oMlambo, lawo anamandla amakhulu, kwaukumkani waseAsiriya nobunzima bakhe bonke. Wonyuka wona ube ngaphezu kwemisele yawo yonke, uhambe ngaphandle kweendonga zawo zonke,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:8">8:8</a> utyhudisele kwelakwaYuda, ukhukule, udlule, ubethe emqaleni;  kuthi ukunaba kwamahlelo awo kuzalise ububanzi belizwe lakho,  Imanuweli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:9">8:9</a> Bhavumani, zizwe, niqotywe; bekani indlebe, nonke mimandla ikude yehlabathi; bhinqani, niqotywe; bhinqani, niqotywe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:10">8:10</a> Cebani icebo, lotshitsha; thethani ilizwi, aliyi kuma;  ngokuba uThixo unathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:11">8:11</a> Kuba utshilo uYehova kum, eseyisa ngamandla, endithethisa ukuba ndingahambi ngendlela yabo bantu, ukuthi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:12">8:12</a> Ize ningathi, Ikukucetywa into yonke abathi abo bantu,  Ikukucetywa; nento eyoyikwa ngabo ningayoyiki,  ningangcangcazeliswa yiyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:13">8:13</a> UYehova wemikhosi, ngcwalisani yena nina, abe nguye enimoyikayo, abe nguye oningcangcazelisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:14">8:14</a> Woba yingcwele kuni; ke yena uya kuba lilitye lokubetheka,  neliwa lokukhubeka, kuzo zombini izindlu zakwaSirayeli, abe sisibatha nomgibe kubemi baseYerusalem.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:15">8:15</a> Abaninzi kubo baya kukhubeka apho, bawe, baphuke,  barhintyeleke, babanjiswe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:16">8:16</a> Bopha isingqino, tywina uqinise isiyalo kubafundi bam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:17">8:17</a> Ndiya kulindela kuYehova, lo ubusithelisayo ubuso bakhe kwindlu kaYakobi, ndithembele kuye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:18">8:18</a> Yabona, mna nabantwana andinikileyo uYehova,  singabemiqondiso nezimanga kwaSirayeli, ezivela kuYehova wemikhosi, ulohlala entabeni yaseZiyon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:19">8:19</a> Xa bathe kuni, Quqelani kwabaneshologu nakoosiyazi,  abalozayo, abadumzelayo, yithini, Abantu mabangaquqeli kuThixo wabo, yini na? Ngenxa yabaphilileyo mabaquqele kwabafileyo na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:20">8:20</a> Bhekani esiyalweni, esingqinweni! Ukuba bathe abathetha ngokwelo lizwi, boba abanasifingo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:21">8:21</a> Baya kucanda kulo ilizwe begogotyelwe, belambile; kuthi ke,  xa bathe balamba, babe noburhalarhume, batshabhise ukumkani wabo noThixo wabo, babheke phezulu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:22">8:22</a> babheke emhlabeni, nanko kuyimbandezelo nobumnyama, bethiwe ncithi yingcutheko, begxothelwe esithokothokweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:1">9:1</a> Ngokuba akuyi kuhlala kuthe ncithi kwelinengcutheko.  Ngexesha lokuqala walicukuceza ilizwe lakwaZebhulon nelizwe lakwaNafetali; ngelakamva uya kuyizukisa indlela yaselwandle,  phesheya kweYordan, ummandla weentlanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:2">9:2</a> Abantu abo babamba emnyameni babone ukukhanya okukhulu;  abemi basezweni lethunzi lokufa, ukukhanya kubengezele phezu kwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:3">9:3</a> Uyalwandisa uhlanga, ulukhulisela uvuyo; bayavuya phambi kwakho, njengokuvuya kwexa lokuvuna, njengokuvuyelela kwabo ekwabeni kwabo amaxhoba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:4">9:4</a> Kuba idyokhwe yomthwalo wabo noswazi lwamagxa abo, intonga yomqhubi wabo, uyaphule njengemini yakwaMidiyan.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:5">9:5</a> Ngokuba zonke izihlangu zabanyathela ngezihlangu ekungxoleni kokulwa, neengubo ezityikitywe emagazini, ezo ziya kutshiswa,  zibe kukudla komlilo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:6">9:6</a> Ngokuba sizalelwe umntwana, sinikwe unyana; ukuthethela kusesixhantini sakhe; igama lakhe kuthiwa nguMmangaliso,  nguMcebisi, nguThixo oligorha, nguSonini-nanini, nguMthetheli woxolo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:7">9:7</a> ukuba kwande ukuthethela oko, kubekho uxolo olungenakuphela etroneni kaDavide, nasebukumkanini bakhe, ukuba bumiswe buxhaswe ngokusesikweni nangobulungisa, kususela koko kude kuse ephakadeni. Ikhwele likaYehova wemikhosi liya kukwenza oko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:8">9:8</a> INkosi ithumela ilizwi kwaYakobi, liwa ke kwaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:9">9:9</a> Bonke ke abantu bephela baya kwazi, amaEfrayim nabemi belakwaSamari: abathi ngekratshi nangobukhulu bentliziyo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:10">9:10</a> Izitena ziwile, siya kwakha ngamatye aqingqiweyo; imithombe ixakaxiwe, siya kuyimisela ngemisedare.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:11">9:11</a> UYehova ubaphakamisile ababandezeli bakaRetsin phezu kwakhe, uzixhoxhile iintshaba zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:12">9:12</a> Ama-Aram ngasempumalanga, namaFilisti ngasentshonalanga,  awadlile amaSirayeli ngomlomo wonke. Kuko konke oko, awubuyi umsindo wakhe; isandla sakhe sisolukile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:13">9:13</a> Aba bantu ke ababuyeli kulowo ubabethileyo; abamngxamele uYehova wemikhosi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:14">9:14</a> Ngoko ke usuke uYehova wanqumla kuSirayeli intloko nomsila,  isebe lomthi wesundu nomzi, ngamini-nye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:15">9:15</a> Amadoda amakhulu nabafo ababekekileyo, yintloko ke leyo;  abaprofeti abayala ngobuxoki, ngumsila ke lowo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:16">9:16</a> Abakhokeli baba bantu basuke baba ngaba bandwendwisayo,  nabakhokelwa ngabo basuke baba ngabaginyiweyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:17">9:17</a> Ngenxa yoko iNkosi ayiyi kuvuya ngamadodana abo, ingabi namfesane ngeenkedama zabo nabahlolokazi babo; ngokuba bonke bephela baziintshembenxa, nabenzi bobubi; yonke imilomo ithetha ngobudenge. Kuko konke oko, awubuyi umsindo wakhe; isandla sakhe sisolukile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:18">9:18</a> Kuba okungendawo kutsha njengomlilo, kudla ubobo namakhakakhaka, kufaka isikhuni ezintshinyeleni zehlathi,  kunyuka njengomqulu womsi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:19">9:19</a> Ngokuphuphuma komsindo kaYehova wemikhosi ilizwe liyatsha;  abantu banjengokudla komlilo; umntu akamcongi umzalwana wakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:20">9:20</a> Basika ngasekunene, balambe noko; badle ngasekhohlo,  bangahluthi noko; umntu adle inyama yengalo yakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:21">9:21</a> uManase adle uEfrayim, uEfrayim adle uManase; bona bachasane noYuda. Kuko konke oko, awubuyi umsindo wakhe;  sisolukile isandla sakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:1">10:1</a> Yeha, abamisi bemimiselo yobutshinga, ababhali ababhala uxhamlo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:2">10:2</a> ukuze bazisunduze izisweli, zingafiki ematyaleni,  bazihluthe ibango lazo iintsizana zabantu bam, ukuba abahlolokazi babe lixhoba labo, baphange iinkedama!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:3">10:3</a> Niya kuthini na ke ngemini yovelelo, nasesithongeni esivela kude? Niya kusabela kubani na ukuba anincede, nilushiye phi na uzuko lwenu?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:4">10:4</a> Akukho kumbi, sekukukuguqa phakathi kwabakhonkwixeyo, bawe phakathi kwababuleweyo. Kuko konke oko, awubuyi umsindo wakhe,  sisolukile isandla sakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:5">10:5</a> Yeha, uAsiriya, ntonga yomsindo wam: luswazi olusesandleni sabo ukubhavuma kwam!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:6">10:6</a> Ndiya kumthumela kuhlanga oluyintshembenxa, ndimwisele umthetho ngabantu bokuphuphuma komsindo wam, ukuba athimbe amaxhoba, aphange okuphangiweyo, abenze into yokunyathelwa njengodaka lwezitrato.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:7">10:7</a> Ke yena akabi kunjalo; intliziyo yakhe ayiyicingi loo nto;  ngokuba okusentliziyweni yakhe kukutshabalalisa nokunqumla iintlanga ezingembalwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:8">10:8</a> Kuba uthi, Abathetheli bam asingookumkani bonke na? IKaleno ayinjengeKarkemishe na,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:9">10:9</a> iHamati ayinjengeArpadi na, owakwaSamari awunjengeDamasko na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:10">10:10</a> Njengokuba isandla sam sazifumanayo izikumkani zezithixo ezingeni; ukanti imifanekiso yazo eqingqiweyo ingaphezulu kweyaseYerusalem neyakwaSamari:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:11">10:11</a> andiyi kuthi na, njengoko ndenza ngako kowakwaSamari nezithixo zawo ezingeni, ndenjenjalo kwiYerusalem nezithixo zayo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:12">10:12</a> Kuya kuthi, xa ithe iNkosi yazifeza izenzo zayo zonke entabeni yaseZiyon naseYerusalem, ndizivelele iziqhamo zobukhulu bentliziyo yokumkani waseAsiriya, nokuqhayisa ngokuqwayinga kwamehlo akhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:13">10:13</a> Kuba uthe, Ndenze ngamandla esandla sam nangobulumko bam;  ngokuba ndinengqondo, ndayishenxisa imida yezizwe, ndaziphanga iimpahla zazo, ndabahlisa njengenkunzi eyimbalasane abahleli ezitroneni;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:14">10:14</a> isandla sam sabufumana ubutyebi bezizwe njengendlu yentaka, ndalibutha mna lonke ihlabathi, njengokubutha amaqanda; akwabakho nanye ishukumisa iphiko, neyakhamayo,  netswinayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:15">10:15</a> Izembe lingamqhayisela na ogawula ngalo? isarha ingazikhulisa na ngaphezu koyitsalayo? ngathi intonga ingabajingisa abaphakamisi bayo, ngathi uswazi lungamphakamisa ongenguwo umthi!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:16">10:16</a> Ngako oko iNkosi, iNkosi yemikhosi, iya kubathumela ukungcumbeka kwabatyebileyo bakhe, nangaphantsi kobuqaqawuli baseAsiriya kutshe ukutsha, njengokutsha komlilo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:17">10:17</a> Ukhanyiso lukaSirayeli luya kuba ngumlilo, oyiNgcwele wakhe abe lilangatye, litshise lidle amakhakakhaka akhe nobobo lwakhe ngamini-nye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:18">10:18</a> Uya kubuphelisa ubuqaqawuli behlathi lakhe, nobentsimi yakhe echumayo, ethabathela emphefumlweni ase enyameni, kube njengokungcungcutheka komntu ofayo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:19">10:19</a> abe mbalwa amasalela emithi yehlathi lakhe, ibhalwe nangumntwana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:20">10:20</a> Kuya kuthi ngaloo mini, angabi saphinda amasalela akwaSirayeli, nabasindileyo bendlu kaYakobi, bayame ngobabethayo; baya kwayama ngoYehova oyiNgcwele kaSirayeli,  benyanisile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:21">10:21</a> Amasalela aya kubuya, amasalela akwaYakobi, eze kuThixo oligorha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:22">10:22</a> Kuba nangona bathe baba ngangentlabathi yaselwandle abantu bakho, Sirayeli, kobuya amasalela odwa kubo; ukupheliswa kumisiwe kwagqitywa, kukhukula ubulungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:23">10:23</a> Ngokuba iNkosi uYehova wemikhosi iza kwenza phakathi kwehlabathi lonke impeliso, iyemisiweyo ke yagqitywa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:24">10:24</a> Ngako oko, itsho iNkosi, uYehova wemikhosi, ukuthi, Musani ukumoyika uAsiriya, bantu bam bahleliyo eZiyon, akunibetha ngentonga, aniphakamisele uswazi lwakhe ngohlobo lwamaYiputa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:25">10:25</a> Kuba kusaya kuba mzuzwana mncinane, kuphele ukubhavuma kwam, nomsindo wam uye kumonakalisa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:26">10:26</a> ajiwule phezu kwakhe uYehova wemikhosi iziniya, njengoko wabetha amaMidiyan eweni likaOrebhe; intonga yakhe ibe phezu kolwandle, ayiphakamise ngohlobo lwamaYiputa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:27">10:27</a> Kuya kuthi ngaloo mini, usuke umthwalo wakhe esixhantini sakho, nedyokhwe yakhe entanyeni yakho, idyokhwe yonakale kukutyeba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:28">10:28</a> Ufikile eAyati, ucande eMigron, uyibeke eMikimashe impahla yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:29">10:29</a> Baqabele enkalweni, bathi, Masilalise eGebha. Iyagubha iRama, isabile iGibheha yakwaSawule.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:30">10:30</a> Khala ngezwi lakho, ntombi yaseGalim! Baza iindlebe,  Layisha! Uha, Anatoti!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:31">10:31</a> IMadema ibalekile; abemi baseGebhim bazisabisile iintsapho zabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:32">10:32</a> Umisa eNobhi kwanamhlanje, ulingisa ngesandla sakhe entabeni yentombi enguZiyon, endulini yaseYerusalem.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:33">10:33</a> Yabona, iNkosi, uYehova wemikhosi, iyawathi tyhobotyhobo amahlamvu ngokungcangcazelisayo, namade aphezulu axakaxwe,  naphakamileyo athotywe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:34">10:34</a> ihlahla neentshinyela zehlathi ngesixengxe, iwiswe iLebhanon ngonamandla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:1">11:1</a> Kophuma igatya esiphunzini sikaYese, kuqhame ihlumelo ezingcanjini zakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:2">11:2</a> ahle ahlale phezu kwalo uMoya kaYehova, umoya wobulumko nowengqondo, umoya wecebo nowobugorha, umoya wokwazi nowokoyika uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:3">11:3</a> Ivumba elithozamisayo kuye likukoyika uYehova, angagwebi ngokokubona kwamehlo akhe, angohlwayi ngokokuva kweendlebe zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:4">11:4</a> Uya kuligweba ityala lezisweli ngobulungisa, abalungiselele abalulamileyo behlabathi ngokuthe tye, alibethe ihlabathi ngentonga yomlomo wakhe, ambulale ongendawo ngomoya wemilebe yomlomo wakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:5">11:5</a> Yoba bubulungisa iqamesi lesinqe sakhe, ibe yintembeko iqamesi lamanqe akhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:6">11:6</a> Ingcuka iya kuhlala nemvana, ingwe ibuthe netakane lebhokhwe; kubuthe ndawonye ithole lenkomo, nengonyama entsha,  nenkomo etyetyisiweyo; nomntwana aziqhube ezo zinto.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:7">11:7</a> Ithokazi lenkomo nemazi yebhere ziya kudla utyani ndawonye,  amankonyana azo abuthe ndaweni-nye; ingonyama idle umququ njengenkomo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:8">11:8</a> adlale umntwana owanyayo emngxunyeni wephimpi, olunyulweyo ase isandla sakhe elukhozweni lweliso lerhamba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:9">11:9</a> Ezo zinto aziyi kwenza bubi, aziyi konakalisa ezintabeni zam zonke ezingcwele; ngokuba ilizwe liya kuzala kukwazi uYehova, njengamanzi egubungele ulwandle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:10">11:10</a> Kuya kuthi ngaloo mini, ihlumelo likaYese, elimele ukuba yibhanile yezizwe, iintlanga ziquqele kulo; nendafo yokuphumla kwalo ibe bubuqaqawuli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:11">11:11</a> Kuya kuthi ngaloo mini, iNkosi isiphindise okwesibini isandla sayo sokuwathenga siwakhulule amasalela abantu bayo,  aya kusala eAsiriya, naseYiputa, nasePatros, nakwaKushi,  nakwaElam, naseShinare, naseHamati, naseziqithini zolwandle:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:12">11:12</a> izinyusele ibhanile iintlanga, ibahlanganise abagxothiweyo bakwaSirayeli, izibuthe iintsali zakwaYuda emasondweni omane ehlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:13">11:13</a> Losuka ikhwele likaEfrayim, banqunyulwe ababandezeli bakaYuda. UEfrayim akayi kumkhweletela uYuda, uYuda angambandezeli uEfrayim.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:14">11:14</a> Bophaphazela egxalabeni lamaFilisti, babheke ngasentshonalanga. Baya kudibana baphange oonyana basempumalanga, base isandla kooEdom noMowabhi; oonyana baka-Amon babeve.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:15">11:15</a> UYehova wosisingela phantsi isibhaxa solwandle lwaseYiputa, alingise ngesandla sakhe kuwo uMlambo ekuvutheni komoya wakhe, awubethe ube yimilanjana esixhenxe, abaweze beneembadada.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:16">11:16</a> Kuya kubakho umendo wamasalela abantu bakhe, abaya kusala eAsiriya, njengoko kwaba njalo kumaSirayeli, mini anyuka ephuma ezweni leYiputa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:1">12:1</a> Uya kuthi wena ngaloo mini, Ndiyabulela kuwe, Yehova,  ngokokuba ubundiqumbele, waza wabuya umsindo wakho,  wandithuthuzela wena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:2">12:2</a> Yabona, uThixo ukukusindiswa kwam; ndikholosile,  andikwantyi; ngokokuba iqhayiya lam nengoma yam nguYa,  nguYehova obuye waba lusindiso kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:3">12:3</a> Ngoko ke niya kukha amanzi ninemihlali emithonjeni yosindiso;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:4">12:4</a> nithi ngaloo mini, Bulelani kuYehova, nqulani igama lakhe,  zaziseni ezizweni izenzo zakhe, izenzo zakhe ezincamisayo;  likhankanyeni igama lakhe ukuba liyingxonde.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:5">12:5</a> Mbetheleni uhadi uYehova; ngokuba enze ngobungangamsha;  makwazeke oko ehlabathini lonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:6">12:6</a> Tsholoza umemelele, wena mmi waseZiyon; ngokuba mkhulu phakathi kwakho oyiNgcwele kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:1">13:1</a> Isihlabo esisingisele kwiBhabheli, awasibonayo uIsaya,  unyana ka-Amotsi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:2">13:2</a> Nyusani ibhanile phezu kwentaba eluqayi, baphakamiseleni ilizwi; khobani ngesandla, bangene emasangweni amanene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:3">13:3</a> Mna ndibawisele umthetho abangcwalisiweyo bam, ndiwabizele umsindo wam amagorha am, abadlamkileyo bam abanekratshi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:4">13:4</a> Yiveni ingxokolo ezintabeni, ngathi yeyabantu abaninzi.  Yiveni ingxokolo yezikumkani zeentlanga, zihlanganisene;  uYehova wemikhosi uhlanganisa umkhosi wemfazwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:5">13:5</a> Bavela ezweni elikude, ekupheleni kwamazulu-nguYehova nezixhobo zengqumbo yakhe, ukuba alonakalise ilizwe lonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:6">13:6</a> Bhombolozani, kuba isondele imini kaYehova, ivela ngokwembuqo kuSomandla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:7">13:7</a> Ngenxa yoko ziwile iingalo zonke, zonke iintliziyo zabantu zinyibilikile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:8">13:8</a> Bakhwankqile, bafikelwe kukupenapena nayinimba;  bayazibhijabhija njengozalayo, bakhwankqiswe ulowo nguwabo;  ubuso babo bubuso bamalangatye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:9">13:9</a> Yabona, imini kaYehova iyeza, inobujorha, iphuphuma umsindo, ishushu, ukuba ilenze libe senkangala ilizwe,  ibatshabalalise aboni balo kulo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:10">13:10</a> Kuba iinkwenkwezi zezulu namakroza alo akayi kukhanyisa kukhanya kwawo; liya kuba mnyama ilanga ekuphumeni kwalo,  inyanga ingabi mhlophe ukukhanya kwayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:11">13:11</a> Ndolivelela elimiweyo ngenxa yobubi balo, nabangendawo ngenxa yobugwenxa babo, ndiliphelise ikratshi labakhukhumeleyo,  ndilithobele phantsi ikratshi labangcangcazelisi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:12">13:12</a> ndiwenze amadoda anqabe ngaphezu kwegolide engcwengiweyo,  noluntu lunqabe ngaphezu kwegolide ecikizekileyo yakwaOfire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:13">13:13</a> Ngenxa yoko ndiya kuligungqisa izulu, nehlabathi linyikime, lishenxe endaweni yalo ngokuphuphuma komsindo kaYehova wemikhosi, ngemini yokuvutha komsindo wakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:14">13:14</a> bathi ke, njengebhadikazi elisukeliswayo, nanjengomhlambi ongenamhlanganisi, babheke elowo kubantu bakowabo, basabele elowo ezweni lakowabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:15">13:15</a> Bonke abo bafunyenweyo baya kuhlatywa amahlanza, bonke abo babanjiweyo bawe likrele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:16">13:16</a> Zocunyuzwa iintsana zabo phambi kwamehlo abo, ziphangwe izindlu zabo, balalwe abafazi babo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:17">13:17</a> Yabona, ndibaxhoxhela amaMedi angayibekiyo isilivere,  angayinanzileyo negolide.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:18">13:18</a> Izaphetha zawo ziya kukhahlela amadodana, nesiqhamo sesizalo angabi namfesane siso; iliso lawo lingabi nanceba kubo abantwana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:19">13:19</a> IBhabheli, ikhazikhazi lezikumkani, isihombo sekratshi lamaKaledi, iya kuba njengokubhukuqa kukaThixo iSodom neGomora.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:20">13:20</a> Ayi kumiwa naphakade, ayi kuza ihlalwe ezizukulwaneni ngezizukulwana, angagxumeki ntente khona nomArabhi, nabalusi bangakhi khona buhlanti.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:21">13:21</a> Obutha khona amarhamncwa omqwebedu, zizale izindlu zabo zizihuluhulu, kuhlale iinciniba khona, kuqakathe izinto ezimaxhonti khona;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:22">13:22</a> kulile amaxhwili ezingxandeni zabo ezinde, neempungutye emabhotweni okuxhamla ubuncwane; kusondele ukuza kwexesha layo,  nemini yayo ingalibali.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:1">14:1</a> Ngokuba uYehova uya kuba nemfesane kuYakobi, abuye awanyule amaSirayeli, awahlalise emhlabeni wakowawo, bathelele kuwo abasemzini, bahlomele endlwini kaYakobi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:2">14:2</a> Ziya kuwathabatha izizwe, ziwazise endaweni yawo: bazifuye zona abendlu kaSirayeli emhlabeni kaYehova, zibe ngamakhoboka namakhobokazana, babe ngabathimbi babathimbi babo, babe nobukhosi kubaqhubi babo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:3">14:3</a> Kuya kuthi, mini uYehova aniphumzayo ekwaphukeni kwenu,  nasekugungqeni kwenu, nasekukhonzeni okunzima, enakhonziswa ngako,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:4">14:4</a> nihlabe lo mzekeliso ngokumkani waseBhabheli, nithi, Utheni na ukupheza umqhubi! ukupheza umzi othisayo!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:5">14:5</a> UYehova ulwaphule uswazi lwabangendawo, intonga yabalawuli,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:6">14:6</a> ebizibetha izizwe ngokuphuphuma komsindo, ngokubetha okungenakupheza; ebizinyathela ngomsindo iintlanga ngokusukelwa okungenakubanjezelwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:7">14:7</a> Liphumle, lizolile ihlabathi lonke; bayagqabhuka bamemelele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:8">14:8</a> Nayo imisipres ikuvuyele, imisedare yaseLebhanon ithi,  Kuseloko walalayo, akunyuki mgawuli usigawulayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:9">14:9</a> Elabafileyo ngaphantsi liyagungqa nguwe, ngokubona ukuza kwakho; likuxhoxhela abafileyo, zonke iinkunzi ezikhokelayo zehlabathi; liphakamisa ezitroneni zabo bonke ookumkani beentlanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:10">14:10</a> Zonke ziphela zasusela ngelithi kuwe, Nawe wenziwe ofayo njengathi na? usuke wafana nathi na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:11">14:11</a> Buhliselwe kwelabafileyo ubungangamsha bakho, isandi semirhubhe yakho; kwandlelwe iimpethu ngaphantsi kwakho,  akugubungele amanundu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:12">14:12</a> Utheni na ukuwa emazulwini, Khwezi, nyana wesifingo!  ukunqunyulwa uwe emhlabeni, mngquli weentlanga!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:13">14:13</a> Wena ke wathi entliziyweni yakho, Ndiyakunyukela emazulwini, ndiyinyuse itrone yam ibe ngaphezu kweenkwenkwezi zikaThixo; ndihlale entabeni yentlanganiso, engontsini yasentla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:14">14:14</a> Ndiya kunyuka ngaphezu kweziganga zamafu, ndizifanise nOsenyangweni;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:15">14:15</a> kanti uya kuhliselwa kwelabafileyo, engontsini yomhadi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:16">14:16</a> Abakubonayo baya kukuthi nzo ngamehlo, bakugqale, bathi,  Yiyo na le indoda ebiligungqisa ihlabathi, ebizinyikimisa izikumkani?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:17">14:17</a> eyalenza intlango elimiweyo, yayigungxula imizi yalo;  ayabavulela ababanjwa balo ukuba bagoduke?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:18">14:18</a> Bonke ookumkani beentlanga, bonke bephela, balele benozuko, elowo endlwini yakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:19">14:19</a> ke wena ulahlelwe kude nengcwaba lakho, njengegatya elilisikizi; wambethe ababuleweyo, abahlatywe ngekrele, abahle baya ematyeni omhadi; njengesidumbu esinyashwe ngeenyawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:20">14:20</a> Akuyi kubandakanywa nabo engcwabeni, ngokokuba walonakalisayo ilizwe lakho, wababulala abantu bakho; ayiyi kuba nagama naphakade imbewu yabenzi bobubi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:21">14:21</a> Oonyana bakhe balungiseleni ukusikwa, ngenxa yobugwenxa booyise, Mabangesuki balidle ilifa ihlabathi, bazalise elimiweyo ngemizi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:22">14:22</a> Ndiya kusukela phezulu kubo, utsho uYehova wemikhosi,  iBhabheli ndiyinqumle ingabi nagama namasalela, nanyana nanzalo, utsho uYehova;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:23">14:23</a> ndiyenze ibe lilifa lokhwalimanzi nezadunge zamanzi,  ndiyitshayele ngomtshayelo wentshabalalo; utsho uYehova wemikhosi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:24">14:24</a> Ufungile uYehova wemikhosi wathi, Inyaniso, njengoko ndicinge ngako, koba njalo; njengoko ndicebe ngako, koma ngolo hlobo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:25">14:25</a> ukuba ndimaphule uAsiriya ezweni lam, ndimnyashe ngeenyawo ezintabeni zam, isuke kubo idyokhwe yakhe, usuke umthwalo wakhe esixhantini sabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:26">14:26</a> Lilo elo icebo elicetyiweyo ngehlabathi lonke; siso eso isandla esolukileyo phezu kweentlanga zonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:27">14:27</a> Kuba uYehova wemikhosi ucebile, ngubani na onokutshitshisa? nesandla sakhe eso solukile, ngubani na onokusibuyisa?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:28">14:28</a> Ngomnyaka wokufa kokumkani onguAhazi kwabakho esi sihlabo sithi:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:29">14:29</a> Musa ukuvuyelela, wena Filisti uphela, ngakuba yaphukile intonga ebikubetha; kuba engcanjini yenyoka kuphuma irhamba,  isiqhamo sayo sibe yinyoka etshisayo, ephaphazelayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:30">14:30</a> Baya kudla abazizisweli, abuthe ekholosile amahlwempu;  ndibulale ingcambu yakho ngendlala, abulawe amasalela akho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:31">14:31</a> Bhomboloza, sango! Khala, mzi! Yitha amandla, wena Filisti uphela, ngokuba entla kuphuma umsi; akukho wahlukayo ebuthweni lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:32">14:32</a> Bathini na ukuphendula abathunywa beentlanga? Bathi,  UYehova uyisekile iZiyon, zozimela ngayo iintsizana zabantu bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:1">15:1</a> Isihlabo esisingisele kuMowabhi. Kuba ngobusuku iAri yakwaMowabhi ibhuqiwe, yadaka; kuba ngobusuku ibhuqiwe iKire yakwaMowabhi, yathi shwaka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:2">15:2</a> Banyuke baya endlwini naseDibhon, ezigangeni, besiya kulila; phezu kweNebho naphezu kweMedebha uMowabhi uyabhomboloza; zonke iintloko zichetyiwe, zonke iindevu ziguyiwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:3">15:3</a> Ezitratweni zakhe babhinqa ezirhwexayo; phezu kwezindlu zakhona, nasezindaweni zeembutho zakhona, bonke bephela bayabhomboloza, besithi ngxa iinyembezi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:4">15:4</a> Iyakhala iHeshbhon ne-Elale, lide laya kuvakala naseYahazi izwi labo; ngenxa yoko abaxhobileyo bakwaMowabhi benza isijwili, umphefumlo wabo uyajijitheka kubo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:5">15:5</a> Intliziyo yam iyakhala ngokubona uMowabhi, omivalo ide yesa eTsohare, elithokazi elilizibulokazi; kuba banyuka eqhineni laseLuhiti belila; kuba endleleni yaseHoronayim bakhaliswa kukwaphulwa kwabo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:6">15:6</a> kuba amanzi aseNimrim athe qoko; kuba bubunile utyani,  luphelile uhlaza, awukho umfuno.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:7">15:7</a> Ngenxa yoko intwana ebisele, ababeyenzile, ababeyiqwebile,  bayayithwala bayiweze esihlanjeni semingculuba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:8">15:8</a> Kuba isikhalo siwuzungulezile umda wakwaMowabhi;  ukubhomboloza kwakhe kwesa e-Eglayim, kwesa naseBhere-elim ukubhomboloza kwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:9">15:9</a> Kuba amanzi aseDimon azele ligazi; ngokuba iDimon ndiyimisela ezinye izinto ezimbi; abasindileyo bakwaMowabhi nabaseleyo emhlabeni ndibamisela ingonyama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:1">16:1</a> Thumelani iimvana kumlawuli welizwe, zivela eSela, zibheke entlango, ziye entabeni yentombi uZiyon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:2">16:2</a> Kuba njengeentaka eziphekuziweyo, njengendlu yentaka esuselweyo, aya kuba njalo amagxamesi akwaMowabhi emazibukweni aseArnon, esithi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:3">16:3</a> Siphe iqhinga, yahlula; misa isithunzi sakho sibe njengobusuku emini enkulu; fihla abagxothiweyo, musa ukumncetheza obhadubhadulayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:4">16:4</a> Mabaphambukele kuwe abagxothiweyo bam; ube lisithe kuye uMowabhi phambi kombhuqi; ngokuba umkhamangi ugqibele, umbhuqi uphelile, abanyashi batshatyalalisiwe ezweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:5">16:5</a> Kuya kuzinziswa itrone ngenceba, kuhlale phezu kwayo onenyaniso, ententeni kaDavide: umgwebi okhathalele okusesikweni, okhawulezayo ukulungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:6">16:6</a> Silivile ikratshi likaMowabhi, ikratshi elikhulu. Hayi,  ukukratsha kwakhe! Hayi, ikratshi lakhe nokuphuphuma komsindo wakhe, ukuphololoza kwakhe into engeyiyo!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:7">16:7</a> Ngako oko uMowabhi uya kubhomboloza ngenxa kaMowabhi; bonke bephela baya kubhomboloza; niya kunkwinizela izicumba zeerasintyisi zaseKir-hareshete, nithe dakumba kanye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:8">16:8</a> Kuba amasimi aseHeshbhon antshwenyile, nomdiliya waseSibhema. Abantu beentlanga bayivithile imidiliya yawo yohlobo; ibide yaya kufika eYazere, yanabela entlango, amasebe ayo anaba ada awela ulwandle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:9">16:9</a> Ngenxa yoko ndiyawulilela ngokulila kweYazere umdiliya waseSibhema; ndikunyakamisa ngeenyembezi zam, Heshbhon, nawe Elale, ngokuba ukuvunwa kweziqhamo zakho nokuvunwa kweediliya zakho kufikelwe ngamayeyeye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:10">16:10</a> Isukile imivuyo nemigcobo entsimini echumayo;  akusamemelelwa ezidiliyeni, akusadunywa nokudunywa; umxovuli akasaxovuli newayini emkhombeni; ndiwaphelisile amayeyeye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:11">16:11</a> Ngenxa yoko izibilini zam ziyahlokoma njengohadi ngoMowabhi, nento ephakathi kwam ngeKir-beres.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:12">16:12</a> Kuya kuthi, xa athe wabonakala, xa athe wazidinisa uMowabhi esigangeni, wangena engcweleni yakhe ukuba athandaze,  asuke angabi nakuthini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:13">16:13</a> Lilo elo ilizwi, awalithethayo uYehova ngoMowabhi kwanini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:14">16:14</a> Kaloku ke uYehova uthetha esithi, Ngeminyaka emithathu,  njengeminyaka yomqeshwa, buya kucukucezwa ubuqaqawuli bukaMowabhi, naloo ngxokolo yonke eninzi, amasalela abe mancinane, abe mbalwa, angabi makhulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:1">17:1</a> Isihlabo esisingisele kwiDamasko. Yabona, iDamasko iya kususwa ekubeni ngumzi, ibe ngumwewe owileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:2">17:2</a> Ishiyiwe imizi yaseArohere; iya kuba yeyemihlambi, ibuthe khona, kungabikho uyothusayo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:3">17:3</a> ipheliswe inqaba kwaEfrayim nobukumkani kwiDamasko,  amasalela ama-Aram abe njengobuqaqawuli boonyana bakaSirayeli;  utsho uYehova wemikhosi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:4">17:4</a> Kuya kuthi ngaloo mini, busweleke ubuqaqawuli bukaYakobi,  ingcumbeke inyama yakhe etyebileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:5">17:5</a> Kuya kuba njengomvuni ehlanganisa ingqolowa emiyo, ingalo yakhe isika izikhwebu, kube njengokubhikica izikhwebu esihlanjeni samaRafa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:6">17:6</a> kusale okubhikicwayo khona, njengasekuvuthululweni komnquma; amabhumbulu abe mabini namathathu emancamini phezulu,  abe mane namahlanu ezimbaxeni zawo umthi oneziqhamo; utsho uYehova, uThixo kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:7">17:7</a> Ngaloo mini umntu uya kondela kuMenzi wakhe, amehlo akhe akhangele koyiNgcwele kaSirayeli;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:8">17:8</a> anganoneleli izibingelelo, izenzo zezandla zakhe,  angayikhangeli into eyenziwa yiminwe yakhe, noAshera, nezithixo zelanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:9">17:9</a> Ngaloo mini imizi yakhe enqabileyo iya kuba ngamanxuwa asezintshinyeleni zehlathi, nawasezincotsheni zeentaba,  abawashiyayo phambi koonyana bakaSirayeli; koba senkangala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:10">17:10</a> Ngokokuba umlibele uThixo, umsindisi wakho, akwalikhumbula neliwa lokunqaba kwakho; ngenxa yoko watyala izityalo ezimnandi, wamilisela kuzo iintswazi zomdiliya wasemzini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:11">17:11</a> Ngemini yokutyala kwakho wawubiyela, kusasa wayityatyambisa imbewu yakhosisitha sokwindla eso ngemini yesifo, nomvandedwa obulalayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:12">17:12</a> Yeha, ukuguguma kwezizwe ezininzi, ziguguma njengokuguguma kweelwandle! Yeha, ukungxola kwezizwe, zingxola njengokungxola kwamanzi anamandla!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:13">17:13</a> Izizwe zingxola njengokungxola kwamanzi amaninzi; ke uThixo wozikhalimela, zisabe ziye kude, zisukelwe njengomququ weentaba phambi komoya, njengefukufuku lothuli phambi kwesaqhwithi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:14">17:14</a> Ngexa langokuhlwa, nanko zikhwankqile; kungekasi, azikho.  Siso eso isahlulo sabasidywidayo, nelifa labasiphangayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:1">18:1</a> Yeha ke, ilizwe lenzwinini yamaphiko, eliphesheya kwemilambo yakwaKushi:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:2">18:2</a> elithuma izigidimi ngolwandle ngemikhombe yemikhanzi phezu kwamanzi! Ndithi, Hambani, bathunywa banamendu, niye kuhlanga olude, olugudileyo, kubantu aboyikekayo ngapha nangapha,  kuhlanga olumithetho inzima, olugqushayo, olulizwe licandwacandwe yimilambo!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:3">18:3</a> Nonke bemi belimiweyo, nani bahleli ehlabathini, xa kuthe kwenyuka ibhanile ezintabeni, khangelani; xa kuthe kwavuthelwa isigodlo, yivani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:4">18:4</a> Ngokuba utshilo uYehova kum ukuthi, Ndiya kuzola, ndibonele ndisendaweni yam; kufudumele, lisile, likho ilanga, kukho ilifu lombethe ekufudumaleni ngexa lokuvuna.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:5">18:5</a> Kuba phambi kokuvuna, akugqibela ukuphuma amathupha,  intyantyambo yakuba yidiliya emuncu: uya kuwanqumla amasebe ngesitshetshe, awasuse awavikive anabayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:6">18:6</a> Onke aya kushiywa abe ngawamaxhalanga eentaba, abe ngawamarhamncwa elizwe; amaxhalanga adlulise ihlobo phezu kwawo, onke amarhamncwa elizwe adlulise ubusika phezu kwawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:7">18:7</a> Ngelo xesha kuya kusiwa kuYehova wemikhosi isithabathaba,  esingabantu abade, abagudileyo, bephuma kubantu aboyikekayo abangapha nangapha; kuhlanga olumithetho inzima, olugqushayo,  olulizwe licandwacandwe yimilambo; sisiwe endaweni yegama likaYehova wemikhosi, entabeni yaseZiyon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:1">19:1</a> Isihlabo esisingisele kwiYiputa. Bona ke uYehova ekhwele efini elinamendu, uza eYiputa. Ziya kudidizela izithixo ezingento zaseYiputa phambi kwakhe, intliziyo yeYiputa inyibilika phakathi kwayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:2">19:2</a> AmaYiputa ndiya kuwaxhokonxela kwa-amaYiputa, alwe elowo nomzalwana wakhe, elowo nommelwane wakhe, umzi nomzi,  ubukumkani nobukumkani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:3">19:3</a> Wothiwa qongqololo umoya wamaYiputa phakathi kwawo;  ndiliginye icebo lawo, aquqele kwizithixo ezingento,  nakwabadumze layo, nakwabaneshologu, nakoosiyazi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:4">19:4</a> ndiwavingcele amaYiputa ngesandla senkosi esilukhuni,  alawulwe ngukumkani onengcwangu; itsho iNkosi, uYehova wemikhosi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:5">19:5</a> Aya kuthi qoko amanzi aselwandle, utshe wome umlambo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:6">19:6</a> zinuke izibhaxa zawo, iwuthe itshe imijelo yoMnayile waseYiputa, zishwabane iingcongolo nemikhanzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:7">19:7</a> Iintili ezingakuMnayile, ngasechwebeni loMnayile, nento yonke ehlwayelweyo, iya koma, iphetshethwe ingabikho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:8">19:8</a> Baya kuncwina ababambisi beentlanzi, bambambazele bonke abaphosa iqherhu eMnayileni, bathi matshamatsha abaneka umnatha phezu kwamanzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:9">19:9</a> Baya kudana abasebenzi beflakisi echazwayo, nabaluki belinen emhlophe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:10">19:10</a> zithiwe vithivithi iintsika zalo, ube buhlungu umphefumlo wabo bonke abasebenzela umvuzo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:11">19:11</a> Bazizimathane zodwa abathetheli baseTsohan; amaphakathi alumkileyo kaFaro, icebo labo libubutyhakala. Ningathini na ukuthi kuFaro, Ndingunyana wezilumko, ndingunyana wookumkani bamandulo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:12">19:12</a> Ziphi na, ziphi na ke izilumko zakho? Mazikuxelele kaloku,  ziyazi into ayicebileyo uYehova wemikhosi ngeYiputa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:13">19:13</a> Bazizimathane abathetheli baseTsohan, balukuhliwe abathetheli baseNofu; bayilahlekisile iYiputa abayimbombo yezizwe zayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:14">19:14</a> UYehova uthululele embilinini wayo umoya wobugwenxa, ukuba bayilahlekise iYiputa ekwenzeni kwayo konke, njengokugxadazela kwenxila emhlanzweni walo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:15">19:15</a> IYiputa ayiyi kuba nasenzo isenzayo intloko kwanomsila,  isebe lesundu nomzi womlambo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:16">19:16</a> Ngaloo mini amaYiputa aya kuba njengabafazi, agubhe,  ankwantye phambi kokulingisa ngesandla kukaYehova wemikhosi,  alingisa ngaso kuwo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:17">19:17</a> Umhlaba wakwaYuda woyixhalabisa iYiputa; athi othe wawukhankanya kuyo, ankwantye, ngenxa yecebo likaYehova wemikhosi, alicebileyo ngayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:18">19:18</a> Ngaloo mini imizi emihlanu ezweni lamaYiputa iya kuthetha intetho yelakwaKanan, ifunge uYehova wemikhosi; omnye kuya kuthiwa yi-Ir-heres.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:19">19:19</a> Ngaloo mini kuya kubakho isibingelelo kuYehova phakathi kwelizwe lamaYiputa, nelitye elimisiweyo kuYehova ngasemdeni walo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:20">19:20</a> Oko koba ngumqondiso nobungqina kuYehova wemikhosi ezweni lamaYiputa; xa athe akhala kuYehova ngenxa yabaxinezeli bawo,  wowathumela umsindisi nomthetheleli, awahlangule.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:21">19:21</a> UYehova uya kuzazisa kumaYiputa, amazi uYehova amaYiputa ngaloo mini, amkhonze ngemibingelelo nangeminikelo yokudla;  abhambathise ngezibhambathiso kuYehova, azizalise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:22">19:22</a> UYehova uya kuwabetha ke amaYiputa, ebetha ephilisa;  abuyele kuYehova, yena athandazeke ngawo, awaphilise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:23">19:23</a> Ngaloo mini kuya kubakho umendo ophuma eYiputa, oya eAsiriya; eze ama-Asiriya eYiputa, amaYiputa aye eAsiriya,  akhonze uYehova amaYiputa kunye nama-Asiriya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:24">19:24</a> Ngaloo mini amaSirayeli aya kuba sisahlulo sesithathu kumaYiputa nakuma-Asiriya, eyintsikelelo phakathi kwehlabathi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:25">19:25</a> ewasikelela uYehova wemikhosi, esithi, Nisikelelwe,  maYiputa, bantu bam; ma-Asiriya, msebenzi wezandla zam;  maSirayeli, lifa lam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:1">20:1</a> Ngomnyaka wokuza kukaTartan eAshdode, ethunywe nguSargon,  ukumkani waseAsiriya (walwa neAshdode, wayithimba), ngelo xesha,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:2">20:2</a> wathetha uYehova ngoIsaya unyana ka-Amotsi, esithi, Yiya ukhulule ingubo erhwexayo emanqeni akho, uzikhulule iimbadada ezinyaweni zakho. Wenjenjalo ke, wahamba ze, engenazo neembadada.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:3">20:3</a> Wathi ke uYehova, Njengokuba umkhonzi wam uIsaya ehambe ze,  engenambadada, iminyaka emithathu, waba ngumqondiso nesimanga kwiYiputa nakwaKushi:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:4">20:4</a> uya kwenjenjalo ukumkani waseAsiriya ukubaqhuba abathinjiweyo baseYiputa, nabafudusiweyo bakwaKushi, abantwana namadoda amakhulu, beze, bengenambadada, behamba ngeempundu,  intoleyo eziintloni kwiYiputa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:5">20:5</a> Baya kuqhiphuka umbilini badane nguKushi, inqolonci yabo,  nayiYiputa, iqhayiya labo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:6">20:6</a> bathi ke abemi bolo nxweme ngaloo mini, Yabonani, inje inqolonci yethu, esasabela kuyo ukuba sincedwe, sihlangulwe kukumkani waseAsiriya; singathini na ke ukusinda thina?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:1">21:1</a> Isihlabo esisingisele kwintlango yaselwandle.  Njengezaqhwithi zasezantsi zikhukula, kuphuma into entlango,  ezweni eloyikekayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:2">21:2</a> Ndiboniswe umbono olukhuni: inginingini linginiza, umbhuqi ebhuqa. Nyuka, Elam; ngqinga, Madayi; ukuncwina kwabo konke ndiya kuphelisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:3">21:3</a> Ngenxa yoko azele amanqe am kukuzibhijabhija, inimba indifikele njengenimba yozalayo; ndiyapenapena, andiva;  ndikhwankqile, andiboni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:4">21:4</a> Intliziyo yam iyadinga, ukududuzela kundidandathekisile;  ungcwalazi, into endiyilangazelelayo, ulwenze into endigubhisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:5">21:5</a> Kulungiswa isithebe, kuboniselwa umboniselo, kuyadliwa,  kuyaselwavukani, bathetheli, thambisani iingweletshetshe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:6">21:6</a> Ngokuba itsho kum iNkosi, ukuthi, Yiya umise umboniseli,  athi akubona into aze kuyixela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:7">21:7</a> Wabona umkhoko wabakhweli, abamahashe bengababini,  nabakhweli bamaesile, nabakhweli beenkamela; wabaza iindlebe,  wazibaza kakhulu kunene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:8">21:8</a> Wadanduluka ngelengonyama, esithi, Nkosi, kususela koko ndimi emboniselweni emini, ndizimisile esigxineni sam ubusuku ngobusuku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:9">21:9</a> Ke, yabona, kweza umkhoko wamadoda, abamahashe bengababini.  Wasusela wathi, Iwile, iwile iBhabheli; yonke imifanekiso eqingqiweyo yoothixo bayo uyaphulele emhlabeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:10">21:10</a> Wena, nto yam ibhuliweyo, ngqolowa yesanda sam,  endikuvileyo kuYehova wemikhosi, uThixo kaSirayeli, ndikuxelile kuni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:11">21:11</a> Isihlabo esisingisele kothe cwaka. Omemeza kum ekwelakwaSehire, uthi, Mlindi, kuxa liphi na ebusuku? mlindi,  kuxa liphi na ebusuku?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:12">21:12</a> Uthi umlindi, Kuyeza ukusa, kwanobusuku. Ukuba niyabuza,  buzani; buyani, yizani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:13">21:13</a> Isihlabo esisingisele kwelaseArabhi. KwelaseArabhi niya kulalisa emxawukeni, nina mikhoko yamaDedan.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:14">21:14</a> Baziseleni amanzi abanxaniweyo; nina, bemi bakwaTema,  nibakhawulele ngesonka abaphalaphalayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:15">21:15</a> Ngokuba baphalaphaliswa ngamakrele, amakrele athiwe kruthu, nasisaphetha esityhidiweyo, nayimfazwe enzima.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:16">21:16</a> Ngokuba iNkosi itshilo kum ukuthi, Kwakulo mnyaka,  njengeminyaka yomqeshwa, buya kuphela ubuqaqawuli bonke bakwaKedare;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:17">21:17</a> abe mbalwa amasalela enani lezaphetha zamagorha, oonyana bakaKedare; ngokuba uYehova uThixo kaSirayeli uthethile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:1">22:1</a> Isihlabo esisingisele kumfula wombono. Ukholose ngantoni na kaloku, le nto unyukileyo waya phezu kwezindlu wonke uphela?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:2">22:2</a> Wena uzeleyo kukungxola, wena mzi uxokozelayo, wena nqaba ivuyelelayo; ababuleweyo bakho ababulawanga likrele, abafanga yimfazwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:3">22:3</a> Bonke abaphathi bakho babaleka kunye, bakhonkxwe kungabangakho saphetha; bonke abafunyanwa kuwe bakhonkxwa kunye ekubalekeleni kwabo kude.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:4">22:4</a> Ngenxa yoko ndathi, Susani amehlo kum, ndikwenze kube krakra ukulila kwam; musani ukundizama ngokundithuthuzela ngenxa yokubhuqwa kwentombi yabantu bakowethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:5">22:5</a> Ngokuba ifikelwe ngumhla wokudungwadungwa, wokugqushwa,  wokuqungwaqungwa, okuvela kwiNkosi uYehova wemikhosi, emfuleni wombono; umhla wokuwiselwa phantsi iindonga, wokuzibika ezintabeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:6">22:6</a> AmaElam aqubule umphongolo, eneenqwelo zokulwa ezinamadoda na bamahashe; amaKiri ahlube iingweletshetshe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:7">22:7</a> Zathi ke iintili zakho ezintle zazala ziinqwelo zokulwa,  bathi abamahashe bamisa bemisile esangweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:8">22:8</a> Wasibhenqa isigqubuthelo sakwaYuda; waza wena ngaloo mini wabheka esikrweqeni sendlu yehlathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:9">22:9</a> Nazibona iintanda zomzi kaDavide ukuba ninzi, nahlanganisa amanzi echibi lasezantsi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:10">22:10</a> izindlu zaseYerusalem nazibala; nazidiliza izindlu, ukuze ninqabise udonga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:11">22:11</a> Nenza isigingqi samanzi echibi elidala phakathi kweendonga zombini, anakhangela kumenzi wale nto, anambeka owayibumbayo kwakudala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:12">22:12</a> INkosi, uYehova wemikhosi, ngaloo mini yabizela ekulileni,  nasekumbambazeleni, nasekuchebeni intloko, nasekubhinqeni iingubo ezirhwexayo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:13">22:13</a> kanti kusuke kwaba yimihlali nemivuyo, kusoselwa iinkomo,  kuxhelwa iigusha, kudliwa inyama, kuselwa iwayini; kudliwa,  kuselwa, kuba kusithiwa, Ngomso soba sesifile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:14">22:14</a> UYehova wemikhosi wazityhila ngokwakhe ezindlebeni zam,  wathi, Nento, ukuba nokha nicanyagushelwe obo bugwenxa, nide nife! itsho iNkosi, uYehova wemikhosi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:15">22:15</a> Yatsho iNkosi, uYehova wemikhosi, ukuthi, Hamba uye kwelaa gosa, kuShebhena umphathi wendlu, uthi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:16">22:16</a> Unantoni na apha, unabani na apha, ukuba nje uzixholele ingcwaba apha, njengoxhola ingcwaba lakhe phezulu, ezikrolela ikhaya engxondorheni?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:17">22:17</a> Yabona, uYehova uya kukudandalazisa ngokudandalazisa kwendoda, akuxhakamfule, akuqinise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:18">22:18</a> Uya kukuthandela akuthandele, ube yinto yokunqakulisa,  imbumbulu esinga ezweni elibanzi ngeenxa zombini. Uya kufela apho, zibe lapho iinqwelo zobuqaqawuli bakho, wena, hlazo lendlu yenkosi yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:19">22:19</a> Ndokuguzula usuke ebugoseni bakho, akugungxule ebumeni bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:20">22:20</a> Kuya kuthi ngaloo mini, ndibize umkhonzi wam, uEliyakim unyana kaHilekiya;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:21">22:21</a> ndimambathise iingubo zakho zangaphantsi, ndimbophe ngombhinqo wakho, ndimnikele esandleni ulawulo lwakho, abe nguyise wabemi baseYerusalem nowabendlu kaYuda.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:22">22:22</a> Ndiya kusibeka isitshixo sendlu kaDavide esixhantini sakhe, avule kungabikho uvalayo, avale kungabikho uvulayo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:23">22:23</a> ndimbethelele abe sisikhonkwane endaweni eqinileyo; abe yitrone yozuko kwindlu kayise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:24">22:24</a> Baya kubuxhoma kuye bonke ubunzima bendlu kayise, amagatya neempakatha, yonke impahla encinane, kuthabathele empahleni ezizidendeleko, kuse empahleni yonke eyimiphanda.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:25">22:25</a> Ngaloo mini, utsho uYehova wemikhosi, siya kususwa isikhonkwane, eso sibethelelwe endaweni eqinileyo, sixakaxwe,  siwe, unqanyulwe umthwalo ophezu kwaso; ngokuba uYehova ethethile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:1">23:1</a> Isihlabo esisingisele kwiTire. Bhombolozani, nina zinqanawa zaseTarshishe, ngokuba ibhuqiwe, akwabakho ndlu, akwabakho kungena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:2">23:2</a> Bakutyhilelwe ezweni lamaKiti. Yithini cwaka, bemi bonxweme; wena uzaliswe ngabarhwebi baseTsidon, abawela ulwandle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:3">23:3</a> Yayisemanzini amakhulu imbewu yaseSihore, ukuvuna koMnayile kwaba lungeniselo kuyo; yaba yindawo yokurhweba kweentlanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:4">23:4</a> Dana, Tsidon; kuba luthethile ulwandle, inqaba yolwandle,  lwathi, Andizibhijabhijanga, andizalanga, andikhulisanga mlisela, andondlanga mthinjana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:5">23:5</a> Lothi lwakuthi ukuthi ukufika olu daba eYiputa, basuke bazibhijabhije ngodaba olungeTire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:6">23:6</a> Welelani niye eTarshishe; bhombolozani, bemi bonxwene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:7">23:7</a> Kunje na kuwe, wena mvuyeleli, ukuvela kwakho kukho kwasemihleni yamandulo, iinyawo zakho zakusa kude, ukuba uye kuthi vu?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:8">23:8</a> Ngubani na lo ucebe le nto ngeTire, ngomzi othwesa ngezithsaba, obarhwebi bawo bangabathetheli, obathengeli bawo bangabazukileyo behlabathi?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:9">23:9</a> Icetywe nguYehova wemikhosi, ukuba angcolise ubungangamsha bamakhazikhazi onke, ukuba acukuceze bonke abazukileyo behlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:10">23:10</a> Canda kulo ilizwe lakowenu njengoMnayile, ntombi inguTarshishe; akusekho luqhwemesha lukuxinileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:11">23:11</a> Isandla sakhe usolulele phezu kolwandle, ugungqise izikumkani. UYehova uwise umthetho ngelakwaKanan wokutshabalalisa iinqaba zalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:12">23:12</a> Wathi, Akuyi kuba sabuya udlamke, nkazana idlwengulweyo,  ntombi inguTsidon. Suk ume, welela kumaKiti; nalapho akuyi kuba nakuphumla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:13">23:13</a> Yabona, ilizwe lamaKaledi, ngabantu ababengekho;  ama-Asiriya abamisela ukuba babe ngabomqwebedu; bamisa iimboniselo zabo, bezinqika iingxande zalo ezinde, bezenza umwewe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:14">23:14</a> Bhombolozani, zinqanawa zaseTarshishe, ngokuba ibhuqiwe inqaba yenu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:15">23:15</a> Kuya kuthi ngaloo mini, ilityalwe iTire iminyaka engamashumi asixhenxe, njengemihla yokumkani omnye. Ekupheleni kweminyaka engamashumi asixhenxe kuya kwenzeka kwiTire ngokwengoma yehenyukazi, ethi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:16">23:16</a> Thabatha uhadi uwujikajike umzi, henyukazi lilityelweyo;  betha kamnandi; vuma iingoma ezininzi, ukuze ukhunjulwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:17">23:17</a> Kuya kuthi ekupheleni kweminyaka emashumi asixhenxe,  ayivelele iTire uYehova, ibuyele elutsheqweni lwayo, ihenyuzane nezikumkani zonke zehlabathi eziphezu komhlaba;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:18">23:18</a> lube ngcwele kuYehova urhwebo lwayo notsheqo lwayo; aluyi kubekwa, aluyi kuqwetywa; kuba urhwebo lwayo luya kuba lolwabahleli phambi koYehova, ukuze badle bahluthe, nokuze bambathe ngokobunene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:1">24:1</a> Yabona uYehova ulithi qongqololo ihlabathi, ulenza amagqagala, uyabuphethula ubuso balo, uyabachithachitha abemi balo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:2">24:2</a> kube mfani-nye abantu nababingeleli, kube mfani-nye ikhoboka nenkosi yalo, kube mfani-nye ikhobokazana nenkosikazi yalo, kube mfani-nye othengayo nothengisayo, kube mfani-nye obolekayo nobolekwayo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:3">24:3</a> kube mfani-nye umnikimali nomamkelimali. Ihlabathi lithiwe qongqololo ngakunye, liphangwe liphangiwe; kuba uYehova elithethile elo lizwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:4">24:4</a> Ihlabathi lenza isijwili, libunile; lintshwenyile, libunile elimiweyo; bathe matshamatsha abaphakamileyo ebantwini behlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:5">24:5</a> Ihlabathi lihlanjelwe ngaphantsi kwabemi balo; ngokokuba beyigqithile imiyalelo, badlula emimiselweni, bawaphula umnqophiso ongunaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:6">24:6</a> Ngenxa yoko lidliwe ihlabathi kukuqalekiswa, bathwele ityala abemiyo kulo; ngenxa yoko baphanzile abemi behlabathi,  kwasala abantu abambalwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:7">24:7</a> Iwayini entsha yenza isijwili, untshwenyile umdiliya,  bayancwina bonke abantliziyo inemivuyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:8">24:8</a> Iphelile imihlali yengqongqo; iyekile ingxokozelo yabadlamkileyo; iphelile imihlali yohadi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:9">24:9</a> Abayi kusela wayini benengoma; sikrakra isiselo esinxilisayo kwabasiselayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:10">24:10</a> Uqhekekile umzi osenyanyeni, zivalekile zonke izindlu ukuba zingangenwa mntu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:11">24:11</a> Bakhala ngewayini phandle; itshonile yonke imivuyo; iphele kwathi tu imihlali yehlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:12">24:12</a> Umzi usele walinxuwa, laqotywa isango layimvithi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:13">24:13</a> Kuba kuya kuba nje esazulwini sehlabathi lonke phakathi kwezizwe, kube njengasekuvuthululweni komnquma,  njengasekubhikiceni ukuphela kokuvuna iidiliya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:14">24:14</a> Bona aba baya kuphakamisa ilizwi, bamemelele; baya kutsholoza ngobungangamsha bukaYehova, beselwandle, bathi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:15">24:15</a> Ngenxa yoko, zukisani uYehova emimandleni yokukhanya:  igama likaYehova, uThixo kaSirayeli, eziqithini zolwandle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:16">24:16</a> Esondweni lehlabathi siva iingoma ezithi, Udumo malube kwilungisa. Ndaza ndathi, Hayi, ukungcungcutheka kwam!  ukungcungcutheka kwam! Athi ke mna! Amanginingini ayanginiza,  amanginingini ayanginiza ngonginizo lwawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:17">24:17</a> Ufikelwe lunkwantyo nomgongxo nesibatha, wena mmi wehlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:18">24:18</a> Kuya kuthi, othe walibaleka ilizwi elinkwantyisayo, eyele emgongxweni; othe wenyuka waphuma emgongxweni, abanjiswe sisibatha; ngokuba iingcango zaphezulu zivulekile, zanyikima iziseko zehlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:19">24:19</a> Liyavikiveka livikiveke ihlabathi; liyacandeka licandeke ihlabathi; liyashukuma lishukume ihlabathi; liyatalasa ihlabathi njengenxila;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:20">24:20</a> liyajinga njengomandlalo oxhonyiweyo; ukreqo lwalo lunzima phezu kwalo; liyawa, lingabuyi livuke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:21">24:21</a> Kuya kuthi ngaloo mini, awuvulele uYehova umkhosi wabaphezulu, nokumkani behlabathi ehlabathini;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:22">24:22</a> bahlanganiswe behlanganiswa njengamakhonkxwa emhadini,  bavalelwe entolongweni, bavelelwe kwakuba yimihla emininzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:23">24:23</a> Iya kuba neentloni inyanga, lidane ilanga, xa uYehova wemikhosi angukumkani entabeni yeZiyon, naseYerusalem, naphambi kwamadoda akhe amakhulu, ngobuqaqawuli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:1">25:1</a> Yehova, unguThixo wam; ndiya kukuphakamisa, ndiya kubulela kwigama lakho; ngokuba wenze imisebenzi ebalulekileyo, amacebo akho kwakude, ukunyaniseka, inyaniso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:2">25:2</a> Ngokuba umzi uwenze walinxuwa; inqaba enqatyisiweyo yangumwewe; uxande olude lwabasemzini alwaba mzi, ungakhiwa naphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:3">25:3</a> Ngenxa yoko baya kukuzukisa abantu abanengcwangu, ikoyike imizi yeentlanga ezingcangcazelisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:4">25:4</a> Ngokuba waba ligwiba kwisisweli, igwiba kwihlwempu ekubandezelweni kwalo, ihlathi esiphangweni, umthunzi lakubalela, xa ukufutha kwabangcangcazelisayo kwaba njengesiphango eludongeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:5">25:5</a> Njengokubalela emqwebedwini, udambise ingxolo yabasemzini;  njengokudanjiswa kokubalela lithunzi lelifu, yathotywa ngokunjalo ingoma yabangcangcazelisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:6">25:6</a> UYehova wemikhosi uya kuzenzela zonke izizwe isidlo sezinto ezityebileyo kule ntaba, isidlo sewayini egcinwe ngeentsipho,  sezinto ezityebileyo ezinomongo, sewayini egcinwe ngeentsipho,  yaza yahluzwa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:7">25:7</a> aginye kule ntaba umphambili wesigqubuthelo esizigqubutheleyo izizwe zonke, nesigubungelo esizigubungeleyo zonke iintlanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:8">25:8</a> Iya kuginya ukufa kuphele, izisule iNkosi uYehova iinyembezi ebusweni bonke, ingcikivo yabantu bayo iyisuse ehlabathini lonke, kuba uYehova ethethile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:9">25:9</a> Kuya kuthiwa ngaloo mini, Yabona, lo nguThixo wethu;  besithembele kuye, ukuba asisindise; nguYehova lo besithembele kuye; masigcobe, sivuye ngosindiso lwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:10">25:10</a> Ngokuba isandla sikaYehova siya kuhlala phezu kwale ntaba,  anyathelwe amaMowabhi endaweni yawo, njengokunyathelwa komququ emanzini omgquba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:11">25:11</a> Aya kuzaneka izandla zawo emthonyameni wawo, njengokuba indadi izaneka izandla ukuba idade; ke uYehova uya kulithoba ikratshi lawo, kunye nezigcaliselo zezandla zawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:12">25:12</a> Wozisibekekisa iindonga zakho ezinqabileyo eziphakamileyo,  azigungxule, ade azifikise emhlabeni, eluthulini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:1">26:1</a> Ngaloo mini kuya kuvunywa le ngoma ezweni lakwaYuda, ithi,  Yinqaba umzi wethu thina; umisa iidonga nongqameko zibe lusindiso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:2">26:2</a> Vulani amasango, lungene uhlanga olunobulungisa, olugcine ukuthembeka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:3">26:3</a> Intliziyo ezimasekileyo uyayilondoloza, ixole ixolile;  ngokuba ikholose ngawe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:4">26:4</a> Kholosani ngoYehova ngonaphakade; kuba uYa, uYehova,  uliliwa elingunaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:5">26:5</a> Ngokuba uthulele phantsi abahleli phezulu; umzi oyingxonde uwugungxule wawugungxulela emhlabeni, wawufikisa eluthulini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:6">26:6</a> Ziyawunyasha iinyawo, iinyawo zeentsizana, amanyathelo ezisweli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:7">26:7</a> Umendo wamalungisa ulungelelene; wena uyawulinganisela umkhondo wamalungisa, ulungelelane.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:8">26:8</a> Kakade, Yehova, sibe sikulindile, ukuba uze emendweni wemigwebo yakho; umnqweno womphefumlo wethu wasinga egameni lakho, nasekukukhumbuleni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:9">26:9</a> Nangomphefumlo wam ndakunqwenela ebusuku; inene, ngomoya wam phakathi kwam ndakufuna kwakusasa; ngokuba xenikweni imigwebo yakho ibhekiswe ehlabathini, baya kufunda ubulungisa abemi belimiweyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:10">26:10</a> Nokuba uthe wababalwa ongendawo, akafundi bulungisa;  nasezweni labathe gca uyagqwetha; akabuboni ubungangamsha bukaYehova.</p>
