 <p><a name="an_26:11">26:11</a> Yehova, sibe siphakamile isandla sakho, ababona; ke baya kulibona ikhwele lakho ngenxa yabantu, badane; ewe, umlilo mawubadle ababandezeli bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:12">26:12</a> Yehova, uya kusimisela uxolo; ngokuba nezenzo zethu zonke usisebenzele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:13">26:13</a> Yehova Thixo wethu, iinkosi ezingenguwe bezinobukhosi phezu kwethu; kodwa sikhankanya igama lakho ngawe wedwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:14">26:14</a> Abafileyo abo abasayi kuba saphila; abangasekhoyo abo abasayi kuba savuka; ngoko ke ubavelele wabatshabalalisa,  wakwenza kwadaka konke ukukhunjulwa kwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:15">26:15</a> Ulwandisile uhlanga, Yehova, ulwandisile uhlanga;  uzizukisile; uzikhwelelisele kude iziphelo zelizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:16">26:16</a> Yehova, embandezelweni baquqela kuwe, bathulula umthandazo ngelizwi eliphantsi ekubathethiseni kwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:17">26:17</a> Njengomithiyo eza kuzala, ezibhijabhija, ekhaliswa yinimba, saba njalo phambi kwakho, Yehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:18">26:18</a> Sibe simithi, sibe sizibhijabhija, sanga sizele umoya.  Asilenzelanga sindiso ilizwe, abaphumanga abemi belimiweyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:19">26:19</a> Abafileyo bakho baya kuphila; izidumbu zakowethu ziya kuvuka. Vukani, nimemelele, nina bahleli eluthulini; kuba ngumbethe wezikhanyiso umbethe wakho, nehlabathi liya kubakhupha abangasekhoyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:20">26:20</a> Hambani, bantu bam, ningene ezingontsini zenu, nivale iingcango zenu ngasemva kwenu, nizimele umzuzwana, kude kudlule ukubhavuma.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:21">26:21</a> Kuba, yabona, uYehova uphuma endaweni yakhe, ukuze abuvelele kubo ubugwenxa babemi behlabathi; ihlabathi lowatyhila amagazi alo, lingabi sabaselela ababuleweyo balo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:1">27:1</a> Ngaloo mini uYehova uya kuyivelela ngekrele lakhe, elo lilukhuni, elo likhulu, elo lomeleleyo, ileviyatan inyoka ebalekayo, neleviyatan inyoka ephinyaphinyelayo; ayibulale ingwenya eselwandle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:2">27:2</a> Ngaloo mini kuya kuthiwa, Isidiliya esinqwenelekayo,  hlabelani ngaso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:3">27:3</a> Mna Yehova ndingumlondolozi waso; ndiya kusinyela ngamaxesha onke, ndiya kusilondoloza ubusuku nemini, hleze sivelelwe yinto.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:4">27:4</a> Ubushushu abukho kum; akwaba bekukho ubobo namakhakakhaka phambi kwam! Bendiya kugaleleka kuwo ngokulwa, bendiya kuwatshisa kanye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:5">27:5</a> Okanye mababambelele egwibeni lam, baxolelane nam, ewe,  baxolelane nam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:6">27:6</a> Ngezayo imihla uYakobi uya kwendelisela iingcambu,  atyatyambe adubule uSirayeli, balizalise lonke elimiweyo ngeziqhamo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:7">27:7</a> Umbethe ngokubetha kwababethi bakhe na? Mhlawumbi ubulewe ngokubulawa kwababulewe nguye na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:8">27:8</a> Ekumaleni wabambana naye, walinganisela, wakha uluhlu,  wamgxotha ngomoya wakhe owomeleleyo ngemini yomoya wasempumalanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:9">27:9</a> Ngako oko ubugwenxa bukaYakobi buya kucanyagushelwa ngale nto; isiqhamo sonke sokususa isono sakhe soba sesi sokuthi,  awenze onke amatye esibingelelo abe njengamatye ekalika ankumenkume, bangavuki ooAshera nezithixo zelanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:10">27:10</a> Ngokuba umzi onqatyisiweyo uwodwa, usisithili esilahliweyo, esishiyiweyo njengentlango. Aya kudla khona amathole, abuthe khona, awadle awagqibe khona amahlamvu aso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:11">27:11</a> Othi akoma amasebe aso, aphulwe; beze abafazi, bawabase;  kuba asibantu banangqondo aba; ngako oko umenzi wabo akayi kuba namfesane kubo, umbumbi wabo akayi kubababala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:12">27:12</a> Kuya kuthi ngaloo mini, abhulise uYehova, athabathele emsingeni woMlambo, ase esihlanjeni saseYiputa, nihlanganiselwe omnye komnye, nina nyana bakaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:13">27:13</a> Kuya kuthi ngaloo mini, kuvuthelwe isigodlo esikhulu, beze ababelahlekele ezweni laseAsiriya, nababegxothelwe ezweni lamaYiputa, baqubude kuYehova entabeni engcwele eseYerusalem.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:1">28:1</a> Yaha ke, isithsaba sekratshi samanxila akwaEfrayim,  nentyantyambo ebunayo yamakhazikhazi esihombo sakhe,  esemantloko omfula ochumayo wababuleweyo yiwayini!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:2">28:2</a> Yabona, iNkosi inento eyomeleleyo, ekhaliphileyo,  njengesiphango sesichotho, isaqhwithi esibhubhisayo;  njengesiphango esimanzi anamandla akhukulayo, iya kunqumela emhlabeni ngesandla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:3">28:3</a> Siya kunyashwa ngeenyawo isithsaba sekratshi samanxila akwaEfrayim.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:4">28:4</a> Intyantyambo ebunayo yamakhazikhazi esihombo sakhe,  esemantloko omfula ochumayo, yoba njengekhiwane elilikhikhizela, kungekabi sehlotyeni; athi olibonileyo alibone, aliginye esaliphethe ngesandla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:5">28:5</a> Ngaloo mini uYehova wemikhosi uya kuba sisithsaba esimakhazikhazi, nesangqawe sokuhomba kumasalela abantu bakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:6">28:6</a> abe ngumoya wesiko kwabahleli esihlalweni sokugweba,  nobugorha kwababuyisela imfazwe esangweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:7">28:7</a> Kwanaba ke bayotywe yiwayini, bayahexa sisiselo esinxilisayo; umbingeleli nomprofeti bayotywe sisiselo esinxilisayo, baginywe yiwayini, bayahexa sisiselo esinxilisayo; bayotyiwe bebona imibono, bayagexa begweba ityala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:8">28:8</a> Kuba zonke izithebe zizele ngumhlanzo oyintshontsho; akukho ndawo ingenawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:9">28:9</a> Bathi, Uya kuyala bani na ukuba azi? aqondise bani na udaba? Abalunyulweyo emasini? abancothulweyo ebeleni?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:10">28:10</a> Kuba umthetho uza phezu komthetho, umthetho phezu komthetho; ummiselo phezu kommiselo, ummiselo phezu kommiselo;  intwana apha, intwana phaya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:11">28:11</a> Inene, uya kuthetha ngentetho ethintithayo nangalulwimi lumbi kwaba bantu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:12">28:12</a> watshoyo kubo ukuthi, Nantsi indawo yokuphumla, phumzani abatyhafileyo; nantsi indawo yokunyhamnyheka; basuka abavuma ukuva.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:13">28:13</a> Ngoko ke ilizwi likaYehova loba ngumthetho phezu komthetho kubo, umthetho phezu komthetho; ngummiselo phezu kommiselo,  ummiselo phezu kommiselo; intwana apha, intwana phaya: ukuze baye bakhubeke, bawe ngomva, baphuke, barhintyelwe, babanjiswe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:14">28:14</a> Ngako oko liveni ilizwi likaYehova, madoda agxekayo,  balawuli baba bantu baseYerusalem.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:15">28:15</a> Ngokuba nisithi, Sinqophisene nokufa, sivumelene nelabafileyo; isibetho esingumkhukula, xa singenelayo, asiyi kufika kuthi, kuba amanga siwenze ihlathi lethu, sasithela ngobuxoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:16">28:16</a> Ngako oko itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Yabona, ndiseke eZiyon ilitye, ilitye locikido, ilitye elinqabileyo lembombo,  loseko olusekiweyo. Okholiweyo akayi kungxama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:17">28:17</a> Isiko ndolenza intambo yokulinganisa, ubulungisa ndibenze ilothe yokulungelelanisa; isichotho siya kumka nalo ihlathi lamanga, amanzi ayikhukulise indawo yokusithela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:18">28:18</a> Kuya kucinywa ukunqophisana kwenu nokufa, kungemi ukuvumelana kwenu nelabafileyo; isibetho esingumkhukula, xa singenelayo, sonenza nibe yinto egqushiweyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:19">28:19</a> Oku kungenela singenelayo, siya kunisusa; ngokuba imiso ngemiso siya kuningenela, imini nobusuku; kuthi ukuqonda udaba kube kukuhlasimla kodwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:20">28:20</a> Inene, umandlalo mfutshane, akukho kunaba; nesigubungelo sincinane, ukuba azisongele kuso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:21">28:21</a> Ngokuba uya kusuk eme uYehova, njengasentabeni yePeratsim; uya kuguguma, njengasentilini yeGibheyon; ukuba enze isenzo sakhe, isenzo sakhe esisodwa, ukuba asebenze umsebenzi wakhe, umsebenzi wakhe ongaqhelekileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:22">28:22</a> Kaloku ke musani ukugxeka, hleze kuqiniselwe ukubotshelelwa kwenu; ngokokuba isiphelo esiya kulifikela ilizwe lonke sisesimisiweyo ke sagqitywa; ndisivile eNkosini,  uYehova wemikhosi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:23">28:23</a> Libekeleni indlebe nilive ilizwi lam; yibazeleni indlebe niyive intetho yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:24">28:24</a> Umlimi ulima iimini ezi zonke na, ukuba ahlwayele? anqike aqwakanise umhlaba wakhe na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:25">28:25</a> Akathi na, akuba ebulungelelanisile ubuso bawo, asasaze idile, agcwayele ikumin, akrozise ingqolowa, nerhasi endaweni ephawuliweyo, nespelete ngasemdeni wayo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:26">28:26</a> Umqeqeshile ngokwesiko uThixo wakhe, wamyala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:27">28:27</a> Kuba idile ayisizilwa ngempahla yokusizila, ayiqengqelwa ngevili yenqwelo ikumin; itsinwa ngoswazi idile, nekumin ngentonga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:28">28:28</a> Ingqolowa ikhe ityunyuzwe na? Hayi, akahlali eyisizila,  agoqozise ivili yenqwelo yakhe namahashe akhe phezu kwayo;  akayityumzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:29">28:29</a> Nale nto iphuma kuYehova wemikhosi; omacebo angummangaliso, obulumko butshatsheleyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:1">29:1</a> Yeha, Ariyeli, Ariyeli, mzi awamisa intente kuwo uDavide!  Yongezelelani umnyaka kumnyaka; mayizunguleze imithendeleko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:2">29:2</a> Ndiya kuyicutha ke iAriyeli, kubekho ukuncwina noncwino,  ibe njengeAriyeli ke leyo kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:3">29:3</a> Ndiya kukurhawula, ndikungqinge ngenqaba, ndikumisele iintango zokukungqinga;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:4">29:4</a> uya kugungxulelwa phantsi, uthethe usemhlabeni, ukuthetha kwakho kudambe, kuvela eluthulini; izwi lakho liphume emhlabeni njengeloneshologu, ukuthetha kwakho kudumzele eluthulini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:5">29:5</a> Ingxokolo yabakungenelayo iya kuba njengothuli olucolekileyo, ingxokolo yabakungcangcazelisayo ibe njengomququ ophephukayo; ibekho le nto ngephanyazo nangesiquphe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:6">29:6</a> Kuphuma kuYehova wemikhosi ukuvelelwa kwayo ngeendudumo nangonyikimo lwehlabathi, nesandi esikhulu; ngesaqhwithi nomoya ovuthuzayo, nokulenya komlilo otshisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:7">29:7</a> Yoba njengephupha, njengombono wasebusuku, ingxokolo yeentlanga zonke eziyiphumela umkhosi iAriyeli; zonke eziyiphumela umkhosi, yona nemboniselo yayo, eziyicuthayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:8">29:8</a> Koba njengokuthi olambileyo aphuphe, abone esidla, avuke ulambatha umphefumlo wakhe; njengokuthi onxaniweyo aphuphe,  abone esela, avuke, nanko etyhafile, utshoba umphefumlo wakhe;  iya kuba njalo ingxokolo yeentlanga eziyiphumele umkhosi intaba yeZiyon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:9">29:9</a> Zilazilani ningakhulumi; zimfamekiseni nibe ziimfama.  Bayanxila kungengawayini, bayatalasa kungengasiselo sinxilisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:10">29:10</a> Ngokuba uYehova uthulule phezu kwenu umoya wobuthongo obukhulu, wawabopha amehlo enu, abaprofeti; nabaziintloko benu,  iimboni zenu, uzigubungele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:11">29:11</a> Kuni umbono weento zonke ube njengamazwi encwadi etywiniweyo, abathi bayinike okwaziyo ukuyifunda, besithi,  Khawulese apha; athi, Ndikhohliwe, kuba itywiniwe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:12">29:12</a> incwadi inikwe ongakwaziyo ukuyifunda, kuthiwe, Khawulese apha; athi, Andikwazi ukuyifunda incwadi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:13">29:13</a> Yathi iNkosi, Ngenxa enokuba aba bantu besondela kum ngomlomo wabo, bendizukisa ngemilebe yomlomo wabo, intliziyo yabo beyikhwelelisele kude kum, nokundoyika kwabo kungumthetho wabantu abawufunda nje kodwa:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:14">29:14</a> ngako oko, yabona, ndiya kuphinda ndibaphathe aba bantu ngokubalulekileyo, kubaluleke, kumangaliseke; butshone ubulumko bezilumko zabo, isithele ingqondo yeengqondi zabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:15">29:15</a> Yeha ke abangxokayo, besithelisa iqhinga labo kuYehova,  zibe semnyameni izenzo zabo: bathi, Ngubani na osibonayo?  ngubani na osaziyo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:16">29:16</a> Hayi, ukuphenduka kwenu! Kuya kuthiwa umbumbi unjengodongwe na? into eyenziweyo ithi na kumenzi wayo,  Akandenzanga? into ebunjiweyo ithi na kumbumbi wayo, Akaqondi?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:17">29:17</a> Awusemncinane na umzuzwana, ukuze iLebhanon ibuye ibe yintsimi echumayo, intsimi echumayo kuthiwe lihlathi?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:18">29:18</a> Kuya kuthi ngaloo mini izithulu ziweve amazwi encwadi,  amehlo eemfama abone esithokothokweni nasemnyameni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:19">29:19</a> Abalulamileyo baya kukwandisa ukuvuya ngoYehova,  abangamahlwempu eluntwini bagcobe ngoyiNgcwele kaSirayeli;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:20">29:20</a> ngokuba esusiwe umngcangcazelisi, ephelile umgxeki,  benqunyulwe bonke abaphaphela ubutshinga;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:21">29:21</a> abamenza umoni umntu ngenxa yelizwi eli, bamthiyele owohlwayayo esangweni, balisunduze ilungisa ngochuku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:22">29:22</a> Ngako oko utsho uYehova kwindlu kaYakobi, lowo wamkhululayo uAbraham, ukuthi, Ngoku uYakobi akayi kudana,  ngoku ubuso bakhe abuyi kuba luthuthu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:23">29:23</a> Ngokuba ekuboneni kwakhe, ekuboneni kwabantwana bakhe,  isenzo sezandla zam phakathi kwabo, baya kulingcwalisa igama lam, bamngcwalise oyiNgcwele kaYakobi, bangcangcazele phambi koThixo kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:24">29:24</a> Baya kukwazi ukuqonda abamoya undwendwayo, bayamkele imfundo abakrokrayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:1">30:1</a> Yeha ke, abantwana abaziinjubaqa, utsho uYehova; abenza iqhinga elingaphumi kum, bathelelane ngothelelwano kungengaMoya wam, ukuze bongeze isono kwisono;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:2">30:2</a> abahamba bahle baye eYiputa, bengabuzanga emlonyeni wam,  basabele egwibeni likaFaro, bazimele ngomthunzi weYiputa!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:3">30:3</a> Ngoko ke liya kuthi igwiba likaFaro libe lidano kuni,  nokuzimela ngomthunzi weYiputa kube lihlazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:4">30:4</a> Ngokuba abathetheli babo baseTsohan, nabathunywa babo bafike eHanes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:5">30:5</a> Bonke baya kudana ngabantu abangabanyusiyo,  abangengabokunceda, nabangengabokunyusa; abangabokudanisa,  abangabokuhlazisa kananjalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:6">30:6</a> Isihlabo esisingisele kwimvubu yelasezantsi. Ezweni leembandezelo nengcutheko, lengonyamakazi nengonyama, lephimpi,  lenyushu enobuhlungu ephaphazelayo, babethwele ubutyebi babo ngemihlana yamankonyana amaesile, nobuncwane babo ngamalunda eenkamela, besiya kubantu abangenakubanyusa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:7">30:7</a> AmaYiputa ke aya kunceda ngokungekwanto nangokulambathayo;  ngako oko ndithe ngawo angabagwagwisayo, behleli phantsi bethe tu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:8">30:8</a> Yiya ngoku, ukrole oko elucwecweni unabo, ukubhale encwadini, kube yinto yemihla ezayo, yanini, yaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:9">30:9</a> Ngokuba ngabantu abaneenkani, ngoonyana abaxokayo,  ngoonyana abangavumiyo ukusiva isiyalo sikaYehova;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:10">30:10</a> abathi kwiimboni, Ze ningaboni; nakwiinkangeli, Ze ningasikhangeleli izinto ezithe gca; sithetheleni izinto ezigudileyo; khangelani izinto eziyinkohliso;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:11">30:11</a> tyekani endleleni, yithini gu bucala emendweni; menzeni aphele ebusweni bethu oyiNgcwele kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:12">30:12</a> Ngako oko utsho oyiNgcwele kaSirayeli ukuthi, Ngokokuba nilicekisile elo lizwi, nakholosa ngokucudisa nangobugwenxa,  nayama khona:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:13">30:13</a> ngako oko, obo bugwenxa kuni buya kuba njengendawo ekrazukileyo, ewayo, ezimkayo eludongeni olude, ekuqhekeka kwayo kuza ngesiquphe nangephanyazo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:14">30:14</a> uya kuyiqhekeza njengokuqhekeka komphanda wombumbi,  wakuqotywa ungayekwa, kungafumaneki ekuqotyweni kwawo negophe lokuthabatha umlilo eziko, nelokukha amanzi equleni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:15">30:15</a> Ngokuba itsho iNkosi, uYehova oyiNgcwele kaSirayeli,  ukuthi, Beniya kusindiswa kukubuya nakukuphumla; ebengabakhoyo amandla enu ngokuzola nangokukholosa; nasuka anavuma.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:16">30:16</a> Ke nathi, Hayi, siya kubaleka ngamahashe; niya kubaleka kambe. Nathi, Siya kukhwela kwiimbaleki; ngenxa yoko baya kuba namendu abanisukelayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:17">30:17</a> Niya kubaleka niliwaka, ekhalime emnye; bekhalime bebahlanu, nibaleke nide nisale njengomtshanyane encotsheni yentaba, nanjengebhanile endulini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:18">30:18</a> Ngako oko uYehova uya kukha alinde, ukuze anibabale; ngako oko uya kukha akhwelele phezulu, ukuze abe nemfesane kuni;  ngokuba nguThixo wogwebo uYehova; hayi, uyolo lwabo bonke abalindele kuye!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:19">30:19</a> Ngokuba abantu aba baya kuhlala eZiyon, eYerusalem; aniyi kuba sabuya nilile; uya kunibabala ngenene ekuvakaleni kokukhala kwenu; akukuva, uya kusabela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:20">30:20</a> INkosi iya kuninika isonka sobandezelweyo namanzi oxiniweyo, bangabi sazimela abayali bakho, amehlo akho esababona abayali bakho;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:21">30:21</a> iindlebe zakho zive ilizwi ngasemva kwakho, lisithi,  Nantsi indlela; hambani ngayo, nokuba nisinga ekunene, nokuba nisinga ekhohlo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:22">30:22</a> Nowenza inqambi umaleko wemifanekiso yenu eqingqiweyo yesilivere, nesingxobo semifanekiso yenu etyhidiweyo yegolide;  niya kuyichithachitha njengesishuba; uya kuthi kuyo, Khwelela umke apha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:23">30:23</a> INkosi yoyinika imvula imbewu yakho, owuhlwayela ngayo umhlaba; nesonka songeniselo lomhlaba sityebe, sibe namafutha;  imfuyo yakho iya kudla ngaloo mini emadlelweni abanzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:24">30:24</a> Iinkomo namaesile amatsha asebenza umhlaba, aya kudla umtywakaniselo onetyuwa, oweliweyo ngomnyazi nefolokhwe yokwela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:25">30:25</a> Phezu kweentaba zonke ezinde naphezu kweenduli zonke eziphakamileyo yoba yimijelo, yimisinga yamanzi, ngemini yembulalo enkulu, ekuweni kweenqaba ezinde.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:26">30:26</a> Ukukhanya kwenyanga kuya kuba njengokukhanya kwelanga,  nokukhanya kwelanga kube kasixhenxe njengokukhanya kweemini ezisixhenxe, ngemini yokubopha kukaYehova ukwaphuka kwabantu bakhe, apholise ukuphalusa kokubetha kwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:27">30:27</a> Yabona, igama likaYehova liyeza, livela kude, uvutha umsindo wakhe, kuthe shinyi umsi: umlomo wakhe ulephuza amagwebu, ulwimi lwakhe lunjengomlilo otshisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:28">30:28</a> Ukufutha kwakhe kunjengomlambo okhukulayo, obetha emqaleni, ukuze azihluze iintlanga ngentluzo yokuziphanzisa,  umkhala olahlekisayo ube semihlathini yezizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:29">30:29</a> Niya kuba nengoma enjengeyobusuku bokungcwaliswa komthendeleko, novuyo lwentliziyo lube njengabahamba bebetha ugwali, ukuya entabeni kaYehova, eliweni likaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:30">30:30</a> Uya kulivakalisa uYehova izwi lakhe elinendili,  akubonakalise ukuhla kwengalo yakhe kunokujala ngumsindo,  nokulenya komlilo otshisayo, nokuphalazeka kwelifu, nesiphango,  namatye esichotho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:31">30:31</a> Kuba uAsiriya uya kuqhiphuka umbilini lilizwi likaYehova,  ekubetheni kwakhe ngentonga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:32">30:32</a> Kuya kuthi konke ukuhamba koswazi lommiselo, aluhlisayo uYehova phezu kwakhe, kube neengqongqo neehadi, kusiliwa naye imfazwe, kujinga ingalo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:33">30:33</a> Kuba kukade icangcisiwe, ilungisiwe iTofete, ibe ke ilungiselwe ukumkani; yenziwa yanzulu, yabanzi; igoqo layo linomlilo neenkuni ezininzi; ukuphefumla kukaYehova kuliphemba njengomlambo wesulfure.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:1">31:1</a> Yeha, abehla baye eYiputa ukuba bancedwe, abayama ngamahashe, abakholosa ngeenqwelo zokulwa, kuba zininzi,  nangabamahashe, kuba beqine kunene; abangamnoneleli oyiNgcwele kaSirayeli, abangamquqeliyo uYehova!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:2">31:2</a> Ulumkile ke naye; uya kuzisa ububi, angawabeki nxamnye amazwi akhe; uya kusukela phezulu kwindlu yabenzi bobubi,  nakuncedo lwabasebenza ubutshinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:3">31:3</a> AmaYiputa angabantu, akaThixo; amahashe awo ayinyama,  akamoya; ukuba uYehova angasolula isandla sakhe, wokhubeka umncedi, awe umncedwa, baphele kunye bonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:4">31:4</a> Ngokuba uYehova utshilo kum ukuthi, Njengokuba ingonyama,  nengonyama entsha, isuka igqume phezu kwento eyibambileyo,  yakubizelwa ihlokondiba labalusi, ingaloyiki ilizwi labo,  ingayilahli ngokuxokozela kwabo: kwangokunjalo uya kuhla uYehova wemikhosi, ukuba ayikhuphele umkhosi intaba yeZiyon nenduli yayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:5">31:5</a> Njengeentaka zindanda, uya kwenjenjalo uYehova wemikhosi ukuyikhusela iYerusalem, eyikhusela, eyihlangula, eyiconga,  eyisiza.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:6">31:6</a> Buyelani kulowo nimkileyo kuye ngokunzulu, nyana bakaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:7">31:7</a> Ngokuba ngaloo mini baya kucekisa elowo izithixo zakhe zesilivere ezingeni, nezegolide ezingeni, ezinenzele zona izandla zenu, ukuba none ngazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:8">31:8</a> Wowa uAsiriya likrele elingelelandoda, limdle ikrele elingelelamntu, asabe phambi kwekrele, amadodana akhe afakwe uviko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:9">31:9</a> Ingxondorha yakhe yodlula imke ngokunxunguphala, baqhiphuke umbilini abathetheli bakhe, bemke kwibhanile; utsho uYehova,  omlilo useZiyon, oziko liseYerusalem.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:1">32:1</a> Yabona, ukumkani uya kulawula ngokobulungisa, abathetheli bathethele ngokwesiko;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:2">32:2</a> umntu abe njengendawo yokuzimela umoya, neyokusithela esiphangweni; abe njengemijelo yamanzi emqwebedwini,  njengomthunzi wengxondorha enkulu ezweni elibharhileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:3">32:3</a> Akayi kuvingcwa amehlo ababonayo; zibazeke iindlebe zabevayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:4">32:4</a> Yoqonda ukwazi intliziyo yabangxamayo, ulwimi lwabathintithayo lungxamise ukuthetha ngokuthe tyhatyhasini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:5">32:5</a> Isidenge akuyi kuba sathiwa silinene, itshivela akuyi kuthiwa lilinono;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:6">32:6</a> kuba isidenge sithetha ubudenge, intliziyo yaso yenza ubutshinga, ukuze senze ububi; sithetha into yokubhuda ngoYehova, silambathise umphefumlo wolambileyo, simswelise onxaniweyo into eselwayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:7">32:7</a> Ubutshivela betshivela bubi; liceba amayelenqe okonakalisa iintsizana ngamazwi obuxoki, naxa ihlwempu lithetha ngokusesikweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:8">32:8</a> Inene lona liceba izinto zobunene; lona limi ngezinto zobunene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:9">32:9</a> Bafazi batyeshileyo, sukani nime; liveni ilizwi lam,  zintombi zingakhathaliyo; yibekeleni indlebe intetho yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:10">32:10</a> Iya kuba ziintsuku nokuba ngumnyaka, nigungqe, zintokazi zingakhathaliyo; kuba kuphelile ukuvuna izidiliya; ukubutha iziqhamo akuyi kubakho nakanye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:11">32:11</a> Gubhani, zintokazi zityeshileyo; gungqani, zintokazi zingakhathaliyo; hlubani nichushuluze, nibhinqe ezirhwexayo emanqeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:12">32:12</a> Baya kubetha emabeleni ngenxa yamasimi anqwenelekayo,  nangenxa yemidiliya eneziqhamo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:13">32:13</a> Kuya kuphuma imithi enameva namakhakakhaka emhlabeni wabantu bakowethu; ewe, naphezu kwezindlu zonke zemihlali kumzi odlamkileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:14">32:14</a> Kuba iingxande ezinde zilahliwe, ingxokolo yomzi ishiyiwe;  iOfele nemboniselo ziza kuba yimiqolomba ngonaphakade, zibe ziindawo zokudlamkela kwamaesile asendle, zibe lidlelo lemihlambi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:15">32:15</a> ade agalelwe phezu kwethu uMoya ophuma phezulu, isuke intlango ibe yintsimi echumayo, intsimi echumayo kuthiwe lihlathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:16">32:16</a> Entlango ke kuya kuma okusesikweni, buhlale ubulungisa entsimini echumayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:17">32:17</a> Wothi umsebenzi wobulungisa ube luxolo, nokwenza kobulungisa kube kukuzola nokukholosa ngonaphakade;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:18">32:18</a> abantu bakowethu baya kuhlala esithilini esinoxolo,  eminqubeni yenkoloseko, ezindaweni zokuphumla ezinokonwaba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:19">32:19</a> Kuya kuphalala izichotho ekuweni kwehlathi, ugungxulelwe umzi endaweni ephantsi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:20">32:20</a> Hayi, uyolo lwenu bahlwayela ngasemanzini onke, bayekele amanqina enkomo nawe-esile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:1">33:1</a> Yeha ke, mbhuqi, wena ke ungabhuqwanga; nginingini, wena ke ungatshinizelwanga! Wakugqiba ukubhuqa, uya kubhuqwa;  wakukufeza ukunginiza, uya kunginizelwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:2">33:2</a> Yehova, sibabale, sithembele kuwe; yiba yingalo yabo imiso ngemiso; yiba lusindiso kuthi ngexesha lembandezelo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:3">33:3</a> Ziyaphalaphaliswa izizwe lilizwi lengxokolo,  ziyaphangalaliswa iintlanga kukuphakama kwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:4">33:4</a> Ohlanganiswa emke amaxhoba enu njengokuhlanganisa kweenkumbi ezinqunquthayo, bawaququzelele njengokuququzela komqikela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:5">33:5</a> UYehova uphakamile, ngokuba ehleli phezulu; uyizalisile iZiyon ngokusesikweni nangobulungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:6">33:6</a> Kuya kubakho ukuzimaseka kwamaxesha akho, nobutyebi bosindiso, nobulumko, nokwazi; ukoyika uYehova bubuncwane bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:7">33:7</a> Yabona, iinjengele zabo ziyakhala ngaphandle; abathunywa boxolo balila ngokukrakra.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:8">33:8</a> Iindlela azihanjwa; umhambi uphelile; uwaphule umnqophiso,  ucekise imizi, akakhathalela mntu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:9">33:9</a> Ilizwe lenza isijwili, lintshwenyile; ineentloni iLebhanon,  ishwabene; iSharon isuke yaba njengenkqantosi; ivuthulula amagqabi iBhashan neKarmele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:10">33:10</a> Kungokunje ndiya kusuka ndime, utsho uYehova; kungokunje ndiya kuphakama; kungokunje ndiya kuzinyusa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:11">33:11</a> Niya kumitha isikhotha, nizale iindiza; ukufutha kwenu ngumlilo oya kunidla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:12">33:12</a> Izizwe zoba yimitshiso yekalika, zoba yimithi enameva ehlahliweyo, ibaswe umlilo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:13">33:13</a> Yivani, nina bakude, endikwenzileyo: nibazi ubugorha bam,  nina basondeleyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:14">33:14</a> Bayankwantya eZiyon aboni, abaziintshembenxa babanjwe kukuthuthumela; bathi, Ngubani na ke kuthi onokuphambukela emlilweni odlayo? ngubani na ke kuthi onokuphambukela emalangatyeni angunaphakade?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:15">33:15</a> Ohamba ngobulungisa, othetha okuthe tye, ocekisa inzuzo yokucudisa, ovuthulula isandla sakhe singaphathi sicengo,  ovingca iindlebe zakhe zingevi ngegazi, ocima amehlo akhe angakhangeli entweni embi:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:16">33:16</a> nguye oya kuhlala ezindaweni eziphezulu. Iimboniselo zeengxondorha yingxonde yakhe; isonka sakhe usinikiwe, amanzi akhe ahleli ekho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:17">33:17</a> Amehlo akho aya kumkhangela ukumkani ebuhleni bakhe; aya kulibona ilizwe elisingise kude.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:18">33:18</a> Intliziyo yakho iya kucamanga ngesothuso, ithi, Uphi na umbali? uphi na umlinganiseli? uphi na umbali weenqaba ezinde?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:19">33:19</a> Abantu abaziingwanyalala akuyi kubabona: abantu abantetho inzulu, ingavakaliyo, abalulwimi luthintithayo lungenakuqondeka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:20">33:20</a> Khangela iZiyon, umzi wemithendeleko yethu. Amehlo akho aya kuyibona iYerusalem, isithili esinokonwaba, iyintente engafuduswayo, ezikhonkwane zingancothulwayo naphakade,  ezintambo zonke zingaqhawukiyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:21">33:21</a> Ewe, ngenxa yethu ikhona ingangamsha uYehova; yindawo enemilambo, enemijelo ebanzi ngeenxa zombini; akuyi kuhamba sinqanawa sibheqwayo apho, kungaweli khona nqanawa iyingangamsha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:22">33:22</a> Kuba umgwebi wethu nguYehova, ummisimthetho wethu nguYehova, ukumkani wethu nguYehova; uya kusisindisa yena.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:23">33:23</a> Zityeketyeke iintambo zakho, azilubambi useko lwemasti yazo, aziyitwabululi iseyile; kuya kwandula kwabiwe amaxhoba amaninzi athinjiweyo, neziqhwala ziphange okuphangiweyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:24">33:24</a> Akayi kuthi ummi wakhona, Ndiyafa; abantu abahleliyo khona babuxolelwe ubugwenxa babo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:1">34:1</a> Sondelani, zintlanga, nive; nibaze iindlebe, zizwe; malive ihlabathi nenzaliseko yalo; elimiweyo, neziveliso zonke eziveliswa lilo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:2">34:2</a> Ngokuba uburhalarhume bukaYehova buphezu kweentlanga zonke,  nobushushu bakhe buphezu komkhosi wazo wonke; uzisingele phantsi, uzinikele ekusikweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:3">34:3</a> Baya kulahlwa ababuleweyo bazo, nezidumbu zabo kunyuke ukunuka kwazo, kunyibilike iintaba ligazi lazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:4">34:4</a> Uya kuvunda wonke umkhosi wezulu, lisongwe izulu njengencwadi, wonke umkhosi walo ubune njengokubuna kwegqabi emdiliyeni, njengokubuna kwegqabi emkhiwaneni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:5">34:5</a> Ngokuba lisele lahlutha ezulwini ikrele lam; yabona, lihla phezu koEdom, naphezu kwabantu endibasingele phantsi, ibe ngumgwebo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:6">34:6</a> Ikrele likaYehova lizele ligazi, lityetyiswe ngamanqatha,  ligazi leemvana neleebhokhwe, ngamanqatha ezintso zeenkunzi zeegusha; ngokuba uYehova unombingelelo eBhotsera, nokuxhela okukhulu ezweni lakwaEdom.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:7">34:7</a> Kuya kuhla inqu kunye nazo, iinkunzi ezintsha kunye neenkabi, lisele lihluthe ilizwe labo ligazi, lutyetyiswe uthuli lwabo ngamanqatha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:8">34:8</a> Kuba uYehova unomhla wempindezelo, unomnyaka wembuyekezo,  wokuthethelela iZiyon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:9">34:9</a> Yoguquka imilambo yabo ibe yitela, uthuli lwabo lube yisulfure, ilizwe labo libe yitela etshayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:10">34:10</a> Aliyi kucinywa ubusuku nemini; umsi walo uya kunyuka ngonaphakade; liya kuchithakala kwisizukulwana ngesizukulwana;  liya kuhlala lihleli lodwa, kungabikho ucanda kulo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:11">34:11</a> Loba lilifa lengcwangube nokhwalimanzi, kuhlale kulo ifubesi nehlungulu, olule phezu kwalo ulutya lokulinganisa lwakwanyanyeni, nelothe yokulungelelanisa yakwalubala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:12">34:12</a> Abanumzana baloakuyi kuba sabakho babiza bukumkani kubo, bonke abathetheli balo babe yinto engekhoyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:13">34:13</a> Iingxande zalo ezinde ziya kumila into enameva, amarhawu namakhakakhaka ezinqabeni zalo ezinkulu, libe sisikhundla seempungutye nedlelo leenciniba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:14">34:14</a> Kohlangabezana amarhamncwa omqwebedu neempungutye, into elixhonti ikhawulelane nowayo; ewe, into yasebusuku iya konwaba khona, izifumanele ukuphumla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:15">34:15</a> Kulapho iya kwenzela khona indlu inyoka ejubayo, izale amaqanda, ifukame emthunzini khona; ewe, khona apho baya kubutha oontloyiya, elowo nowabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:16">34:16</a> Funani encwadini kaYehova, nilese. Akukho nanye kuzo ezo zinto iya kusala, eya kusilela kuwayo; ngokuba ngumlomo wam oziwisele umthetho, ngumoya wawo ozibuthileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:17">34:17</a> Nguye ozirholele iqashiso, isandla sakhe sazabela lona ngolutya lokulinganisa; ziya kulidla ilifa kudekuse ephakadeni,  zihlale kulo kwisizukulwana ngesizukulwana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:1">35:1</a> Inemihlali intlango nomqwebedu; iyagcoba inkqantosi,  iyadubula njengomfiyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:2">35:2</a> Iyatyatyamba, ithi rhoqo; iyagcoba, ewe, iyagcoba,  imemelele, inikwe ubuqaqawuli beLebhanon, ubungangamela beKarmele neSharon; ezo ndawo ziya kububona ubuqaqawuli bukaYehova, ubungangamela boThixo wethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:3">35:3</a> Yomelezani izandla eziwileyo, niwaqinise amadolo agexayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:4">35:4</a> Yithini kwabantliziyo zingxamayo, Yomelelani, ningoyiki.  Yabonani, uThixo wenu uyeza enempindezelo, enembuyekezo kaThixo; uya kuza yena anisindise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:5">35:5</a> Aya kuvulwa amehlo eemfama, zivulwe iindlebe zezithulu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:6">35:6</a> size sitsibe njengexhama isiqhwala, lumemelele ulwimi lwesidenge; ngokuba kuya kugqobhoka amanzi entlango, nemilambo enkqantosini;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:7">35:7</a> isanga sibe lidike, neendawo ezinxaniweyo zimpompoze amanzi. Esikhundleni sempungutye, apho ibuthuma khona, kuya kuba butyani neengcongolo nemikhanzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:8">35:8</a> Kuya kubakho umendo khona, kubekho indlela, kuthiwe ukubizwa kwayo, yindlela engcwele le. Akuyi kudlula nto iyinqambi ngayo; yeyabo yona: abahamba loo ndlela nabazizihula abayi kulahleka kuyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:9">35:9</a> Akuyi kubakho ngonyama khona, aliyi kuqabela khona irhamncwa eliqwengayo; aliyi kufunyanwa khona; kuya kuhamba khona abakhululwe ngokuhlawulelwa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:10">35:10</a> abakhululwa bakaYehova babuye beze eZiyon bememelela;  benovuyo olungunaphakade phezu kweentloko zabo; baya kufumana imihlali nemivuyo, sisabe isingqala nosizi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:1">36:1</a> Kwathi ngomnyaka weshumi elinesine wokumkani uHezekiya,  kwenyuka uSaneribhe ukumkani waseAsiriya, waya kuyo yonke imizi yakwaYuda enqatyisiweyo, wayithimba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:2">36:2</a> Ukumkani waseAsiriya wasusa uRabheshake eLakishe, ukuba aye eYerusalem kukumkani uHezekiya, enempi enzima. Wafika wema emjelweni wechibi lasentla, ongasemendweni wentsimi yomsuki weengubo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:3">36:3</a> Kwaphuma kwaya kuye uEliyakim unyana kaHilekiya, umphathi wendlu, noShebhena umbhali, noYowa unyana ka-Asafu, umkhumbuzi wezinto zakomkhulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:4">36:4</a> Wathi kubo uRabheshake, Khanithi kuHezekiya, Utsho ukumkani omkhulu, ukumkani waseAsiriya, ukuthi, Yeyani na le nkoloseko ukholose ngayo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:5">36:5</a> Ndithi mna, lilizwi lomlomo wodwa iqhinga lakho nobugorha bakho bemfazwe; okungoku ke ukholose ngabani na, ugwilike kum nje?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:6">36:6</a> Uyabona, ukholose ngaloo msimelelo wengcongolo evikivekileyo, iYiputa, ethi, othe wayama ngayo, ingene esandleni sakhe, imhlabe; unjalo uFaro ukumkani weYiputa kubo bonke abakholose ngaye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:7">36:7</a> Ke ukuba uthi kum, Sikholose ngoYehova uThixo wethu,  ndithi, Asinguye na lo uziganga nezibingelelo azisusileyo uHezekiya, wathi kumaYuda nakwiYerusalem, Ize niqubude phambi kwesi sibingelelo sodwa?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:8">36:8</a> Khawubekelane kaloku nenkosi yam, ukumkani waseAsiriya;  ndokunika amawaka amabini amahashe, ukuba unako ngecala lakho ukukhupha abakhweli bokukhwela kuwo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:9">36:9</a> Wothini na ukubujika ubuso benkosana enye, yakubo abancinane babakhonzi benkosi yam, ukholose ngeYiputa,  ngeenqwelo zokulwa nangabamahashe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:10">36:10</a> Ngokunje ndinyuke ndeza kulonakalisa eli lizwe, ndingenaye uYehova, yini na? UYehova uthe kum, Nyuka uye kweli lizwe,  ulonakalise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:11">36:11</a> Bathi ooEliyakim noShebhena noYowa kuRabheshake,  Khawuthethe kubakhonzi bakho ngesiAram, kuba sisiva sona; musa ukuthetha kuthi ngesiYuda ezindlebeni zabantu abaseludongeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:12">36:12</a> Wathi uRabheshake, Inkosi yam indithume ukuba ndiwathethe la mazwi enkosini yakho nakuwe, yini na? Asikula madoda ahleli eludongeni yini na, ukuze adle ilindle lawo, asele umchamo wawo nani?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:13">36:13</a> Wema uRabheshake, wadanduluka ngezwi elikhulu ngesiYuda,  wathi, Waveni amazwi okumkani omkhulu, okumkani waseAsiriya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:14">36:14</a> Uthi ukumkani, Makanganilukuhli uHezekiya, ngokuba akayi kuba nako ukunihlangula.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:15">36:15</a> Makanganikholosisi ngoYehova uHezekiya, esithi, Inene, uya kusihlangula uYehova; lo mzi awusayi kunikelwa esandleni sokumkani waseAsiriya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:16">36:16</a> Musani ukumphulaphula uHezekiya, ngokuba utsho ukumkani waseAsiriya ukuthi, Xolisanani nam, niphume nize kum, nidle elowo umdiliya wakhe, elowo umkhiwane wakhe, nisele elowo amanzi equla lakhe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:17">36:17</a> ndide ndize ndinise ezweni elinjengelizwe lenu, ilizwe lengqolowa newayini entsha, ilizwe lesonka nezidiliya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:18">36:18</a> Ize nilumke hleze aninyange uHezekiya, esithi, UYehova uya kusihlangula. Oothixo beentlanga balihlangule na elowo ilizwe lakhe esandleni sokumkani waseAsiriya?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:19">36:19</a> Baphi na oothixo baseHamati neArpadi? baphi na oothixo baseSefarvayim, ukuba bangabi balihlangule elakwaSamari esandleni sam?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:20">36:20</a> Nguwuphi na koothixo bonke bala mazwe olihlanguleyo ilizwe lakhe esandleni sam, ukuba ade uYehova ayihlangule iYerusalem esandleni sam?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:21">36:21</a> Bathi tu, abamphendula nazwi; ngokuba umthetho wokumkani wona ubusithi, Nize ningamphenduli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:22">36:22</a> Weza ke uEliyakim unyana kaHilekiya, umphathi wendlu,  noShebhena umbhali, noYowa unyana ka-Asafu, umkhumbuzi wezinto zakomkhulu, kuHezekiya, bezikrazule iingubo zabo, bamxelela amazwi kaRabheshake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:1">37:1</a> Kwathi, akukuva okukumkani uHezekiya, wazikrazula iingubo zakhe wazigquma ngezirhwexayo, wangena endlwini kaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:2">37:2</a> Wathuma uEliyakim umphathi wendlu, noShebhena umbhali,  namadoda amakhulu ababingeleli, bezigqume ngezirhwexayo,  kuIsaya umprofeti, unyana ka-Amotsi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:3">37:3</a> Bathi kuye, Utsho uHezekiya ukuthi, Le mini yimini yembandezelo neyokohlwaya neyogibo; ngokuba abantwana baze kufika emlonyeni wesizalo, tu ke amandla okuzala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:4">37:4</a> Mhlawumbi uYehova uThixo wakho angaweva amazwi kaRabheshake, othunyiweyo ngukumkani waseAsiriya inkosi yakhe,  ukungcikiva uThixo ophilileyo; amohlwaye ngenxa yamazwi lawo awavileyo uYehova uThixo wakho; wena uphakamise umthandazo ngenxa yamasalela asekhoyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:5">37:5</a> Baya ke abakhonzi bokumkani uHezekiya kuIsaya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:6">37:6</a> Wathi uIsaya kubo, Nothi kwinkosi yenu, Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Musa ukoyikiswa ngamazwi owavileyo, abandinyelise ngawo abafana bakwakumkani waseAsiriya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:7">37:7</a> Yabona, ndimfaka umoya, ukuba eve udaba olubi, abuye ke aye ezweni lakhe, ndimwise ngekrele ezweni lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:8">37:8</a> Wabuya ke uRabheshake, wamfumana ukumkani waseAsiriya esilwa neLibhena; ngokuba ebevile ukuba undulukile eLakishe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:9">37:9</a> Weva kusithiwa ngoTiraka ukumkani wakwaKushi, Uphumile esiza kulwa nawe. Weva ke, wathumela abathunywa kuHezekiya esithi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:10">37:10</a> Notsho kuHezekiya ukumkani wakwaYuda ukuthi,  Makangakulukuhli uThixo wakho, okholose ngaye wena, usithi,  Ayisayi kunikelwa iYerusalem esandleni sokumkani waseAsiriya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:11">37:11</a> Uyabona, ukuvile wena abakwenzileyo ookumkani baseAsiriya kumazwe onke, ukuba bawaphanzisa; uya kuhlangulwa na ke wena?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:12">37:12</a> Oothixo beentlanga ke bazihlangula na ezo,  bazitshabalalisayo oobawo, iGozan, neHaran, neRetsefe, noonyana bakaEden ababeseTelasare?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:13">37:13</a> Uphi na ukumkani weHamati, nokumkani weArpadi, nokumkani womzi waseSefarvayim, neHena, neIva?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:14">37:14</a> Wawathabatha uHezekiya amaphepha encwadi esandleni sabathunywa, wawafunda; wenyuka waya endlwini kaYehova,  wayaneka uHezekiya phambi koYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:15">37:15</a> Wathandaza uHezekiya kuYehova esithi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:16">37:16</a> Yehova wemikhosi, Thixo wakwaSirayeli, wena uhleli phakathi kweekerubhi, unguye uThixo wena wedwa kwizikumkani zonke zehlabathi; wena ulenzile izulu nehlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:17">37:17</a> Thoba indlebe yakho, Yehova, uve; vula amehlo akho,  Yehova, ubone; uweve onke amazwi kaSaneribhe, awathumele ukungcikiva uThixo ophilileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:18">37:18</a> Okunene, Yehova, ookumkani baseAsiriya baziphanzisile zonke iintlanga namazwe azo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:19">37:19</a> babanikela oothixo bazo emlilweni, kuba bebengethixo,  bebengumsebenzi wezandla zomntu, umthi nelitye;  babatshabalalisa ke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:20">37:20</a> Ke ngoko, Yehova Thixo wethu, sisindise esandleni sakhe,  zazi zonke izikumkani zehlabathi, ukuba wena unguYehova wedwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:21">37:21</a> Wathumela ke uIsaya unyana ka-Amotsi kuHezekiya, esithi,  Utsho uYehova, uThixo wakwaSirayeli, ukuthi, Okuthandazeleyo kum, ngokubhekisele kuSaneribhe ukumkani waseAsiriya,  ndikuvile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:22">37:22</a> Lilo eli ilizwi alithethayo uYehova ngaye, Intombi eyintombi uZiyon iyakudela, iyakugculela; intombi uYerusalem ihlunguzela intloko emva kwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:23">37:23</a> Ngubani na lo umngcikivileyo, umnyelisileyo? Ngubani na lo umphakamisele ilizwi lakho, ukude uwaphakamisele amehlo akho phezulu nje? NgoyiNgcwele wakwaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:24">37:24</a> Uyingcikivile iNkosi ngabakhonzi bakho, wathi, Ngobuninzi beenqwelo zam zokulwa ndiqabele mna ezintlomeni zeentaba,  emathambekeni eLebhanon; ndiyigawule imisedare yayo emide kakhulu nemisipres yayo enyuliweyo; ndifike kweyokuphela indawo yayo ephezulu, ehlathini lentsimi yayo echumayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:25">37:25</a> Ndimbe, ndasela amanzi mna; ndiya kuyomisa ngentende yeenyawo zam yonke imijelo yoMnayile oseYiputa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:26">37:26</a> Akuvanga na? Kwakude ndakwenza oku, kwangemihla yamandulo ndakubumba; ndikufikisile, kwenzeka ngoku ukuba uyikhahlele phantsi imizi enqatyisiweyo, ibe yingxakangxaka yemiwewe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:27">37:27</a> Abemi bayo banqumka izandla, baqhiphuka umbilini, badana,  baba ngumfuno wasendle, nohlaza, utyani obuphezu kwendlu,  nentsimi yengqolowa engekabi mvila.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:28">37:28</a> Ke ukuhlala kwakho, nokuphuma kwakho, nokungena kwakho,  ndiyakwazi, nokuguguma kwakho ngam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:29">37:29</a> Ngenxa yokuguguma kwakho ngam, nangenxa yokutyesha kwakho okunyuke kweza ezindlebeni zam, ndiya kufaka ikhonkco lam empumlweni yakho, nomkhala wam emlonyeni wakho, ndikubuyise ngendlela oweza ngayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:30">37:30</a> Ke kaloku nguwo lo umqondiso kuwe: lo mnyaka kodliwa ummilela, ngomnyaka wesibini kodliwa isihlabane; ngomnyaka wesithathu nohlwayela nivune, nityale izidiliya, nidle iziqhamo zazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:31">37:31</a> Abasindileyo bendlu yakwaYuda, abo baseleyo, baya kubuya bendelisele iingcambu phantsi, benze iziqhamo phezulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:32">37:32</a> Ngokuba kuya kuphuma eYerusalem abaseleyo nabasindileyo entabeni yeZiyon. Ubukhwele bukaYehova wemikhosi buya kukwenza oko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:33">37:33</a> Ngako oko utsho uYehova ngokubhekisele kukumkani waseAsiriya, ukuthi, Akayi kungena kulo mzi, akayi kutola notolo kuwo, akayi kuwuzela enengweletshetshe, akayi kuwufumbela ludonga lakungqinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:34">37:34</a> Uya kubuya ngendlela aweza ngayo; akasayi kungena kulo mzi; utsho uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:35">37:35</a> Ndiya kuwukhusela lo mzi, ndiwusindise ngenxa yam,  nangenxa kaDavide, umkhonzi wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:36">37:36</a> Kwaphuma ke isithunywa sikaYehova, saxabela emkhosini wama-Asiriya ikhulu elinamanci asibhozo anesihlanu amawaka.  Bavuka kusasa, nango ezizidumbu ezifileyo onke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:37">37:37</a> Wanduluka, wahamba; wabuya uSaneribhe ukumkani waseAsiriya, wahlala eNineve.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:38">37:38</a> Kwathi, enqula endlwini kaNiseroki uthixo wakhe, bamxabela ngekrele ooAdrameleki noSharetsere, oonyana bakhe. Baza basabela ezweni laseArarati. UEsar-hadon, unyana wakhe, waba ngukumkani esikhundleni sakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:1">38:1</a> Ngaloo mihla wayesifa UHezekiya, eza kufa. Waya umprofeti kuye, uIsaya unyana ka-Amotsi; wathi kuye, Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Yolela indlu yakho, ngokuba uya kufa wena, akuyi kuphila.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:2">38:2</a> UHezekiya wabubhekisa eludongeni ubuso bakhe, wathandaza kuYehova, wathi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:3">38:3</a> Khawukhumbule, ndiyakukhunga, Yehova, okokuba ndihambe phambi kwakho ngokunyaniseka nangentliziyo ephelelisileyo,  ndakwenza okulungileyo emehlweni akho. Watsho uHezekiya isililo esikhulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:4">38:4</a> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kuIsaya, lisithi,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:5">38:5</a> Yiya uthi kuHezekiya, Utsho uYehova, uThixo kaDavide uyihlo, ukuthi, Ndiwuvile umthandazo wakho, ndizibonile iinyembezi zakho. Uyabona, ndiya kongezelela kwimihla yakho ishumi elinesihlanu leminyaka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:6">38:6</a> Ndiya kukuhlangula wena nalo mzi esandleni sokumkani waseAsiriya, ndiwukhusele lo mzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:7">38:7</a> Nangu ke umqondiso kuwe, uphuma kuYehova, ukuba uya kulenza uYehova elo lizwi alithethileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:8">38:8</a> Uyabona, ndiyasibuyisa isithunzi sezinyuko, esehlayo esinyukweni sika-Ahazi ngelanga, ndisibuyisa umva izinyuko ezilishumi. Labuya ke ilanga izinyuko ezilishumi ezinyukweni elibe lihlile ngazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:9">38:9</a> Umbhalo kaHezekiya ukumkani wakwaYuda, oko ebesifa, waza waphila:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:10">38:10</a> Ndathi mna, yakubon ukuba ithe cwaka imihla yam, mandimke ndiye emasangweni elabafileyo; Ndivelelwe, ndayihluthwa eseleyo iminyaka yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:11">38:11</a> Ndathi, Andiyi kumbona uYa, uYa ezweni labaphilileyo;  Andiyi kuba samkhangela umntu, ndikubemi belabangasekhoyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:12">38:12</a> Umnquba wam uza kuncothulwa, ufuduswe umke kum,  njengentente yomalusi; Ndibusongile njengomluki ubomi bam;  unditsheca ezintsingeni. Uya kundigqibela ngosuku olunye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:13">38:13</a> Ndazizolisa kwada kwasa; njengengonyama, wenjenjalo ukuwaphula onke amathambo am. Uya kundigqibela ngosuku olunye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:14">38:14</a> Njengehlankomo, njengendwe, ndenjenjalo ukukrikriza,  Ndalila njengevukuthu; aphela amehlo am kukubheka phezulu:  Yehova, ndifingekile, ndimele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:15">38:15</a> Ndothini na ukubulela, ethethile nje kum, wenza nokwenza?  Mandicothoze yonke iminyaka yam eya kuza phezu kobukrakra bomphefumlo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:16">38:16</a> Nkosi yam, babuya baphile zezo zinto abantu, Bukuzo kanye ubomi bomoya wam: Wondiphilisa ke, ndidlise ubomi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:17">38:17</a> Yabona, baba lusindiso kum ubukrakra obukhulu. Wena ke ngokundithanda, wawurhola umphefumlo wam esihogweni sokonakala;  Ngokuba izono zam uzilahlile emva komhlana wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:18">38:18</a> Kuba elabafileyo alinakukuncoma, ukufa akunakukudumisa;  Abahla baye emhadini abakulindele ukunyanisa kwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:19">38:19</a> Ophilileyo, ophilileyo nguye owokuncoma, njengam nje namhla. Uyise uya kukwazisa ukunyanisa kwakho koonyana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:20">38:20</a> UYehova uza kundisindisa; Ngoko ke sozibetha iihadi zethu Yonke imihla yobomi bethu, endlwini kaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:21">38:21</a> Wathi uIsaya, mabathabathe isicumba samakhiwane, basibeke ethumbeni, ukuze aphile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:22">38:22</a> Wathi uHezekiya, Uyintoni na umqondiso wokuba ndiya kunyuka ndiye endlwini kaYehova?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:1">39:1</a> Ngelo xesha uMerodaki-bhaladan, unyana kaBhaladan, ukumkani waseBhabheli, wathumela incwadi nomnikelo kuHezekiya; kuba wayevile ukuba ubesifa, wabuya wachacha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:2">39:2</a> Wavuya uHezekiya ngabo, wababonisa indlu yakhe yezinto aziqwebileyo: isilivere, negolide, nobulawu, neoli entle,  nendlu yonke yezixhobo zakhe, nento yonke ebikho ebuncwaneni bakhe. Akwabakho nto endlwini yakhe nasekulawuleni kwakhe konke, angababonisanga yona uHezekiya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:3">39:3</a> Waya uIsaya umprofeti kukumkani uHezekiya, wathi kuye,  Atheni na la madoda? avele ngaphi na ukuza kuwe? Wathi uHezekiya, Avele ezweni elikude eBhabheli, esiza kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:4">39:4</a> Wathi ke, Abone ntoni na endlwini yakho? Wathi uHezekiya,  Abone into yonke esendlwini yam; akubangakho nto ndingababonisanga yona ebuncwaneni bam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:5">39:5</a> Wathi uIsaya kuHezekiya, Live ke ilizwi likaYehova wemikhosi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:6">39:6</a> Uyabona, kuza imihla, eya kuthi yonke into esendlwini yakho, nento abayiqwebayo ooyihlo, kwada kwayile mini,  ithwalelwe eBhabheli, kungasali nto; utsho uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:7">39:7</a> Baya kuthabatha nakoonyana bakho abaya kuphuma kuwe, oya kubazala, babe ngababusi ebhotweni lokumkani waseBhabheli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:8">39:8</a> Wathi uHezekiya kuIsaya, Lilungile ilizwi likaYehova,  olithethileyo. Wathi, Inene, kuya kubakho uxolo nozingiso ngeyam imihla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:1">40:1</a> Thuthuzelani, bathuthuzeleni abantu bam, utsho uThixo wenu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:2">40:2</a> Thethani kakuhle neYerusalem, nimemeze kuyo, nithi kuzalisekile ukuphuma kwayo umkhosi; nithi, buhlawulelwe ubugwenxa bayo; nithi, yamkeliswe esandleni sikaYehova okuphindwe kabini kwizono zayo zonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:3">40:3</a> Yivani omemezayo, esithi, Yigeceni entlango indlela kaYehova; tyenenezelani uThixo wethu umendo enkqantosini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:4">40:4</a> Yonke imifula mayinyuswe, zonke iintaba neenduli zigungxulwe; iindawo ezimagqagala zibe zithabazi, nemixawuka ibe ziintili;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:5">40:5</a> butyhileke ubuqaqawuli bukaYehova, ibubone inyama yonke kunye; ngokuba uthethile umlomo kaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:6">40:6</a> Ilizwi lothile lathi, Memeza. Wathi yena, Ndimemeze ntoni na? Yithi, Yonke inyama ibutyani, bonke ubuhle bayo bunjengentyantyambo yasendle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:7">40:7</a> Buyoma utyani, iyabuna intyantyambo; ngokuba umoya kaYehova uvuthuza kuyo; inene, abantu babutyani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:8">40:8</a> Buyoma utyani, iyabuna intyantyambo; ke lona ilizwi likaThixo wethu liya kuma ngonaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:9">40:9</a> Wena Ziyon, mshumayeli weendaba ezilungileyo, nyuka uye entabeni ephakamileyo; wena Yerusalem, mshumayeli weendaba ezilungileyo, liphakamise ngamandla ilizwi lakho, phakamisa ungoyiki. Yithi kwimizi yakwaYuda, Nanko uThixo wenu!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:10">40:10</a> Uyabona, iNkosi uYehova iya kuza, ingowomeleleyo, ingalo yayo iyilawulela. Uyabona, umvuzo wayo inawo, nomsebenzi wayo uphambi kwayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:11">40:11</a> Iya kuwalusa umhlambi wayo njengomalusi; iya kuwabutha ngeengalo zayo amatakane, iwathwale ngesifuba sayo, izithundeze ezanyisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:12">40:12</a> Ngubani na olinganise amanzi la entendeni yesandla sakhe,  walilungisa izulu ngomoluko weminwe, walukhongozela uthuli lomhlaba ngomlinganiselo, wazilinganisa iintaba ngesilinganiso,  neenduli ngesikali?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:13">40:13</a> Ngubani na owalungisa uMoya kaYehova, waba yindoda emcebisayo, wamazisa?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:14">40:14</a> Wacebisana nabani na owamqondisayo, wamfundisa umendo wesiko, wamfundisa ukwazi, wamazisa indlela yokuqonda?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:15">40:15</a> Yabona, iintlanga zibalelwa ekubeni zinjengethontsi emphandeni, njengesuntswana esikalini. Yabona, iziqithi zinjengothuli oluqhaphukayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:16">40:16</a> ILebhanon ayilingene kubaswa, neenyamakazi zayo azilingene kubalidini elinyukayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:17">40:17</a> Zonke iintlanga zinjengento engento phambi kwakhe; kuye zibalelwa ekuthini asizanto, ziluchuku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:18">40:18</a> Ningamfanekisa ke nabani na uThixo, ninxulumise mfanekiselo mni na naye?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:19">40:19</a> Umfanekiso oqingqiweyo utyhidwa yingcibi, awaleke ngegolide umnyibilikisi, awunyibilikisele imixokelelwane yesilivere.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:20">40:20</a> Okhohliweyo ngumrhumo ukhetha umthi ongenakubola;  uzifunela ingcibi eyaziyo, ukuba imlungisele umfanekiso oqingqiweyo ongayi kushukuma.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:21">40:21</a> Anazi na? aniva na? anixelelwanga na kwasentloko?  aniqondanga na kwasekusekweni kwehlabathi?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:22">40:22</a> Ngulo uhlala phezu kwesazinge sehlabathi, abemi balo ke benjengemicikwane; ulowaneka izulu njengeqhiya eliyasuyasu,  walitwabulula njengentente yokuhlala;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:23">40:23</a> ulozenza izidwangube ukuba zingabi nto, abagwebi behlabathi abenze babe luchuku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:24">40:24</a> Bengekathi ukutyalwa, bengekathi ukuhlwayelwa, singekathi ukwendelisela iingcambu emhlabeni isiphunzi sabo,  uselebafuthela bome, ubathabathe umoya ovuthuzayo njengomququ.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:25">40:25</a> Niya kundifanisa nabani na, ndilingane naye? utsho oyiNgcwele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:26">40:26</a> Phakamiselani amehlo enu phezulu, nibone: ngubani na owadala ezi zinto? Ngulokhupha umkhosi wazo ngamaqela, uzibiza zonke ziphela ngamagama, ngenxa yobukhu bokomelela, ekhaliphile ngamandla; akusali nanye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:27">40:27</a> Yini na ukuba uthi, Yakobiuthethe uthi, Sirayeli Indlela yam isithele kuYehova, nebango lam lidlule kuThixo wam?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:28">40:28</a> Akwazi na? akuvanga na, ukuba uThixo ongunaphakade nguYehova, tyhafi, akadinwa; ayinakugocwagocwa ingqondo yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:29">40:29</a> Umnika otyhafileyo amandla, ongenakomelela amandisele ukuqina.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:30">40:30</a> Namadodana angatyhafa adinwe, nabafana bakhubeke bawe;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:31">40:31</a> ke bona abathembele kuYehova baya kuhlaziyeka emandleni;  banyuke ngamaphiko njengeenkozi. Baya kugidima bangadinwa,  bahambe bangatyhafi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:1">41:1</a> Yithini tu phambi kwam, ziqithi; izizwe mazihlaziye amandla; mazize zisondele, zandule zithethe; masiqubisane ematyaleni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:2">41:2</a> Ngubani na ovuse empumalanga lowo ukhawulelwa bubulungisa ezinyaweni zakhe? Unikela iintlanga phambi kwakhe, unyathela ookumkani, ubanikela ekreleni lakhe njengothuli, esaphetheni sakhe njengomququ ophetshethwayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:3">41:3</a> Uyabasukela, udlula enoxolo ngomendo abengawuhambanga ngeenyawo zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:4">41:4</a> Ngubani na okusebenzileyo wakwenza oko, obiza izizukulwana kwasentloko? Ndim, mna Yehova, ndingowokuqala; nakwabangasemva ndikwanguye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:5">41:5</a> Iziqithi zabona zoyika, iziphelo zehlabathi zagubha,  zasondela, zeza.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:6">41:6</a> Umntu wamnceda ummelwane wakhe, wathi kumzalwana wakhe,  Yomelela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:7">41:7</a> Ingcibi yomeleza umnyibilikisi; ogudisayo ngesando womeleza obetha esikhandelweni, esithi, Kulungile; wasiqinisa ngezikhonkwane, ukuba singashukumi isithixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:8">41:8</a> Ke wena Sirayeli, mkhonzi wam Yakobi, wena ndakunyulayo,  mbewu ka-Abraham umthandi wam;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:9">41:9</a> endakubambayo kwaseziphelweni zehlabathi, endakubizayo kwasemacaleni alo; endathi kuwe, Ungumkhonzi wam wena,  ndikunyule, andikucekisile;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:10">41:10</a> musa ukoyika, kuba ndinawe mna; musa ukubhekabheka, kuba ndinguThixo wakho; ndikukhaliphisile, ewe, ndikuncedile,  ndikuxhasile ngesandla sam sokunene sobulungisa bam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:11">41:11</a> Yabona, baya kudana bahlazeke bonke abavutha umsindo ngawe; aya kuba yinto engento, adake amadoda abambana nawe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:12">41:12</a> Uya kuwafuna, ungawafumani, amadoda aphikisana nawe; aya kuba yinto engento, engekhoyo, amadoda alwa nawe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:13">41:13</a> Ngokuba mna, Yehova Thixo wakho, ndiya kusibamba isandla sakho sokunene; ndingothi kuwe, Musa ukoyika, ndiya kukunceda mna.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:14">41:14</a> Musa ukoyika, mbungu Yakobi, bantu bambalwa bakwaSirayeli;  ndiya kukunceda mna; utsho uYehova, uMkhululi wakho oyiNgcwele kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:15">41:15</a> Yabona, ndikwenze isisizilo esibukhali esitsha,  esintlangothi mbini; uya kuzi bhula iintaba uzicole, iinduli uzixelise umququ.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:16">41:16</a> Uya kuzela, umoya uzitha bathe, umoya ovuthuzayo uziphangalalise; ke wena ugcobe ngoYehova, uqhayise ngoyiNgcwele kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:17">41:17</a> Ke abaziintsizana nabangamahlwempu baya kufuna amanzi,  angabikho, ulwimi lwabo lome linxano; mna Yehova ndiya kubaphendula; mna, Thixo kaSirayeli, andiyi kubashiya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:18">41:18</a> Ndiya kuyivula imilambo eluqayini, nemithombo phakathi kweentili, ndenze intlango ibe lidike elinamanzi, nomhlaba ongumqwebedu ube ziindawo eziphuma amanzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:19">41:19</a> Ndiya kutyala entlango imisedare, nemingampunzi,  nemimirtile, neminquma yasendle, ndimise enkqantosini imisipres, nemipleyini, nemigalagala, ndawonye;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:20">41:20</a> ukuze babone, bazi, bagqale ngentliziyo, baqiqe kunye,  ukuba isandla sikaYehova sikwenzile oko, oyiNgcwele kaSirayeli ukudalile oko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:21">41:21</a> Sondezani iindawo enibambene ngazo, utsho uYehova;  zimiseni iziganeko zenu, utsho uKumkani kaYakobi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:22">41:22</a> Mabazizise, basixelele okuza kuhla; mabaxele izinto zangaphambili, ubunjani bazo, sizigqale ngeentliziyo, silazi ikamva lazo; nokuba zezizayo siviseni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:23">41:23</a> Xelani izinto ezizayo ngasemva, ukuze sazi ukuba ningoothixo; ewe, yenzani okulungileyo, nokuba kokubi,  sikhwankqiswe, sibonisane ngako.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:24">41:24</a> Yabonani, ningabento engento, nomsebenzi wenu awuni yani;  ulisikizi oninyulayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:25">41:25</a> Ndivuse owasentla, weza; owasempumalanga, onqula igama lam; uzifikela iirhuluneli njengodaka, njengombumbi exovula udongwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:26">41:26</a> Ngubani na owakuxelayo oko kwasekuqaleni? makavele sazi;  owakuxelayo ngenxa engaphambili makavele, sithi, Ulungisile.  Hayi, akukho waxelayo; hayi, akukho wavakalisayo; hayi, akukho wazivayo iintetho zenu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:27">41:27</a> Ndim endaqala ndathi kwiZiyon, Yabona, nanzo; ndayinika iYerusalem umshumayeli weendaba ezilungileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:28">41:28</a> Kuba ndakhangela, akwabakho bani; nakwaba akwabakho bacebisi ndingababuzayo, baphendule ngelizwi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:29">41:29</a> Yabona, bonke bephela bayinto engento, ziyinto engekhoyo izenzo zabo, imifanekiso yabo etyhidiweyo ingumoya nochuku.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:1">42:1</a> Mboneni ke umkhonzi wam endimxhasayo; umnyulwa wam, okholwa nguye umphefumlo wam. Ndibeke uMoya wam phezu kwakhe; uya kukuphumelelisa okusesikweni ezintlangeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:2">42:2</a> Akayi kunkqangaza, aliphakamise, alivakalise ezitratweni ilizwi lakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:3">42:3</a> Ingcongolo evikivekileyo akayi kuyaphula, umsonto oqhumayo akayi kuwucima; uya kukuphumelelisa okusesikweni ngokwenyaniso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:4">42:4</a> Akayi kuba nakucinywa, akayi kuvikiveka, ade akumise okusesikweni ehlabathini, zilindele isiyalo sakhe iziqithi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:5">42:5</a> Utsho uThixo yena, uYehova, udala izulu, alaneke;  utwabulula umhlaba neziveliso zawo; unika abantu abaphezu kwawo ukuphefumla, unika abahamba kuwo umoya:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:6">42:6</a> ukuthi, Mna, Yehova, ndikubizile ngokobulungisa, ndakubamba ngesandla; ndiya kukulondoloza, ndikwenze umnqophiso wabantu,  isikhanyiselo seentlanga;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:7">42:7</a> ukuba uvule amehlo eemfama, ukuba ukhuphe abakhonkxiweyo ekuvalelweni, abahleli ebumnyameni ubakhuphe entolongweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:8">42:8</a> NdinguYehova, lilo elo igama lam; andiluniki omnye uzuko lwam, nendumiso yam andiyiniki imifanekiso eqingqiweyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:9">42:9</a> Izinto zokuqala, yabona, zifikile; ndixela izinto ezintsha,  ke zingekantshuli ndiyanivisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:10">42:10</a> Vumani kuYehova ingoma entsha, indumiso yakhe kwaseziphelweni zehlabathi, nina bahla baye elwandle,  nenzaliseko yalo, nina ziqhithi nabemi bazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:11">42:11</a> Mayiphakamise izwi intlango, nemizi yayo, nemizana ehleli amaKedare; mabamemelele abemi bengxondorha, batsholoze ezincotsheni zeentaba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:12">42:12</a> Mabamzukise uYehova, baxele indumiso yakhe eziqithini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:13">42:13</a> UYehova uya kuphuma njengegorha, uya kuxhoxha ikhwele njengendoda yokulwa; uya kuduma, ewe, uya kunkqangaza; uya kuba ligorha ezintshabeni zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:14">42:14</a> Kususela kwakude ndithe quthu, ndathi tu, ndazibamba;  ngoku ndiya kubefuza njengozalayo, ndibe nephika, ndifuthe nokufutha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:15">42:15</a> Ndobharhisa iintaba neenduli, ndiyitshise yonke imifuno yazo, imilambo ndiyenze iziqithi, ndiwatshise amadike.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:16">42:16</a> Ndozihambisa iimfama ngendlela ezingayaziyo,  ndizinyathelise kwiingqushu ezingazaziyo; ubumnyama ndibenza ukukhanya phambi kwazo, iindawo ezimagqagala zibe zithabazi.  Zizo ezo izinto endiya kuzenza, ndingazishiyi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:17">42:17</a> Baya kubuya umva, badane bedanile, abakholosa ngemifanekiso eqingqiweyo, abathi kwetyhidiweyo, Ningoothixo bethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:18">42:18</a> Yivani, zithulu; bhekani nibone, zimfama.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:19">42:19</a> Ngubani na oyimfama, ingenguye umkhonzi wam? osisithulu njengomthunywa wam endimthumayo? Ngubani na oyimfama njengenqogu, oyimfama njengomkhonzi kaYehova?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:20">42:20</a> Ubona izinto ezininzi, akazigcini noko; uvula iindlebe,  akeva noko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:21">42:21</a> UYehova uthande ngenxa yobulungisa bakhe ukuwukhulisa umyalo, wawenza wanobungangamsha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:22">42:22</a> Ke bona ngabantu abaphangiweyo, abahluthiweyo,  ababotshelelwe emingxunyeni bonke bephela, abafakwe ezintolongweni, baba lixhoba, akwabakho mhlanguli; baba ngabahluthiweyo, akwabakho uthi, Buyisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:23">42:23</a> Ngubani na kuni oya kukubekela indlebe oko, abaze indlebe,  eve emveni koku?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:24">42:24</a> Ngubani na owamnikela uYakobi ekuhluthweni, owamnikela uSirayeli kubaphangi? AsinguYehova nalowo sonayo kuye, lowo bangavumanga ukuhamba ngeendlela zakhe, abawuphulaphula umyalo wakhe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:25">42:25</a> Wamphalazela ngobushushu bomsindo wakhe, nangamandla emfazwe; wamlenya ngomlilo ngeenxa zonke, akakwazi noko;  wamtshisa, noko akakunyamekela oko ngentliziyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:1">43:1</a> Kaloku ke utsho uYehova, uMdali wakho, Yakobi, uMbumbi wakho, Sirayeli, ukuthi, Musa ukoyika; ngokuba ndikukhulule ngokukuhlawulela; ndikubizile ngegama lakho, ungowam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:2">43:2</a> Xa uthi uwele emanzini, ndoba nawe: nasemilanjeni, ayisayi kukuntywilisela; xa uthi uhambe emlilweni, akuyi kurhawuka,  nelangatye lingakutshisi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:3">43:3</a> Ngokuba mna, Yehova, ndinguThixo wakho, mna, Ngcwele kaSirayeli, ndingumsindisi wakho; ndirhole iYiputa yakucamagushela, iKushi neSebha zaba sesikhundleni sakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:4">43:4</a> Ngenxa yokuba unqabile emehlweni am, uzukile, mna ke ndikuthandile; ndirhola abantu esikhundleni sakho, nezizwe esikhundleni sobomi bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:5">43:5</a> Musa ukoyika, ngokuba ndinawe: ndiya kuyizisa imbewu yakho ivela empumalanga, ndikubuthe nasentshonalanga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:6">43:6</a> Ndiya kuthi kumntla, Ethe; nakumzantsi, Musa ukuthintela;  nazise oonyana bam bevela kude, neentombi zam zivela eziphelweni zehlabathi:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:7">43:7</a> yonke into ebizwe ngegama lam, endiyidalele uzuko lwam,  endiyibumbileyo, endiyenzileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:8">43:8</a> Khupha abantu abaziimfama benamehlo, nabazizithulu beneendlebe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:9">43:9</a> Nonke zintlanga, buthelanani ndawonye, zihlangane izizwe.  Ngubani na kuni onokukuxela oko? Mabasivise izinto zangaphambili, mabamise amangqina abo, bagwetyelwe; mabeve ke abantu, bathi, Yinyaniso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:10">43:10</a> Ningamangqina am, utsho uYehova, nina ningumkhonzi wam endimnyulileyo; ukuze nazi, nikholwe ndim, niqonde ukuba ndim;  phambi kwam akubunjwanga thixo, nasemva kwam akuyi kubakho namnye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:11">43:11</a> Mna ke, mna ndinguYehova, akukho msindisi ingendim.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:12">43:12</a> Mna ndixelile, ndasindisa, ndabonisa, kungekho thixo wumbi kuni; ningamangqina am, utsho uYehova, ukuba ndinguThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:13">43:13</a> Unanamhla ndinguye, akukho unokuhlangula esandleni sam;  ndisebenza, ngubani na ke onokukubuyisa oko umva?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:14">43:14</a> Utsho uYehova, umkhululi wenu, oyiNgcwele kaSirayeli,  ukuthi, Ngenxa yenu ndithumele eBhabheli, ukuba ndibahlise abasabayo bonke bephela, namaKaledi, ngeenqanawa zokumemelela kwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:15">43:15</a> Mna, Yehova, ndingoyiNgcwele wenu, uMdali kaSirayeli,  uKumkani wenu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:16">43:16</a> Utsho uYehova, umenzi wendlela elwandle, womendo emanzini anamandla;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:17">43:17</a> umkhuphi wenqwelo nehashe, wempi nentshatshela; baya kulala bangavuki, bethile, becimile njengomsonto wesibane:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:18">43:18</a> utsho ukuthi, Musani ukukhumbula izinto zangaphambili,  ningazikhathaleli nezamandulo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:19">43:19</a> Yabonani, ndiya kwenza into entsha, intshule ngoku; aniyi kuyazi na? Inene, ndiya kwenza indlela entlango, nemilambo enkangala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:20">43:20</a> Izilo zasendle ziya kundizukisa, iimpungutye neenciniba;  ngokuba ndenza amanzi entlango, nemilambo enkangala, ukuze ndiseze abantu bam, abanyulwa bam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:21">43:21</a> Abantu endizibumbeleyo baya kubalisa indumiso yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:22">43:22</a> Akundinqulanga ke mna, Yakobi, ngokude uzixhamle ngam,  Sirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:23">43:23</a> Akundiziselanga mpahla imfutshane yamadini akho anyukayo;  akundizukisanga ngamibingelelo yakho. Andikukhonzisanga ngaminikelo yakudla, andikudinisanga ngantlaka imhlophe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:24">43:24</a> Akundithengelanga kalamo ngemali, akundihluthisanga ngamanqatha emibingelelo yakho; hayi, undikhonzise ngezono zakho, undidinisile ngobugwenxa bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:25">43:25</a> Mna ndinguye ocima izikreqo zakho ngenxa yam,  ndingazikhumbuli izono zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:26">43:26</a> Ndikhumbuze, masimangalelane; misa intetho yakho, ukuze ugwetyelwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:27">43:27</a> Uyihlo wokuqala wona, nabalamleli bakho bakreqa kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:28">43:28</a> Ngako oko ndabangcolisa ke abathetheli abangcwele,  ndamnikela uYakobi ukuba asingelwe phantsi, uSirayeli ukuba anyeliswe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:1">44:1</a> Kaloku ke yiva, Yakobi mkhonzi wam, Sirayeli endikunyulileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:2">44:2</a> Utsho uYehova uMenzi wakho, uMbumbi wakho kwasesizalweni,  uMncedi wakho, ukuthi, Musa ukoyika, mkhonzi wam Yakobi,  Yeshurun endimnyulileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:3">44:3</a> Ngokuba ndiya kugalela amanzi phezu kwabanxaniweyo,  nemiqukuqela yamanzi phezu kwelizwe elomileyo. Ndiya kugalela uMoya wam phezu kwembewu yakho, nentsikelelo yam phezu kwenzala yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:4">44:4</a> Baya kuhluma phakathi kotyani, njengemingculuba engasemisingeni yamanzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:5">44:5</a> Omnye uya kuthi, NdingokaYehova; nomnye uya kunqula igama likaYakobi; kwanomnye uya kuzibhala ngesandla sakhe kuYehova,  alihloniphe igama likaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:6">44:6</a> Utsho uYehova, uKumkani wakwaSirayeli, uMkhululi wakhe,  uYehova wemikhosi, ukuthi, Ndingowokuqala, ndingowokugqibela;  akukho Thixo ingendim.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:7">44:7</a> Ngubani na oshumayela njengam-makaxele andicacisele-ethabathela ekumiseni kwam abantu basendaleni?  Izinto ezizayo, neziza kubakho, mabazixele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:8">44:8</a> Musani ukunkwantya, ningajijitheki; andikuvisanga na kwanini, ndanixelela? Ningamangqina am. Kukho Thixo na,  ingendim? Akukho liwa, andilazi mna.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:9">44:9</a> Abayili bemifanekiso eqingqiweyo bonke bephela baluchuku,  neento zabo ezinqwenelekayo azincedi nto; bona bangamangqina azo; ababoni, abazi, ukuze badane.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:10">44:10</a> Ngubani na oyile uthixo, watyhida umfanekiso ongenakunceda nto?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:11">44:11</a> Yabona, onke amadlelane awo aya kudana, neengcibi ezo zezasebantwini; mababuthelane bonke bephela, beme, bankwantye,  badane kunye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:12">44:12</a> Ingcibi yesinyithi ilola inkxola, isebenza ngamalahle avuthayo, isiyila isithixo ngezando, isibenza ngengalo yayo enamandla; kanjalo iyalamba, ingabi namandla; ayiseli manzi,  ityhafe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:13">44:13</a> Ingcibi yemithi yolula ulutya lokulinganisa, isibabula isiqu saso ngechitywa; isilungisa ngezinto zokuchwela;  isibabula isiqu saso ngekompas, isenze ngemfano yendoda,  ngokobuhle bomntu, ukuba sihlale endlwini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:14">44:14</a> Ugawula imisedare, uthabatha umholem nomoki, akhethe emithini yehlathi; utyala umpayine, imvula iwukhulise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:15">44:15</a> Woba ke yinto yokuba umntu aphembe umlilo; athabathe kuwo,  othe; uphatha kuthi abase umlilo, ose isonka; uphatha kuthi enze uthixo, aqubude kuye, enze umfanekiso oqingqiweyo,  asibekeke kuwo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:16">44:16</a> Inxalenye yawo uyitshisa emlilweni; inxalenye yawo uyidla inyama ngayo; wosa ose ahluthe; ewe, uyotha, athi, Hee ke!  ndiyotha, ndiva umlilo!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:17">44:17</a> Oseleyo kuwo uwenza uthixo, umfanekiso wakhe oqingqiweyo,  asibekeke kuwo, aqubude kuwo, athandaze kuwo, athi,  Ndihlangule; ngokuba, unguthixo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:18">44:18</a> Ahazi, abaqondi; ngokuba avingciwe amehlo abo ukuba angaboni, ukuba iintliziyo zabo zingaqiqi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:19">44:19</a> banganyamekeli ngeentliziyo zabo, kungabikho kwazi,  kungabikho kuqonda, ukuba bathi, Inxalenye yawo ndiyitshisile emlilweni; ewe, ndosa isonka emalahleni awo; ndosa inyama,  ndadla; oseleyo kuwo ndiya kuwenza amasikizi na? ndisibekeke na kwinto evele emthini?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:20">44:20</a> Esukelana nothuthu nje, intliziyo edetshiselweyo imtyekisile kangangokuba angawuhlanguli umphefumlo wakhe, athi,  Akukho buxoki na esandleni sam sokunene?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:21">44:21</a> Khumbula ezo zinto, Yakobi, Sirayeli, ngokuba ungumkhonzi wam; ndikubumbile, ungumkhonzi kum; Sirayeli, akuyi kulityalwa ndim.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:22">44:22</a> Ndilucimile njengelifu elingqingqwa ukreqo lwakho, nezono zakho njengelifu elisibekeleyo; buyela kum, ngokuba ndikukhulule ngokukuhlawulela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:23">44:23</a> Memelelani, mazulu, ngokuba uYehova ekwenzile; dumani,  zinzulu zehlabathi; gqabhukani nimemelele, zintaba, hlathi,  nani nonke mithi ekulo; ngokuba uYehova emhlawulele wamkhulula uYakobi, ezihombisile ngoSirayeli..</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:24">44:24</a> Utsho uYehova, uMkhululi wakho, uMbumbi wakho kwasesizalweni, ukuthi, Mna Yehova ndinguMenzi weento zonke;  uManeki wezulu ndedwa; uMtwabululi wehlabathi ndingenabani;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:25">44:25</a> uMtshitshisi wemiqondiso yabaphololoza into engeyiyo;  uMgezisi wabavumisayo; uMbuyisi wezilumko umva; uMzulisi wokwazi kwazo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:26">44:26</a> uMmisi welizwi lomkhonzi wakhe; uMzalisi wecebo labathunywa bakhe; uNdithi kwiYerusalem, Iya kumiwa; nakwimizi yakwaYuda, Iya kwakhiwa, ndiwamise amanxuwa ayo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:27">44:27</a> uNdithi kumanzi enzonzobila, Yitshani, ndiyomise imilambo yakho;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:28">44:28</a> uNdithi kuKoreshi, Ngumalusi wam, oya kukuzalisa konke ukuthanda kwam; athi kwiYerusalem, Mayakhiwe; nakwitempile,  Mayisekwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:1">45:1</a> Utsho uYehova kumthanjiswa wakhe, kuKoreshi, endimbambe ngesandla sokunene, ukuba ndizinyathele iintlanga phambi kwakhe; ndikhulule amanqe ookumkani, ukuba ndizivule iingcango ezingambini, namasango angabi nakuvalwa:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:2">45:2</a> ukuthi, Ndiya kuhamba phambi kwakho, ndilungelelanise iindawo ezimaqhubu, ndiqhekeze iingcango zobhedu, ndixakaxe nemivalo yesinyithi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:3">45:3</a> ndikunike ubuncwane obusemnyameni, neengqwebo ezisezintsithelweni; ukuze wazi, ukuba mna Yehova ndingulo ukubize ngegama, uThixo kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:4">45:4</a> Ngenxa yomkhonzi wam uYakobi, uSirayeli umnyulwa wam,  ndakubiza ngegama lakho, ndakuthiya namanye amagama, ungandazi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:5">45:5</a> NdinguYehova; akukho wumbi, akukho Thixo ingendim.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:6">45:6</a> Ndakubhinqa ungandazi, ukuze bazi, bethabathela ekuphumeni kwelanga bese nasekutshoneni kwalo, ukuba akukho namnye ingendim; ndinguYehova, akukho wumbi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:7">45:7</a> NdinguMenzi wokukhanya, uMdali wobumnyama, uMenzi woxolo,  uMdali wobubi: mna Yehova ndinguMenzi wezo zinto zonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:8">45:8</a> Vuzisani, mazulu phezulu, sikhumezele ubulungisa isibhakabhaka; mawuvuleke umhlaba, uqhame usindiso, uhlumise ubulungisa kunye: mna Yehova ndikudalile oko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:9">45:9</a> Yeha ke, obambana noMenzi wakhe! Ligophe emagopheni ezitya zomdongwe! Udongwe lunokuthi na kumbumbi walo, Wenza ntoni na?  nomsebenzi wakho unokuthi na, Akunazandla?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:10">45:10</a> Yeha ke, othi kuyise, Uzaleleni na? nakumfazi, Unanimba ngani na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:11">45:11</a> Utsho uYehova, oyiNgcwele kaSirayeli, uMenzi wakhe,  ukuthi, buzani kum izinto ezizayo; oonyana bam nomsebenzi wezandla zam wuyalezeni kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:12">45:12</a> Mna ndenza ihlabathi, ndadala abantu phezu kwalo; izandla zam, mna lo zaneka izulu, nomkhosi walo wonke ndawuwisela umthetho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:13">45:13</a> Mna ndimvelisile ngobulungisa, ndiya kuzilungelelanisa iindlela zakhe zonke. Yena uya kuwakha umzi wam, abakhulule abafuduswa bam, kungarholwanga nani, kungarholwanga sicengo;  utsho uYehova wemikhosi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:14">45:14</a> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Ukuxelenga kweYiputa nokurhweba kukaKushi nokwamaSebha, abafo abanewonga, kuya kuwelela kuwe kube kokwakho. Baya kuhamba emva kwakho, baya kuwela benemixokelelwane, baqubude kuwe; baya kuthandaza kuwe,  besithi, Inene, ukuwe uThixo; akusekho thixo, akukho nokuba abe mnye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:15">45:15</a> Inyaniso, unguThixo ozisithelisayo, Thixo kaSirayeli,  Msindisi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:16">45:16</a> Baya kudana, kananjalo bahlazeke bonke bephela; baya kuhamba behlazekile kunye abaziingcibi zezithixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:17">45:17</a> USirayeli uya kusindiswa nguYehova ngosindiso olungunaphakade; aniyi kudaniswa, aniyi kuhlazeka, kude kuse emaphakadeni asephakadeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:18">45:18</a> Ngokuba utsho uYehova, uMdali wezulu (nguye uThixo),  uMenzi wehlabathi, uMseki walo, yena walizinzisayo (akalidalelanga ukuba kube senyanyeni, walibumba ukuba limiwe),  ukuthi, NdinguYehova, akukho wumbi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:19">45:19</a> Andithethanga entsithelweni, endaweni emnyama yelizwe;  anditshongo embewini kaYakobi ukuthi, Ndiquqeleni enyanyeni.  Mna Yehova ndithetha ubulungisa, ndixela into ethe tye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:20">45:20</a> Buthani nize, sondelani kunye, nina basindileyo basezintlangeni: abanakwazi abathwali bomthi womfanekiso wabo oqinqiweyo, abathandazi bothixo ongasindisiyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:21">45:21</a> Xelani, nifikise; ewe, mabacebisane kunye, ukuthi, Ngubani na owavisa oko kwabamandulo, owakuxelayo kwanini? Asindim na Yehova, ekungekho Thixo wumbi ingendim? UThixo onobulungisa,  osindisayo, akakho ingendim.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:22">45:22</a> Bhekani kum, nisindiswe, nonke ziphelo zehlabathi; ngokuba ndinguThixo, akukho wumbi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:23">45:23</a> Ndizifungile, ilizwi liphume emlonyeni ngobulungisa, aliyi kuguqulwa; lithe, Aya kuguqa kum onke amadolo, zifunge mna zonke iilwimi;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:24">45:24</a> kuthiwe ngokubhekisele kum, KuYehova yedwa bubulungisa namandla, kuyiwa kuye; baya kudana bonke abavutha ngomsindo ngaye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:25">45:25</a> NgoYehova iya kugwetyelwa iqhayise yonke imbewu kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:1">46:1</a> UBhele uyaguqa, uNebho uya bhanyalaza; izithixo zabo zibekwe emaqegwini nasezinkomeni ezitsalayo; ezi nibe nizithwala zibotshiwe, zingumthwalo kwizinto ezityhafileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:2">46:2</a> Izithixo zabhanyalaza, zaguqa kunye, azaba nakuzisiza ekuthwaleni, ke inkqu yazo yaya ekuthinjweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:3">46:3</a> Phulaphulani kum, ndlu kaYakobi, nonke masalela endlu kaSirayeli, nina nabekwayo phezu kwam kwasesiswini, nina nathwalwayo ndim kwasesizalweni;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:4">46:4</a> kude kuse ebudaleni ikwandim, kude kuse ezimvini ndiya kunityatha emagxeni mna. Ndikwenzile mna; ndiya kunithwala mna,  ndiya kunityatha emagxeni mna, ndinisize.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:5">46:5</a> Ninokundifanisa, nindilinganise, nindinxulumise nabani na,  ukuba sifane?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:6">46:6</a> Bona bawohloza igolide engxoweni, balinganise isilivere ngesikali; baqesha umnyibilikisi, ayenze isithixo; basibekeke,  ewe, baqubude.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:7">46:7</a> Bayasithwala, basityathe emagxeni, basibeke phantsi endaweni yaso, sime; asibuyi sisuke kuloo ndawo yaso; ewe,  bayakhala kuso, singaphenduli; asisindisi bani embandezelweni yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:8">46:8</a> Khumbulani oko, nibe ngamadoda; kunyamekeleni ngentliziyo,  nina bakreqileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:9">46:9</a> Khumbulani izinto zangaphambili, zasephakadeni, okokuba ndinguThixo, akukho wumbi; ndinguThixo, akukho namnye unjengam;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:10">46:10</a> ukuxelayo kwasekuqaleni okungasemva, nakwabamandulo okungekenzeki, ndisithi, Icebo lam liya kuma, ndikwenze konke ukuthanda kwam;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:11">46:11</a> ndibiza ukhozi empumalanga, indoda yecebo lam ezweni elikude; nditshilo, ewe, ndiya kukufeza; ndiyilile, ewe, ndiya kukwenza.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:12">46:12</a> Phulaphulani kum, nina bantliziyo ilukhuni, bakude nobulungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:13">46:13</a> Ndisondeza ubulungisa bam, abuyi kuba kude; nosindiso lwam aluyi kulibala; ndinika usindiso eZiyon, uzuko lwam kuSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:1">47:1</a> Yihla, uhlale eluthulini, nkazanandini, ntombi inguBhabheli; hlala phantsi emhlabeni ungenatrone, ntombi ingamaKaledi; ngokuba akuyi kuba sathiwa uyimvoco, noxhamla ubuncwane.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:2">47:2</a> Thabatha amatye, usile umgubo; bhenqa isigqubuthelo sakho,  finyezela phezulu, tyhila umlenze, wela imilambo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:3">47:3</a> Mabutyhileke ubuze bakho, kubonakale nokungcikiveka kwakho;  ndiya kuphindezela, andiyi kubuka mntu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:4">47:4</a> Umkhululi wethu, igama lakhe nguYehova wemikhosi,  oyiNgcwele kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:5">47:5</a> Hlala uthi cwaka, ungeneemnyameni, ntombi ingamaKaledi;  ngokuba akuyi kuba sabizwa ngokuba uyinkosikazi yezikumkani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:6">47:6</a> Ndaba noburhalarhume kubantu bam, ndalingcolisa ilifa lam,  ndabanikela ezandleni zakho; akwaba namfesane kubo; naphezu kwamadoda amakhulu wayenza yanzima kakhulu idyokhwe yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:7">47:7</a> Ubusithi, Ndiya kuba yinkosikazi ngonaphakade; wada akwakunyamekela oko ngentliziyo, akwalikhumbula ikamva lakho oko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:8">47:8</a> Kaloku ke yiva oku, wena mxhamli weziyolo, uhleliyo ukholosile, wena uthi entliziyweni yakho, Ndim kwaphela, akukho wumbi; andiyi kuhlala ndingumhlolokazi, andiyi kukwazi ukungabi nabantwana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:9">47:9</a> Ziya kukuzela ezo zinto zombini ngephanyazo, ngamini-nye,  ukungabi nabantwana nobuhlolokazi; ziya kukuzela ngokugqibelela kwazo ebuninzini bokukhafula kwakho, enkitheni eninzi yomabophe bakho.</p>
