 <p><a name="an_47:10">47:10</a> Ngokuba ukholose ngezinto zakho ezimbi, wathi, Akukho undibonayo; ubulumko bakho nokwazi kwakho kuko okukuphambanisileyo; wathi entliziyweni yakho, Ndim kwaphela,  akukho wumbi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:11">47:11</a> Bokuzela ke ububi, ungakwazi ukubunyanga; ikuwele inkohlakalo, ungabi nako ukuyicamagushela; ikuzele ngesiquphe intshabalala ongayaziyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:12">47:12</a> Khawumise ngomabophe bakho, nangokukhafula kwakho okuninzi, ozixhamle ngako kwasebuncinaneni bakho; mhlawumbi ungaba nokunceda, mhlawumbi ungaba nokweyisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:13">47:13</a> Udiniwe bubuninzi bamaqhinga akho; mabamise kaloku,  bakusindise oonocanda bezulu, oojongiinkwenkwezi, abakwazisayo ekuthwaseni kwenyanga ngenyanga izinto ezikuzelayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:14">47:14</a> Yabona, basuke baba njengeendiza; umlilo ubatshisile;  abanakuwuhlangula umphefumlo wabo emandleni elangatye; akukho lahle lakuzifudumeza, akukho mlilo kungahlalwa phambi kwawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:15">47:15</a> Boba njalo kuwe abo uzixhamle ngabo, ababerhwebelana nawe kwasebuncinaneni bakho; elowo uya kundwendwela ecaleni lakhe,  kungabikho ukusindisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:1">48:1</a> Yivani oko, ndlu kaYakobi, nibizwayo ngegama likaSirayeli,  naphumayo emanzini kaYuda; nina nilifungayo igama likaYehova,  nimkhankanye uThixo kaSirayeli, kungenganyaniso,  kungengabulungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:2">48:2</a> Ngokuba bazibiza ngokuthi ngabomzi ongcwele, bazixhase ngoThixo kaSirayeli, ogama lakhe linguYehova wemikhosi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:3">48:3</a> Izinto zangaphambili ndazixela kwanini; zaphuma emlonyeni wam, ndazibonakalalisa; ndazenza ngesiquphe, zabakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:4">48:4</a> Ngokukwazi kwam ukuba ulukhuni, nentamo yakho ingumsipha wesinyithi, nebunzi lakho lilubhedu,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:5">48:5</a> ndakuxelela ezo zinto kwanini; zingekafiki ndakuvisa, hleze uthi, Isithixo sam sizenzile, umfanekiso wam oqingqiweyo notyhidiweyo uzimisile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:6">48:6</a> Uvile; sikhangele zonke ziphela; wena ke akunakuzixela na?  Ndiya kukuvisa izinto ezintsha, ezifihlakeleyo, obungazazi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:7">48:7</a> Zidalwa ngoku, azidalwanga kwanini; ingekabikho le mini,  ubungaziva; hleze uthi, Yabona, bendizazi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:8">48:8</a> Ubungaziva; ubungazazi; ibingavulekile indlebe yakho kwanini. Kuba bendisazi ukuba unginiza unginizile; ukubizwa kwakho kuthiwa ungumkreqi kwasesizalwani.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:9">48:9</a> Ngenxa yegama lam ndizeka kade ukuba nomsindo, nangenxa yendumiso yam ndiyawubamba ngakuwe, ukuze ndingakunqumli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:10">48:10</a> Uyabona, ndikunyibilikisile, akwaba ngokwesilivere;  ndakucikida ezikweni leentsizi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:11">48:11</a> Ndikwenza oko ngenxa yam, ngenxa yam (hayi, ukuhlanjelwa kwegama lam!); andiluniki wumbi uzuko lwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:12">48:12</a> Phulaphula kum, Yakobi, Sirayeli, mbizwa wam; ndim,  ndingowokuqala, ewe, ndingowokugqibela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:13">48:13</a> Ewe, isandla sam siseke ihlabathi, esokunene sam saneke izulu; ndithi ndakuzibiza ezo zinto, zime kunye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:14">48:14</a> Zihlanganiseni, nonke niphela, nive; ngubani na phakathi kwezithixo owazixelayo ezo zinto? Umthandwa kaYehova uya kukwenza ukuthanda kwakhe kwiBhabheli, nengalo yakhe ikwenze kumaKaledi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:15">48:15</a> Mna nditshilo, ewe, ndimbizile, ndimzisile; inempumelelo indlela yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:16">48:16</a> Sondelani kum, nive oku. Kwasekuqaleni andithethanga entsithelweni; kususela kwixesha lokwenzeka kwako oko,  ndilapha; nangoku iNkosi uYehova indithumile, mna noMoya wayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:17">48:17</a> Utsho uYehova, umkhululi wakho, oyiNgcwele kaSirayeli,  ukuthi, Mna Yehova, Thixo wakho, ndingokufundisa okungakuncedayo, ndikunyathelise ngendlela oya kuhamba ngayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:18">48:18</a> Akwaba imithetho yam ubuyibazele indlebe! Beluya kuba njengomlambo uxolo lwakho, nobulungisa bakho bube njengamaza olwandle;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:19">48:19</a> ibiya kuba njengentlabathi imbewu yakho, abaphuma ezibilinini zakho babe njengamasuntsu ayo belingayi kunqunyulwa litshabalale igama labo ebusweni bam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:20">48:20</a> Phumani eBhabheli, sabani kwelamaKaledi; kuxeleni ninelizwi lokumemelela, kuvakaliseni oku, kuhlabeleni kuye naseziphelweni zehlabathi; yithini, UYehova umkhulule ngokumhlawulela umkhonzi wakhe uYakobi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:21">48:21</a> Abanxanwanga, ebahambisa engqaqasini; wabatsitsisela amanzi eweni, wacanda iliwa, atsaza amanzi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:22">48:22</a> Akukho luxolo kwabangendawo, utsho uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:1">49:1</a> Phulaphulani kum, ziqithi; bazani indlebe, zizwe zikude;  uYehova undibize kwasesizalweni, ulikhankanye kwasezibilinini zikama igama lam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:2">49:2</a> Wawenza umlomo wam wanjengekrele elibukhali, wandizimeza esithunzini sesandla sakhe, wandenza utolo olubaziweyo,  wandisithelisa emphongolweni;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:3">49:3</a> wathi kum, Ungumkhonzi wam, wena Sirayeli, endiya kuhomba ngaye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:4">49:4</a> Ndathi mna, Ndifumane ndazixhamla, ndawaphelisa amandla am ngochuku, nangento engento; noko ibango lam likuYehova, nomvuzo wam unoThixo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:5">49:5</a> Kaloku ke uthi uYehova, owandibumba kwasesizalweni, ukuba ndibe ngumkhonzi kuye wokubuyisela uYakobi kuye, uSirayeli ahlanganiselwe kuye (ndizukile emehlweni kaYehova, uThixo wam waba ngamandla am);</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:6">49:6</a> uthi ke, Kuyinto elula ukuba ube ngumkhonzi kum wokumisa izizwe zakwaYakobi, ubuyise abalondolozwa bakaSirayeli;  kananjalo ndiya kukwenza isikhanyiso seentlanga, ukuba ube lusindiso lwam, ude uze eziphelweni zehlabathi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:7">49:7</a> Utsho uYehova, uMkhululi kaSirayeli, oyiNgcwele wakhe,  komphefumlo udelekileyo, kongamasikizi ezintlangeni, kumkhonzi wezilawuli, ukuthi, Ookumkani baya kubona, basuke beme,  nabathetheli babone, baqubude ngenxa kaYehova onyanisekileyo,  oyiNgcwele kaSirayeli, ngokokuba ekunyule.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:8">49:8</a> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Ngexesha elamkelekileyo ndikuphendule, ndakunceda ngemini yosindiso. Ndiya kukubumba,  ndikunike ukuba ube ngumnqophiso wabantu, ukuba ulimise ilizwe,  ukuba uwabe amafa angamanxuwa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:9">49:9</a> uthi kubabanjwa, Phumani; kwabasemnyameni, Velani. Baya kudla ngokomhlambi ezindleleni, amadlelo abo abekho naseluqayini lonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:10">49:10</a> Abayi kulamba, abayi kunxanwa, abayikubethwa sisanga nalilanga; ngokuba onemfesane kubo uya kubaqhuba, abathundezele emanzini ampompozayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:11">49:11</a> Ndiya kuzenza zonke iintaba zam zibe ziindlela, uphakame umendo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:12">49:12</a> Yabona, aba baya kuvela kude; yabona, aba baya kuvela kwelasentla naselwandle, aba bavele ezweni lamaSini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:13">49:13</a> Memelelani, mazulu; gcoba, hlabathi; gqabhukani nimemelele, zintaba; ngokuba uYehova ubathuthuzele abantu bakhe, unemfesane kwabaziintsizana zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:14">49:14</a> Ke yathi iZiyon, UYehova undishiyile, iNkosi yandilibala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:15">49:15</a> Umfazi angalulibala yini na usana lwakhe, ukuba angabi namfesane kunyana wesizalo sakhe? Nokuba oonina abo bathe balibala, andiyi kukulibala mna.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:16">49:16</a> Uyabona, ndikuvambile ezintendeni zezandla zam; iindonga zakho zihlala zimi phambi kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:17">49:17</a> Oonyana bakho bayakhawuleza, bayeza; abagungxuli bakho nabachithi bakho bayaphuma kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:18">49:18</a> Phakamisa amehlo akho ngeenxa zonke, ubone; bonke bephela bayahlanganisana, beza kuwe. Ndihleli nje, utsho uYehova, uya kubanxiba bonke bephela njengezivatho, ubabhinqe ngokombhinqo womtshakazi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:19">49:19</a> Ngokuba amanxuwa akho la, neendawo zakho ezigungxuliweyo,  nelizwe lakho elichithakeleyo-inene, ngoku uya kuxinana ngabemi kulo, babe kude abaginyi bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:20">49:20</a> Basaya kuthi ezindlebeni zakho oonyana bakho obubahluthiwe, Indawo ixinene kum, ndikhwelele, ndihlale;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:21">49:21</a> uya kuthi entliziyweni yakho, Ngubani na lo undizalele aba? Mna bendihluthiwe abantwana nje, ndaba ludlolo,  ndafuduswa, ndagxothwa; ke aba bakhuliswe ngubani na? Uyabona,  mna bendisele ndedwa; aba babephi na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:22">49:22</a> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Uyabona, ndisiphakamisela ezintlangeni isandla sam, ndiyinyusele ezizweni ibhanile yam,  zibazise ke oonyana bakho, zibawole ngeengalo, neentombi zakho zithwalwe ngamagxa,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:23">49:23</a> Ookumkani baya kuba ngabondli bakho, namakhosikazi abo abe ngabanyisi bakho. Baya kuqubuda kuwe, bese ubuso emhlabeni,  bakhothe uthuli lweenyawo zakho; wazi ke ukuba ndinguYehova,  obathembi bakhe bangayi kudana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:24">49:24</a> Anokuthatyathwa na amaxhoba kwigorha, basinde na abathinjiweyo bengamulungisa?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:25">49:25</a> Inene, utsho uYehova ukuthi, Nabathinjwe ligorha baya kuthatyathwa, namaxhoba omngcangcazelisi aya kusinda; ke obambana nawe, mna ndiya kubambana naye, ndibasindise mna oonyana bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:26">49:26</a> Abakuxinzelela phantsi ndobadlisa eyabo inyama, banxiliswe lelabo igazi ngathi kungewayini entsha; yazi inyama yonke,  ukuba mna, Yehova, ndinguMsindisi wakho, ukuba uMkhululi wakho ngOnamandla kaYakobi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:1">50:1</a> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Iphi na incwadi yokwaliwa kukanyoko,  endamgxotha ngayo? Khona kwabandibolekayo, uphi na lowo ndathengisa ngani kuye? Yabonani, kwathengiswa ngani ngenxa yobugwenxa benu; wagxothwa unyoko ngenxa yezikreqo zenu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:2">50:2</a> Yini na ukuba ndifike, kungekho mntu? ndibize, kungabikho usabelayo? Sifutshane kakhulu na isandla sam ukuba singakhululi? Akakho na kum amandla okuhlangula? Yabonani,  ngokukhalima kwam ndomisa ulwandle, imilambo ndiyenze intlango;  ziyabola iintlanzi zayo, ngokuba kungekho manzi, ziyafa kukunxanwa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:3">50:3</a> ndambesa izulu ngezimnyama zokuzila, ndenze ezirhwexayo zibe sisigubungelo salo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:4">50:4</a> INkosi uYehova indinike ulwimi lwabafundileyo, ukuze ndikwazi ukuzimasa otyhafileyo ngelizwi. Ivusa imiso ngemiso,  indivusela indlebe ukuba ndive ngokwabafundileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:5">50:5</a> INkosi uYehova indivule indlebe: ke mna andenza zinkani,  andabuya umva.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:6">50:6</a> Ndawunikela umhlana wam kubabethi, nezidlele zam kubadlathuli beendevu; andibusithelisanga ubuso bam ehlazweni nasekutshicelweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:7">50:7</a> Ke iNkosi uYehova iya kundinceda; ngenxa yoko andihlazekanga; ngenxa yoko ndabenza ubuso bam banjengeqhwitha;  ndiyazi ukuba andiyi kudana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:8">50:8</a> Usondele ondigwebelayo; ngubani na oya kubambana nam?  masime ndaweni-nye. Ngubani na ummangaleli wam? makeze kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:9">50:9</a> Uyabona, INkosi uYehova iya kundinceda; ngubani na yena oya kundigweba? Yabona bonke bephela baya konakala njengengubo,  amanundu aya kubadla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:10">50:10</a> Ngubani na kuni owoyika uYehova, ophulaphula izwi lomkhonzi wakhe? Ohamba emnyameni, kungabi mhlophe kuye,  makakholose ngegama likaYehova, ayame kuThixo wakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:11">50:11</a> Yabonani, nonke niphela, nina baphemba umlilo, baxhobe iintolo ezinomlilo, hambani niye elangatyeni lomlilo wenu,  nasezintolweni ezinomlilo enizivuthisileyo. Ke esandleni sam nantsi into eniya kuyizuza; niya kulala phantsi ninembulaleko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:1">51:1</a> Phulaphulani kum, nina babusukelayo ubulungisa, bamquqelayo uYehova; bhekani eweni enaxholwa kulo, nasesigingqini somhadi enembiwa kuwo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:2">51:2</a> Bhekani kuAbraham uyihlo, nakuSara owanizalayo; kuba waye emnye ndakumbiza, ndakumsikelela, ndakumandisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:3">51:3</a> Ngokuba uYehova uyithuthuzele iZiyon, uwathuthuzele onke amanxuwa ayo, wayenza intlango yayo yanjenge-Eden, nenkqantosi yayo yanjengomyezo kaYehova; kufumaneka imihlali nemivuyo kuyo,  imibulelo nezwi lohadi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:4">51:4</a> Ndibazeleni indlebe, bantu bam; ndibekeleni indlebe, sizwe sam; ngokuba isiyalelo siya kuphuma kum, ndilizinzise isiko lam, ukuba libe sisikhanyiso sezizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:5">51:5</a> Busondele ubulungisa bam, luphumile usindiso lwam; iingalo zam ziya kugweba izizwe, iziqithi zithembele kum, zilindele engalweni yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:6">51:6</a> Phakamiselani ezulwini amehlo enu, nibheke nasemhlabeni phantsi; ngokuba izulu liya kuthi shwaka njengomsi, wonakale umhlaba njengengubo, nabemi bawo bafe ngokunjalo, lube ngonaphakade lona usindiso lwam, bungaqotywa ubulungisa bam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:7">51:7</a> Phulaphulani kum, nina nibaziyo ubulungisa, bantu banesiyalo sam entliziyweni yabo; musani ukukoyika ukungcikiva kwabafo, ningaqhiphuki umbilini kukunyelisa kwabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:8">51:8</a> Kuba amanundu aya kubadla njengengubo, umbungu ubadle njengoboya begusha; ke bona ubulungisa bam buya kuba ngunaphakade, nosindiso lwam lube kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:9">51:9</a> Vuka, vuka, nxiba amandla, ngalo kaYehova! Vuka,  njengokwemihla yamandulo, njengokwezizukulwana zaphakade!  Asinguwe na lowa wachitha uRahabhi, wayihlaba ingwenya?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:10">51:10</a> Asinguwe na lowa womisa ulwandle, amanzi enzonzobila enkulu; iinzulu zolwandle wazenza indlela yokuwela abahlawulelweyo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:11">51:11</a> Ke abakhululwa bakaYehova baya kubuya babuye, beze eZiyon bememelela, benovuyo olungunaphakade phezu kweentloko zabo;  baya kufumana imihlali nemivuyo, sisabe isingqala nokuncwina.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:12">51:12</a> Mna ndinguye uMthuthuzeli wenu; ungubani na wena, ukuba woyike umfo oza kufa, nonyana womntu owenziwe wanga yingca;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:13">51:13</a> ukuba umlibale uYehova uMenzi wakho, uManeki wezulu,  uMseki wehlabathi; ukuba uhlale unkwantya imini yonke bubushushu bombandezeli, ngokokuba exunela ukonakalisa; buphi na ke ubushushu bombandezeli?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:14">51:14</a> Ogotyiweyo ngamakhamandela wobehle akhululwe, angafeli esihogweni, angasisweli isonka sakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:15">51:15</a> Kuba ndinguYehova uThixo wakho, uMlatyuzisi wolwandle,  agqume amaza alo, ogama lakhe linguYehova wemikhosi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:16">51:16</a> Ndiwabekile amazwi am emlonyeni wakho, ndakugubungela ngesithunzi sesandla sam, ukuba ndityale izulu, ukuba ndiseke ihlabathi, ukuba ndithi kwiZiyon, Ningabantu bam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:17">51:17</a> Zivuse, zivuse, suk ume, Yerusalem wena uyiseleyo esandleni sikaYehova indebe yobushushu bakhe; uyisele wayifinca indebe enombilini ehexisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:18">51:18</a> Bekungekho namnye uyithundezayo iYerusalem, phakathi koonyana bonke eyabazalayo; bekungekho namnye uyibambe ngesandla, phakathi koonyana bonke eyabakhulisayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:19">51:19</a> Zazimbini izinto ezakuhlelayo; ngubani na owakukhuzayo?  Yimbuqo nokwaphuka, yindlala nekrele; bendingathini na ukukuthuthuzela?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:20">51:20</a> Oonyana bakho bawa isiduli, balala emantloko ezitrato zonke, njengeula eli libanjisiweyo; bazele bubushushu bukaYehova, kukukhalima koThixo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:21">51:21</a> Ngako oko, khawuve le nto, wena ludwayinge, unxilayo kodwa kungengayo iwayini;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:22">51:22</a> itsho iNkosi yakho uYehova, uThixo wakho obathethelelayo abantu bakhe, ukuthi, Yabona, ndiyayithabatha esandleni sakho indebe ehexisayo, indebe enombilini yobushushu bam; akusayi kuphinda usele kuyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:23">51:23</a> Ndoyibeka esandleni sabakwenza isingqala, ababesithi kumphefumlo wakho, Qubuda sigqithe, waza wena wawenza umhlana wakho wanjengomhlaba, wanjengesitrato kwabagqitha phezu kwawo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:1">52:1</a> Vuka, vuka, nxiba amandla akho, Ziyon! Nxiba iingubo zakho zokuhomba, Yerusalem, mzi ungcwele! Kuba akuyi kuba saphinda kungene kuwe ongalukanga, noyinqambi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:2">52:2</a> Zivuthulule uthuli; suk ume, hlala phantsi, Yerusalem;  zikhulule iimbophelelo zentamo yakho, mthinjwa, ntombi inguZiyon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:3">52:3</a> Ngokuba utsho uYehova ukuthi, Kwathengiswa ngani ngelize;  aniyi kuhlawulelwa nikhululwe ngamali.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:4">52:4</a> Kuba itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Abantu bam behla baya eYiputa ekuqaleni, ukuba baphambukele khona; ke ama-Asiriya abacudisa kungekho sizathu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:5">52:5</a> Kaloku ke yintoni na enamapha, utsho uYehova, bethatyathwe ngelize nje abantu bam? Abalawuli babo bayabhomboloza, utsho uYehova; igama lam lihlala ligitywa imini yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:6">52:6</a> Ngako oko abantu bam baya kulazi igama lam; ngako oko baya kwazi ngaloo mini ukuba ndinguye lowo uthi, Ndingokhoyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:7">52:7</a> Hayi, ukuba zintle kwazo ezintabeni iinyawo zabashumayela iindaba ezimnandi, zabavakalisa uxolo, zabashumayela iindaba ezilungileyo, zabavakalisa usindiso; zabathi kwiZiyon,  Uyalawula uThixo wakho!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:8">52:8</a> Phulaphula ilizwi lababoniseli bakho. Baliphakamisa kunye ilizwi, bayamemelela; ngokuba bekubona iliso kwiliso ukuyibuyisa kukaYehova iZiyon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:9">52:9</a> Gqobhokelani ekumemeleleni kunye, manxuwa aseYerusalem;  ngokuba uYehova ubathuthuzele abantu bakhe, uyihlawulele wayikhulula iYerusalem.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:10">52:10</a> UYehova uyihlubile ingalo yakhe engcwele emehlweni eentlanga zonke; zonke iziphelo zehlabathi ziya kulubona ke usindiso loThixo wethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:11">52:11</a> Mkani, mkani, phumani apho; musani ukuphatha nto iyinqambi; phumani phakathi kwayo; zenzeni nyulu, nina bathwali beempahla zikaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:12">52:12</a> Ngokuba aniyi kuphuma buphuthuphuthu, nihambe ngokusaba;  kuba uYehova uhamba phambi kwenu, uMqoshelisi wenu nguThixo kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:13">52:13</a> Yabonani, umkhonzi wam uya kwenza ngengqiqo, uya kuphakama, athi gqi, anyuke kakhulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:14">52:14</a> Kwanjengokuba babemangaliswa nguwe abaninzi (ibinje ukonakala imbonakalo yakhe, ukuda ingabi yeyomntu, nesithomo sakhe ukuda singabi sesoonyana baka-Adam):</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:15">52:15</a> ngokunjalo yena uya kubetha zithi makatha iintlanga ezininzi; ngenxa yakhe ookumkani baya kuthi khamnqa; ngokuba baya kukubona abangazanga bakubaliselwe, bakugqale abangazanga bakuve.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:1">53:1</a> Ngubani na okholiweyo ludaba lwethu, nengalo kaYehova ityhileke kubani na?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:2">53:2</a> Kuba yena umkhonzi unyuka njengegatya phambi kwakhe,  njengehlumelo eliphuma ezweni elingumqwebedu, engenasithomo nabungangamela; sakukhangela, akwabakho kubonakala ukuba masimnqwenele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:3">53:3</a> Udeliwe, ushiyiwe ngabantu; yindoda enomvandedwa, eqhelene nesifo wanga ngulowo kusitheliswa kuye ubuso, udeliwe, thina ke asambeka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:4">53:4</a> Okwenene, uzithabathele phezu kwakhe izifo zethu, wathwala umvandedwa wethu, ke thina besiba ungobandezelwayo nguThixo,  ungocinezelwa nguye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:5">53:5</a> Kanti yena uhlatywe ngenxa yezikreqo zethu, watyunyuzwa ngenxa yezenzo zethu ezigwenxa; ubetho lokuba sibe noxolo thina lube luphezu kwakhe; siphiliswe ngemivumbo yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:6">53:6</a> Thina zonke salahleka njengeegusha, sabheka elowo endleleni yakhe, waza uYehova wamwela ngobugwenxa bethu sonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:7">53:7</a> Wakhandaniswa, wazithoba, engawuvuli umlomo wakhe,  njengemvana esiwa ekuxhelweni; nanjengegusha esisidenge phambi kwabachebi bayo, akawuvula umlomo wakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:8">53:8</a> Uthatyathwe ekuxinweni nasematyaleni; esizukulwaneni sakhe ngubani na owathelekelela ukuthi, unqanyulwe ezweni labaphilileyo, ubandezelwe ngenxa yesikreqo sabantu bakowethu?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:9">53:9</a> Lamiswa nawaboni ingcwaba lakheke laba nosisityebi,  akuba efile; ekubeni engenzanga lugonyamelo, kungabangakho nkohliso emlonyeni wakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:10">53:10</a> UYehova ke wathanda ukumtyumza nokumvisa isifo. Xa uthe umphefumlo wakhe wawenza idini letyala, woyibona imbewu yakhe,  abe nemihla emide; ukuthanda kukaYehova kube nempumelelo ngesandla sakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:11">53:11</a> Ngokwaphuka komphefumlo wakhe wobona, aneliswe; ngokwazi kwakhe, umkhonzi wam olilungisa uya kugwebela abaninzi, athwale yena izenzo zabo ezigwenxa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:12">53:12</a> Ngako oko ndiya kumahlulela isahlulo nabakhulu, alabe nabanegunya ixhoba, ngethuba lokuba ewuminyele ekufeni umphefumlo wakhe, wavuma ukubalelwa kubakreqi, akubon ukuba usithabathile phezu kwakhe isono sabaninzi, ebathandazele abakreqi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:1">54:1</a> Memelela, ludlolo lungazaliyo; gqabhuka umemelele,  utsholoze, wena ungenanimba; ngokuba baninzi abantwana besishiywa, ngaphezu kwabantwana bonendoda; utsho uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:2">54:2</a> Yenze banzi indawo yentente yakho, uwatwabulule amalengalenga eminquba yakho, ungathinteli; zolule izintya zakho, uziqinisele izikhonkwane zakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:3">54:3</a> Kuba uya kutyhobozela ekunene nasekholo, imbewu yakho izidle ilifa iintlanga, iyime imizi ebingamanxuwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:4">54:4</a> Musa ukoyika, ngokuba akuyi kudana; musa ukudideka lihlazo,  ngokuba akuyi kuba nazintloni. Ngokuba ukudana kobuntombi bakho uya kukulibala, ungcikivo lobuhlolokazi bakho ungabi salukhumbula.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:5">54:5</a> Ngokuba indoda yakho nguMenzi wakho, ogama lakhe linguYehova wemikhosi; nguMkhululi wakho oyiNgcwele kaSirayeli,  ekuthiwa nguThixo wehlabathi lonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:6">54:6</a> Ngokuba uYehova ukubize njengomfazi obeshiyiwe, omoya ubulalekileyo, njengomfazi wobutsha, xeshikweni ebethe wacekiswa; utsho uThixo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:7">54:7</a> Ndakushiya okwephanyazo elincinane; ndiya kukubutha ngemfesane enkulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:8">54:8</a> Ngomkhukula woburhalarhume ndabusithelisa ubuso bam kuwe okwephanyazo; ndiya kuba nemfesane kuwe ngenceba engunaphakade;  utsho uMkhululi wakho uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:9">54:9</a> Ngokuba injengonogumbe kaNowa le nto kum; oko ndafungayo ukuba amanzi kaNowa akasayi kuba sahamba phezu kwehlabathi,  ngokunjalo ndifungile ukuba andiyi kuba naburhalarhume kuwe,  ndingakukhalimeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:10">54:10</a> Ngokuba zingade zimke iintaba, neenduli zishukume; yona inceba yam ayiyi kumka kuwe, ungashukumi nomnqophiso wam woxolo; utsho onemfesane kuwe, uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:11">54:11</a> Wena lusizana, uphetshethwayo ungenantuthuzelo, yabona,  ndiwabeka amatye akho kwistibhiya, ndikuseka ngeesafire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:12">54:12</a> Ndolumisa uqoqo lwakho ngeerubhi, namasango akho ngamatye abengezelayo, nemida yakho yonke ngamatye anqabileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:13">54:13</a> Bonke abantwana bakho baya kuba ngabafundi bakaYehova,  lube lukhulu uxolo lwabantwana bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:14">54:14</a> Uya kuzinza ngobulungisa; ungakhe uxhale, ngokuba akuyi kuba nakoyika; ungakhe uqhiphuke umbilini, ngokuba akuyi kusondela kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:15">54:15</a> Yabona, bayaqukana bahlanganisane, andikho mna kuloo nto;  nokuba ngoobani na abaya kuqukana ngawe, baya kuwa ngenxa enawe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:16">54:16</a> Yabona, mna ndadala ingcibi efutha umlilo wamalahle,  ivelise impahla ngokweshishini layo; kwamna ndadala nomonakalisi wokuyonakalisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:17">54:17</a> Zonke izixhobo ezikhandelwa ukulwa nawe aziyi kuba nampumelelo; zonke iilwimi ezimelene nawe ematyaleni uya kuzigweba. Lilo eli ilifa labakhonzi bakaYehova, nobulungisa babo obuphuma kum; utsho uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:1">55:1</a> Wenani! Nonke nina ninxaniweyo, yizani emanzini,  nabangenamali; yizani, thengani nidle; yizani, thengani iwayini namasi, ningenani, ningenamali.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:2">55:2</a> Yini na ukuba nilinganisele imali ngento engesonka,  nokuxelenga kwenu ngento engahluthisiyo? Phulaphulani kum ninyameke, nidle okulungileyo, umphefumlo wenu uxhamle ukutyeba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:3">55:3</a> Thobani iindlebe zenu, nize kum; yivani, uphile umphefumlo wenu; ndenze umnqophiso ongunaphakade nani, iinceba zikaDavide ezinyanisekileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:4">55:4</a> Yabona, ndimenze ingqina ezizweni, inganga nomwisimethetho ezizweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:5">55:5</a> Yabona, uya kubiza uhlanga ongalwaziyo, uhlanga olungakwaziyo wena lugidimele kuwe, ngenxa kaYehova uThixo wakho, ngenxa yoyiNgcwele kaSirayeli, kuba ekuhombisile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:6">55:6</a> Funani uYehova esenokufunyanwa; mbizeni esekufuphi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:7">55:7</a> Ongendawo makashiye indlela yakhe, indoda enobutshinga mayishiye iingcinga zayo, ibuyele kuYehova: woba nemfesane kuyo; ibuyele kuThixo wethu ngokuba woxolela ngokukhulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:8">55:8</a> Kuba iingcinga zam asizizo iingcinga zenu, neendlela zenu asizizo iindlela zam, utsho uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:9">55:9</a> Inene, njengokuba izulu liwuphakamele umhlaba, ngokunjalo iindlela zam ziziphakamele iindlela zenu, neengcinga zam ziziphakamele iingcinga zenu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:10">55:10</a> Kuba, njengokuba kusihla imvula nekhephu ezulwini,  ingabuyeli kulo ingathanga iwunyakamise umhlaba uvunde,  iwuhlumise, iwenze untshule, imnike imbewu umhlwayeli, imnike isonka odlayo:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:11">55:11</a> liya kuba njalo ilizwi lam eliphuma emlonyeni wam; aliyi kubuyela kum lilambatha, lingakwenzanga endikuthandayo,  lingakuphumelelisanga oko ndilithumela kuko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:12">55:12</a> Kuba niya kuphuma ninovuyo, nithundezwe ninoxolo. Iintaba neenduli ziya kugqabhuka zimemelele phambi kwenu, imithi yasendle ibethe izandla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:13">55:13</a> Esikhundleni somqaqoba kuya kuphuma imisedare,  esikhundleni serhawu kuya kunyuka imimirtile; oko kube ligama kuYehova, nomqondiso ongunaphakade ongayi kunqanyulwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:1">56:1</a> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Gcinani isiko, nenze ubulungisa; kuba lusondele ukuba luze usindiso lwam, nobulungisa bam ukuba butyhileke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:2">56:2</a> Hayi, uyolo lomntu okwenzayo oku, nonyana womntu obambelela kuko oku; ogcina isabatha ukuba angayihlambeli; ogcina isandla sakhe ukuba singenzi nanye into embi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:3">56:3</a> Makangatsho ke unyana wolunye uhlanga, lo unamathele kuYehova, ukuthi, UYehova uya kundahlula kube kanye ebantwini bakhe; malingathi ithenwa, Yabona, ndingumthi owomileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:4">56:4</a> Ngokuba utsho uYehova kumathenwa ukuthi, Abazigcinayo iisabatha zam, banyule endikuthandayo, babambelele emnqophisweni wam,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:5">56:5</a> ndobanika, endlwini yam nasezindongeni zam, indawo negama elilungileyo ngaphezu koonyana neentombi; ndobanika igama elingunaphakade elingayi kunqunyulwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:6">56:6</a> Ke oonyana bolunye uhlanga, abanamathele kuYehova, ukuze balungiselele kuye, balithande igama likaYehova, ukuba babe ngabakhonzi kuye, bonke abayigcinayo isabatha bangayihlambeli,  ababambelela emnqophisweni wam:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:7">56:7</a> ndobazisa entabeni yam engcwele, ndibavuyise endlwini yam yokuthandaza; amadini abo anyukayo nemibingelelo yabo yokholiseka esibingelelweni sam; kuba indlu yam kuya kuthiwa yindlu yokuthandaza ezizweni zonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:8">56:8</a> Itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Ekubabutheni abagxothiweyo bakaSirayeli, ndisaya kubutha nabanye ngaphaya kwakhe, ngaphaya kwababuthiweyo bakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:9">56:9</a> Nonke marhamncwa asendle, yizani apha; yizani kudla, nonke marhamncwa asehlathini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:10">56:10</a> Ababoniseli bakhe baziimfama, bonke bephela abanakwazi,  bonke bephela bazizinja ezizizidenge, ezingenakukhonkotha;  zibhuda, zilala, zithanda ubuthongo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:11">56:11</a> Ewe, bazizinja ezithanda ukudla, ezingahluthiyo nokuhlutha; banjalo ke abalusi, abakwazi ukuqonda; bonke bephela babheke kwezabo iindlela, elowo kweyakhe inzuzo,  kowakhe ummandla.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:12">56:12</a> Uthi, Yizani, ndiya kuthabatha iwayini, sisele kunene isiselo esinxilisayo; neyangomso imini ibe njengale, ibe nkulu,  incamise kunene.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:1">57:1</a> Ilungisa liyatshabalala; akukho mntu ke ukunyamekelayo oko ngentliziyo; amadoda anobubele ayemka, akukho mntu ke uqondayo ukuba ilungisa limka phambi kokuba kubekho ububi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:2">57:2</a> Lingena eluxolweni; baphumla ezililini zabo ababehambe ngokuthe gca.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:3">57:3</a> Ke nina, sondelani apha, nyana betolakazi, mbewu yomkrexezi neyehenyukazi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:4">57:4</a> Nivuyelela bani na? Nisinekela bani na, ningongoza nje?  Aningabantwana bokreqo, imbewu yobuxoki, yini na,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:5">57:5</a> nina bazitshisekisayo emiterebhintini, phantsi kwemithi yonke eluhlaza; nina babasikayo abantwana ezihlanjeni phantsi kwemiqhokro yeengxondorha?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:6">57:6</a> Isahlulo sakho saba sematyeni agudileyo esihlambo; wona aba ngamaqashiso akho; kananjalo wawathululela amadini athululwayo,  wenyusa iminikelo yokudla kuwo. Mandizithuthuzele na ngezo zinto?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:7">57:7</a> Entabeni ephakamileyo ende wabeka isilili sakho, wenyuka waya kubingelela imibingelelo nalapho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:8">57:8</a> Isikhumbuzo sakho wasibeka emva kocango nomgubasi; ngokuba wathi ungekum wazityhila, wenyuka, wasenza sabanzi isilili sakho, wanqophisana nabo, wathanda kulala nabo, wandlala ukhuko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:9">57:9</a> Wahambela kukumkani uneoli, wanyhikiza iziqholo zakho,  wazithuma kude izigidimi zakho, wazithoba kwada kwaba kwelabafileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:10">57:10</a> Wadinwa ngokuba nde kwendlela yakho; akwathi, Ndincamile;  wawafumana ebuya ephila amandla akho ngenxa yoko akuthanga fehlefehle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:11">57:11</a> Ubunesithukuthezi ngabani na, ubusoyika bani na, ukuba uthethe amanga, ungandikhumbuli, ungakunyamekeli oko ngentliziyo? Andithe quthu na kususela kwaphakade, ungandoyiki nje?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:12">57:12</a> Ndiya kubuxela mna ubulungisa bakho, nezenzo zakho aziyi kukunceda nto.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:13">57:13</a> Ekukhaleni kwakho mazikuhlangule iimfumba zezithixo zakho;  zonke ziphela zimka nomoya, zithatyathwa ngumphunga. Ke yena okholosa ngam uya kulidla ilifa ilizwe, ayime intaba yam engcwele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:14">57:14</a> Uthile wothi, Fumbani, fumbani, gecani indlela; susani isikhubekiso endleleni yabantu bam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:15">57:15</a> Ngokuba utsho ophezulu, owongamileyo, ohleli ngonaphakade,  ogama linguNgcwele, ukuthi, Ndihleli phezulu, engcweleni,  ndihleli nakotyumkileyo, omoya uthobekileyo; ukuba ndibuye ndiphilise umoya wabathobekileyo, ndibuye ndiphilise intliziyo yabatyumkileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:16">57:16</a> Ngokuba andiyi kubambana naye ngonaphakade, andiyi kuhlala ndinoburhalarhume; kuba umoya ubungatyhafayo phambi kwam,  nemiphefumlo endiyenzileyo mna.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:17">57:17</a> Ngenxa yobugwenxa bokubawa kwakhe ndaba noburhalarhume,  ndambetha, ndazisithelisa, ndaba noburhalarhume; wahamba ephamba ngendlela yentliziyo yakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:18">57:18</a> Iindlela zakhe ndizibonile: ndiya kumphilisa,  ndimalathise, ndimbuyekezele intuthuzalo yena, nabakhe ke abenza isijwili.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:19">57:19</a> Umdali weziqhamo zomlomo, uYehova, uthi, Uxolo, uxolo malubekho kwabakude nakwabakufuphi, ndibaphilise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:20">57:20</a> Ke bona abangendawo banjengolwandle oluvunjululweyo,  ngokuba alunakuzola; amanzi alo avumbulula udaka nezibi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:21">57:21</a> Alukho uxolo kwabangendawo, utsho uThixo wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:1">58:1</a> Danduluka uphimisele, ungathinteleki; phakamisa izwi lakho njengesigodlo, ubaxelele abantu bam ukreqo lwabo, uyixelele indlu kaYakobi izono zayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:2">58:2</a> Ke bayandingxoka imini ngemini, bakunanzile ukuzazi iindlela zam. Njengohlanga olwenze ubulungisa alwalishiya isiko loThixo walo, bacela kum imigwebo yobulungisa, bakunanzile ukusondela kuThixo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:3">58:3</a> Bathi, Yini na ukuba sizile ukudla, ungaboni? siwuthobe umphefumlo wethu, ungazi? Yabonani, ngomhla wokuzila kwenu nifumana enikunanzileyo, nibakhandanise abasebenzi benu bonke ababulalekayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:4">58:4</a> Yabonani, nizilela ukubambana, niphikisane, nibethane ngenqindi lokungendawo; namhla anizileli ukuze nivakalise ilizwi lenu phezulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:5">58:5</a> Into enjalo ingaba kukuzila endikunyulileyo na? Ingaba ngumhla wokuba umntu awuthobe umphefumlo wakhe na?  Ukuthokombisa intloko yakhe njengomzi andlale ezirhwexayo nothuthu, oko ukubiza ngokuthi kukuzila na? Ngumhla okholekileyo na kuYehova?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:6">58:6</a> Ukuzila endikunyulileyo asikoku na: ukucombulula iziqamangelo zokungendawo, ukukhulula izitropu zeedyokhwe,  ukundulula abavikivekileyo bekhululekile, naphule zonke iidyokhwe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:7">58:7</a> Asikoku na: ukumqhekezela esonkeni sakho olambileyo,  ubangenise endlwini abaziintsizana, abatshutshiswayo? xa uthe wabona ohamba ze, umambese, ungazifihli kwinyama yakho?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:8">58:8</a> Kuya kwandula ke ukukhanya kwakho kuthi qhiphu njengokusa,  kuhlume kamsinya ukupholiswa kwakho, buhambe phambi kwakho ubulungisa bakho, buqoshelise emva kwakho ubuqaqawuli bukaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:9">58:9</a> Uya kwandula ubize, asabele uYehova; uzibike, athi, Ndikho!  Ukuba uthe wakususa phakathi kwakho ukufaka idyokhwe,  nokwalatha ngomnwe, nokuthetha ubudenge;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:10">58:10</a> wamvukelisa olambileyo ngento oyidlayo, wawuhluthisa umphefumlo wocinezelweyo: kophumela ke ukukhanya kwakho emnyameni, nesithokothoko sakho sibe njengemini enkulu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:11">58:11</a> Uya kuhlala ekwalathisa uYehova, awuhluthise umphefumlo wakho ekubaleleni kwelanga, omeleze amathambo akho, ube njengomyezo onyakanyiswa yimvula, nanjengendawo ephuma amanzi,  emanzi angatshiyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:12">58:12</a> Baya kwakha amanxuwa angunaphakade abakowenu, uvuse iziseko zezizukulwana ngezizukulwana; bathi ukukubiza nguMvingci wamathuba, nguMbuyisi womendo wokuhlala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:13">58:13</a> Ukuba uthe walubuyisa unyawo lwakho kwisabatha, ukuba ungenzi okunanzileyo ngomhla wam ongcwele; wathi ukuyibiza isabatha isisonwabiso, ingcwele kaYehova; wathi inozuko,  wayizukisa ke ngokungenzi iindlela zakho, ngokungafumani okunanzileyo, uthethe iintetho ezingeni:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:14">58:14</a> uya kwandula ukuziyolisa ngoYehova, ndikukhwelise emimangweni yomhlaba, ndikudlise ilifa likaYakobi uyihlo; kuba umlomo kaYehova uthethile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:1">59:1</a> Yabonani, isandla sikaYehova asisifutshane, ukuba singasindisi; nendlebe yakhe ayinzima, ukuba ingevi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:2">59:2</a> Bubugwenxa benu obunahlukanisileyo noThixo wenu, zizono zenu ezibusithelisileyo ubuso bakhe kuni, ukuba angevi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:3">59:3</a> Kuba izandla zenu zidyobhekile ligazi, neminwe yenu bubugwenxa; nomlomo wenu uthetha ubuxoki, ulwimi lwenu ludumzela ubugqwetha.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:4">59:4</a> Akukho uvakalisa ilizwi elinobulungisa, akukho umangalelana nomnye enyanisile; bakholose ngochuku, bathethe inkohlakalo;  bakhawula ububi, bazale ubutshinga.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:5">59:5</a> Baqandusela amaqanda erhamba, baluka izindlu zesigcawu.  Lowo udla amaqanda abo uya kufa; elinyathelweyo liqandulelwa inyushu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:6">59:6</a> Imisonto yabo ayiyi kuba yingubo, nemisebenzi yabo ayiyi kubagubungela. Izenzo zabo zizenzo zobutshinga; ukusebenza ngogonyamelo kusezandleni zabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:7">59:7</a> Iinyawo zabo zigidimela ebubini, zikhawuleze ukuya kuphalaza igazi elimsulwa; iingcinga zabo ziingcinga zobutshinga; emendweni wabo kukubhuqa nokwaphula.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:8">59:8</a> Abayazi indlela yoxolo, okusesikweni akukho emikhondweni yabo; bazijikajikile iindlela zabo; bonke abanyathela kuzo abalwazi uxolo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:9">59:9</a> Ngenxa yoko kukude kuthi okusesikweni, nobulungisa abufikeleli kuthi. Sithembe ukukhanya, nanku ke kumnyama;  sithembe ukuba kube mhlophe, sihamba esithokothokweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:10">59:10</a> Siya phuthaphutha njengeemfama eludongeni;  siyaphuthaphutha njengabangenamehlo; sikhubeka emini enkulu ngathi kungongcwalazi; phakathi kwabaxhamla ubomi, ngathi thina singabafileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:11">59:11</a> Siyavungama njengebhere sonke siphela; sidumzela sidumzele njengamavukuthu; sithemba okusesikweni, kungabikho; sithemba usindiso, lube kude kuthi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:12">59:12</a> Kuba zininzi izikreqo zethu phambi kwakho, nezono zethu ziyangqina ngathi; kuba izikreqo zethu zinathi, nobugwenxa bethu siyabazi:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:13">59:13</a> ukukreqa kuYehova, nokumkhanyela, nokubuya umva kuThixo wethu, ukuthetha okucudisayo, okutyekisayo, ukukhawula nokuphimisela ngentliziyo amazwi obuxoki.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:14">59:14</a> Okusesikweni kubuyiswe umva, nobulungisa bumi kude;  ngokuba inyaniso ikhubekile endaweni yembutho, akunakungena okuthe gca.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:15">59:15</a> Yesuka yasweleka inyaniso, nocezayo ebubini wazibhunyulisa. Wabona ke uYehova, kwakubi emehlweni akhe,  ukuba kungekho okusesikweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:16">59:16</a> Wabona ukuba akukho mntu, wamangaliswa ukuba kungekho mthandazeli; yaza yamsindisela ingalo yakhe, nobulungisa bakhe bona bamxhasa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:17">59:17</a> Wanxiba ubulungisa ngokwengubo yentsimbi, wanxiba isigcina-ntloko sosindiso entloko; ukwambatha wambatha iingubo zempindezelo, wazithi wambu ngekhwele, kwanga kungengubo yokwaleka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:18">59:18</a> Ngokwempatho yabo leyo uya kubuyekeza ngokoko, ubushushu kubabandezeli bakhe, kwaimpatho yabo kwabaziintshaba zakhe;  kwiziqithi uya kubuyekeza kwaimpatho yazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:19">59:19</a> Baya kuloyika igama likaYehova entshonalanga, baboyike ubuqaqawuli bakhe empumalanga; kuba uya kuza njengomlambo oxineneyo, obalekiswa ngumoya kaYehova;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:20">59:20</a> eze engumkhululi weZiyon, wababuyayo elukreqweni kwaYakobi; utsho uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:21">59:21</a> Mna ke nguwo lo umnqophiso wam nabo, utsho uYehova; uMoya wam ophezu kwakho, nelizwi lam endilibeke emlonyeni wakho,  aliyi kusuka emlonyeni wakho, nasemlonyeni wembewu yakho,  nasemlonyeni wembewu yembewu yakho, utsho uYehova, kuthabathele kweli xesha kude kuse ephakadeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:1">60:1</a> Suk ume ukhanye, kuba kufikile ukukhanya kwakho,  nobuqaqawuli bukaYehova buthe chapha kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:2">60:2</a> Ngokuba, uyabona, ubumnyama buwugubungele umhlaha,  isithokothoko sizigubungele izizwe; ke kuwe uYehova uthe chapha, ubuqaqawuli bakhe bubonakele phezu kwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:3">60:3</a> Ziya kuhamba iintlanga zize ekukhanyeni kwakho, ookumkani beze ebumhlotsheni bokuthi chapha kwakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:4">60:4</a> Phakamisa amehlo akho ngeenxa zonke, ubone; bonke bephela bayahlanganisana, baza kuwe; oonyana bakho bavela kude,  neentombi zakho zibelekwe ephangweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:5">60:5</a> Uya kwandula ukubona, ukhazimle, inkwantye yande intliziyo yakho; ngokuba iya kuguqulelwa kuwe intabalala yolwandle,  ubutyebi beentlanga buya kuza kuwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:6">60:6</a> Inkitha yeenkamela iya kukugubungela, amagobo akwaMidiyan nawakwaEfa, bonke bephela baya kuza bevela kwaShebha, bezisa igolide nentlaka emhlophe, beshumayela iindaba ezilungileyo zeendumiso zikaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:7">60:7</a> Yonke imihlambi yakwaKedare ibuthelana kuwe, iinkunzi zeegusha zakwaNebhayoti ziyakulungiselela; zinyuka ngokulikholo kum esibingelelweni sam, ndihombise indlu yokuhomba kwam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:8">60:8</a> Ngoobani na abaya, beza bebaleka njengelifu,  njengamavukuthu esiza emakrobeni awo?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:9">60:9</a> Okwenene zithembele kum iziqithi, ziinqanawa zaseTarshishe phambili; zizisa oonyana bakho bevela kude, benesilivere yabo negolide yabo, kwigama likaYehova uThixo wakho, koyiNgcwele kaSirayeli, ngokokuba ekuhombisile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:10">60:10</a> Oonyana bolunye uhlanga baya kuzakha iindonga zakho,  ookumkani babo bakulungiselele; kuba ndikubethe ndinoburhalarhume, kodwa ndaba nemfesane kuwe ndinetarhu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:11">60:11</a> ohlala evuliwe amasango akho imini nobusuku; akayi kuvalwa, ukuze bungeniswe kuwe ubutyebi beentlanga, nookumkani bazo beqhutywa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:12">60:12</a> Kuba uhlanga nobukumkani obungayi kukukhonza buya kutshabalala, ezo ntlanga ziphanze ziphanzile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:13">60:13</a> Ubuqaqawuli beLebhanon buya kuza kuwe, umsipres nompleyini nomgalagala ndawonye, ukuze ihombe indawo yengcwele yam,  ndiyizukise indawo yeenyawo zam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:14">60:14</a> Baya kuza kuwe besibekeka oonyana babacinezeli bakho,  baqubude ezintendeni zeenyawo zakho abakugibayo; ukukubiza bathi, Mzi kaYehova, Ziyon yoyiNgcwele kaSirayeli.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:15">60:15</a> Esikhundleni sokuba ubushiyiwe, uthiyiwe, akwabakho bani ucanda kuwe, ndiya kukwenza ke ingangamsha engunaphakade,  imihlali yezizukulwana ngezizukulwana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:16">60:16</a> Uya kwanya amasi eentlanga, wanye ibele lokumkani, wazi ukuba mna Yehova ndinguMsindisi wakho, uMkhululi wakho,  iMbalasane kaYakobi.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:17">60:17</a> Esikhundleni sobhedu ndizisa igolide, esikhundleni sesinyithi ndizisa isilivere, esikhundleni semithi ubhedu,  esikhundleni samatye isinyithi; isiveleli sakho ndisenze uxolo,  abaphathi bakho ndibenze ubulungisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:18">60:18</a> Akuyi kuba savakala lugonyamelo ezweni lakho, imbuqo nolwaphulo emideni yakho; iindonga zakho ukuzibiza wothi luSindiso, namasango akho uthi yiNdumiso.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:19">60:19</a> Ilanga aliyi kuba saba sisikhanyiso kuwe emini, nenyanga ingakukhanyiseli, ukuze kube mhlophe kuwe; uYehova uya kuba sisikhanyiso esingunaphakade kuwe, uThixo wakho abe sisihombo sakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:20">60:20</a> Aliyi kuba satshona ilanga lakho, ingafi nenyanga yakho;  kuba uYehova uya kuba sisikhanyiso esingunaphakade kuwe,  zizaliseke iimini zesijwili sakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:21">60:21</a> Abantu bakho bayakuba ngamalungisa bonke bephela, balidle ilifa ilizwe ngonaphakade; besisithole esityelwe ndim, isenzo sesandla sam sokuba ndihombe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:22">60:22</a> Omncinanana uya kuba liwaka, noweyeleyo abe luhlanga olunamandla. Mna, Yehova, ndiya kukukhawulezisa oko ngexesha lako oko.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:1">61:1</a> UMoya weNkosi uYehova uphezu kwam; ngenxa yokuba uYehova endithambisele ukuba ndishumayeze abalulamileyo iindaba ezilungileyo. Undithume ukubopha abantliziyo zaphukileyo,  ukumemeza inkululeko kwabathinjiweyo, ukuvulwa kwamehlo kwabakhonkxiweyo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:2">61:2</a> ukumemeza umnyaka wetarhu likaYehova, nomhla wempindezelo yoThixo wethu: ukuthuthuzela bonke abanesijwili;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:3">61:3</a> ukubamisela abanesijwili baseZiyon, ukubanika isihombo sentloko esikhundleni sothuthu, ioli yemihlali esikhundleni sesijwili, ingubo yendumiso esikhundleni somoya odambayo;  ukubizwa kwabo kuthiwe yimiterebhinti yobulungisa, isityalo sikaYehova sokuhomba.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:4">61:4</a> Baya kwakha amanxuwa angunaphakade, bavuse iindawo ezichithakeleyo zangaphambili, bahlaziye imizi engamanxuwa,  iindawo ezichithakeleyo zezizukulwana ngezizukulwana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:5">61:5</a> Baya kuma abasemzini, baluse imihlambi yenu, oonyana bezinye iintlanga babe ngabalimi bomhlaba wenu, nabezidiliya zenu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:6">61:6</a> Ke nina ukubizwa kwenu, kuya kuthiwa ningababingeleli bakaYehova; kuya kuthiwa kuni, ningabalungiseleli boThixo wethu; niya kudla ubutyebi beentlanga, nindolose ninozuko lwazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:7">61:7</a> Esikhundleni sokudana kwenu niya kuzuza okuphindiweyo;  esikhundleni sehlazo baya kumemelela ngesahlulo sabo; ngako oko baya kudla ilifa eliphindiweyo ezweni labo, baya kuba novuyo olungunaphakade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:8">61:8</a> Kuba mna, Yehova, ndithanda okusesikweni, ndikuthiyile ukuphanga ngokugqwetha; ndibanika umvuzo womsebenzi wabo ngenyaniso; ndenza umnqophiso ongunaphakade nabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:9">61:9</a> Iya kwaziwa imbewu yabo ezintlangeni, baziwe nabaphume ezibilinini zabo phakathi kwezizwe; bonke abababonayo baya kubazi ukuba bayimbewu ayisikeleleyo uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:10">61:10</a> Ndinemihlali ndanemihlali ngoYehova, umphefumlo wam uya kugcoba ngoThixo wam; kuba endinxibe iingubo zosindiso, endithe wambu ngengubo yokwaleka yobulungisa, njengomyeni ononkontsho ngokombingeleli, nanjengomtshakazi evethe iimpahla zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:11">61:11</a> Kuba njengoko ilizwe livelisa izilimo zalo, njengoko umyezo untshulisa intlwayelelo yawo, yenjenjalo iNkosi uYehova ukuntshulisa ubulungisa nendumiso phambi kweentlanga zonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:1">62:1</a> Ngenxa yeZiyon andiyi kuthi tu, ngenxa yeYerusalem andiyi kuzola, bude buphume njengokusa ubulungisa bayo, nosindiso lwayo njengesikhuni esidangazelayo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:2">62:2</a> zibubone iintlanga ubulungisa bakho, nookumkani bonke babubone ubuqaqawuli bakho. Uya kubizwa ngegama elitsha, eliya kuxelwa ngumlomo kaYehova;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:3">62:3</a> ube sisithsaba sokuhomba esandleni sikaYehova, nonkontsho lobukumkani entendeni yesandla soThixo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:4">62:4</a> Akuyi kuba sathiwa kuwe unguSishiywa, nelizwe lakho akuyi kuba sathiwa kulo, Kusenkangala; ukubizwa kwakho kuya kuthiwa unguNdimnanzileyo, nelizwe lakho kuthiwe nguNokwenda; ngokuba uYehova ekunanzile, nelizwe lakho lendile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:5">62:5</a> Njengokuba indodana izeka intombi, oonyana bakho baya kuzeka wena; njengomyeni enemihlali ngomtshakazi, uThixo wakho uya kuba nemihlali ngawe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:6">62:6</a> Phezu kweendonga zakho, Yerusalem, ndimise abagcini: imini yonke nobusuku bonke abayi kuze bathi quthu; nina bakhumbuzi bakaYehova, musani ukuthi cwaka.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:7">62:7</a> Musani ukuvuma ukuba athi cwaka, ade ayizinzise, ade ayenze iYerusalem ibe yindumiso ehlabathini.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:8">62:8</a> UYehova ufunge isandla sakhe sokunene, nengalo yakhe eqinileyo, wathi, Inyaniso, ingqolowa yakhe andiyi kuba sayinika iintshaba zakho ziyidle, noonyana bolunye uhlanga bangaseli iwayini yakho entsha, owazixhamla ngayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:9">62:9</a> Kuba ngabayihlanganisileyo abaya kuyidla, badumise uYehova;  ngabayibuthayo abaya kuyisela ezintendelezweni zengcwele yam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:10">62:10</a> Phumani, phumani ngamasango; gecani indlela yabantu;  fumbani, fumbani umendo, ncothulani amatye kuwo; nyusani ibhanile phezu kwezizwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:11">62:11</a> Yabona, uYehova uvakalisile wesa eziphelweni zehlabathi,  wathi, Yithini kwintombi enguZiyon, Yabona, usindiso lwakho luyeza; yabona, umvuzo wakhe unawo, nento ayisebenzileyo iphambi kwakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:12">62:12</a> Ukubizwa kwabo kuya kuthiwa ngabantu abangcwele,  ngabakhululwa bakaYehova ngokumiselwa; ukubizwa kwakho kuthiwe,  ungofuniweyo, ungumzi ongashiyiweyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:1">63:1</a> Ngubani na lo uza evela kwaEdom, evela eBhotsera, zibomvu iingubo zakhe? Lo uyingangamsha ngesambatho sakhe, enyalasa ebuninzini bamandla akhe? Ndim, mna uthetha ngokobulungisa, mna umkhulu ukusindisa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:2">63:2</a> Yini na ukuba sibe yingqombela isambatho sakho, neengubo zakho zibe njengezoxovula esixovulelweni sewayini?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:3">63:3</a> Isifaxangelo ndisixovule ndedwa; ezizweni akubangakho bani inam; ndazixovula ndinomsindo, ndazinyasha ndishushu; igazi lazo lachaphazela iingubo zam, ndasidyobha sonke isambatho sam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:4">63:4</a> Kuba umhla wempindezelo ubusentliziyweni yam, nomnyaka wokukhulula kwam ngokuhlawulela ufikile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:5">63:5</a> Ndabheka, akwabakho mncedi; ndamangaliswa ukuba kungabikho mxhasi; yandisindisela ke ingalo yam, nobushushu bam baba ngumxhasi wam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:6">63:6</a> Ndazigqusha izizwe ndinomsindo, ndazinxilisa ndinobushushu,  ndalihlisela emhlabeni igazi lazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:7">63:7</a> Ndiya kukhankanya iinceba zikaYehova, iindumiso zikaYehova ngokokufanele konke ukusiphatha kukaYehova; nokulunga kwakhe okukhulu kwindlu kaSirayeli, awayiphatha ngako ngokwemfesane yakhe, nangokobuninzi beenceba zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:8">63:8</a> Wathi okwenene, Bangabantu bam ke, oonyana abangayi kuxoka;  waba ngumsindisi kubo ke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:9">63:9</a> Ekubandezelekeni kwabo konke wabandezeleka, nesithunywa sobuso bakhe sabasindisa; ekubathandeni kwakhe nasekubacongeni kwakhe wayebakhulula ngokumisela yena, wabafunqula; wabathwala yonke imihla yasephakadeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:10">63:10</a> Ke bona bamphikisa, bamenza buhlungu uMoya wakhe oyiNgcwele; waguquka ke, waba lutshaba kubo, walwa nabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:11">63:11</a> Baza abantu bakhe bakhumbula imihla yasephakadeni kaMoses,  bathi, Uphi na lo wabanyusa elwandle, ndawonye nomalusi womhlambi wakhe? Uphi na lowo wawubeka phakathi kwabo uMoya wobungcwele bakhe?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:12">63:12</a> wayihambisa ngasekunene kukaMoses ingalo yokuhomba kwakhe?  wawacanda amanzi phambi kwabo, ukuze azenzele igama elingunaphakade?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:13">63:13</a> wabahambisa emanzini anzongonzongo, njengehashe entlango,  abakhubeka?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:14">63:14</a> Njengeenkomo ezihla ziye entilini, uMoya kaYehova wabaphumza; wenjenjalo ukubaqhuba abantu bakho, ukuze uzenzele igama elizukileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:15">63:15</a> Bheka usemazulwini, ubone usengontsini yobungcwele bakho neyesihombo sakho. Buphi na ubukhwele bakho nobugorha bakho?  Ukusika kwezibilini zakho neemfesane zakho zibambekile kum.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:16">63:16</a> Kuba ungubawo wena, ngokuba uAbraham engasazi, uSirayeli engasinakani; wena, Yehova, unguBawo, uMkhululi wethu ligama lakho kwasephakadeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:17">63:17</a> Yini na ukuba usiyeke sidungudele, Yehova, simke ezindleleni zakho, uyiqaqadekise intliziyo yethu, singakoyiki wena? Buya, ngenxa yabakhonzi bakho, izizwe zelifa lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:18">63:18</a> Abantu bakho abangcwele badla ilifa umzuzwana;  ababandezeli bethu bayigqusha ingcwele yakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:19">63:19</a> Sisuke saba njengabo ungabalawulanga kwasephakadeni,  abangabizwanga ngegama lakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:1">64:1</a> Yoo! Wanga ungawakrazula amazulu uhle, zizamazame iintaba ebusweni bakho,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:2">64:2</a> njengomlilo uvuthisa iintsasa, njengomlilo uxhaphazelisa amanzi; ukuze ulazise igama lakho kubabandezeli bakho, zigungqe iintlanga ebusweni bakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:3">64:3</a> Ekwenzeni kwakho imisebenzi eyoyikekayo, ebe singayilindele, wanga ungehla, zizamazame iintaba ebusweni bakho!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:4">64:4</a> Kususela kwasephakadeni, abantu abevanga, abamamelanga,  neliso alibonanga Thixo ingenguwe, omenzelayo lowo ulindele kuye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:5">64:5</a> Umkhawulele onemihlali, enze ubulungisa, ekukukhumbuleni kwabo ezindleleni zakho. Yabona, wena ubunoburhalarhume, masibe ke singaboni; kudala sikwezo zinto; sosindiswa na ke?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:6">64:6</a> Ke sisuke saba njengoyinqambi sonke siphela, yanjengengubo enomzi yonke imisebenzi yethu yobulungisa; sabuna njengamagqabi sonke siphela, ubugwenxa bethu basithabatha njengomoya.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:7">64:7</a> Akwabakho ulinqulayo igama lakho, uzixhoxhayo ukuba abambelele kuwe; ngokuba ubusithelisile ubuso bakho kuthi,  wasinyibilikisa ngobugwenxa bethu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:8">64:8</a> Kaloku ke, Yehova, unguBawo; siludongwe; unguMbumbi wethu;  sisisenzo sesandla sakho, sonke siphela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:9">64:9</a> Musa ukuba noburhalarhume, Yehova, kuphele; ungabukhumbuli ubugwenxa ngonaphakade. Yabona, khawusibheke; singabantu bakho sonke siphela.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:10">64:10</a> Imizi yobungcwele bakho iyintlango, iZiyon iyintlango,  iYerusalem ilinxuwa.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:11">64:11</a> Indlu yobungcwele bethu nokuhomba kwethu, ababekudumisela kuyo oobawo, itshile ngumlilo, neento zonke ezibe zinqweneleka kuthi zichithakele.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:12">64:12</a> Uya kuzihamba na ngokwakho, zinjalonje ezo zinto, Yehova,  uthi cwaka na, usicinezele na kuphele?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:1">65:1</a> Ndangxokeka kwababengandibuzi, ndafumaneka kwababengandifuni. Ndathi, Ndikho, ndikho, kuhlanga obelungabizwa ngegama lam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:2">65:2</a> Ndolula isandla zam imini yonke kubantu abaziinjubaqa,  abahamba ngendlela engalungileyo, emva kweengcinga ezizezabo:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:3">65:3</a> abantu aba bandiqumbisayo ngamaxesha onke besebusweni bam,  bebingelela emiyezweni, beqhumisela eziteneni,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:4">65:4</a> behleli emangcwabeni, belalisa ezindaweni ezinqabileyo,  besidla inyama yehagu, ezityeni zabo ingumhluzi oyimbozisa;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:5">65:5</a> besithi, Yima, ungasondeli kum; ngokuba ndingcwele kunawe.  Abo bangumsi ezimpumlweni zam, umlilo otsha iimini zonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:6">65:6</a> Yabona, kubhaliwe phambi kwam, kwathiwa, Andiyi kuthi tu,  ndingaphindezelanga; ndiya kuphindezelela esondweni lengubo yabo izenzo zenu ezigwenxa,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:7">65:7</a> nezenzo ezigwenxa zooyihlo kunye, utsho uYehova;  abaqhumiselayo ezintabeni, bandingcikiva ezindulini; ngako oko ndiya kuwulinganisela umvuzo womsebenzi wabo kuqala esondweni labo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:8">65:8</a> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Njengokuba incindi ifunyanwa esihlokweni, athi umntu, Musa ukusonakalisa, ngokuba kukho intsikelelo kuso; ndiya kwenjenjalo ngenxa yabakhonzi bam,  ukuze ndingonakalisi into yonke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:9">65:9</a> Ndiya kuvelisa imbewu kaYakobi, indlalifa yentaba yam kwaYuda, balidle ilifa abanyulwa bam, bahlale khona abakhonzi bam;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:10">65:10</a> iSharon yoba likriwa lempahla emfutshane, nentili yeAkore ibe yindawo yokubutha iinkomo ebantwini bam abandiquqeleyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:11">65:11</a> Ke nina nimshiyileyo uYehova, niyilibeleyo intaba yam engcwele, nimlungiselayo uThamsanqa isithebe, nimzaliselayo uSihlo iwayini ephithikeziweyo,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:12">65:12</a> ndinimisele ikrele, niguqele ukusikwa nonke mpela, ngenxa enokuba ndanibizayo, anasabela; ndathetha, aneva; nesuka nenza okubi emehlweni am; nanyula endingakunanzileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:13">65:13</a> Ngako oko itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi, Yabonani, abakhonzi bam baya kudla, ke nina niya kulamba; yabonani, abakhonzi bam baya kusela, ke nina niya kunxanwa; yabonani, abakhonzi bam baya kuvuya, ke nina niya kudana.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:14">65:14</a> Yabonani, abakhonzi bam baya kumemelela ngokuchwayitha kwentliziyo, ke nina niya kukhala ngumvandedwa wentliziyo,  nibhomboloze kukwaphuka komoya wenu.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:15">65:15</a> Niya kulishiya igama lenu libe sisishwabulo kubanyulwa bam, ikubulale iNkosi uYehova, ke ibabize ngalimbi igama abakhonzi bayo;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:16">65:16</a> ngokokude athi ozisikeleleyo elizweni, azisikelele ngoThixo wenyaniso; athi ofungayo elizweni, afunge uThixo wenyaniso; ngokuba zilityelwe iimbandezelo zangaphambili,  nangokuba zisithele emehlweni am.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:17">65:17</a> Ngokuba, niyabona, ndidala amazulu amatsha nehlabathi elitsha; angakhunjulwa awokuqala, angenyuki athi qatha entliziyweni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:18">65:18</a> Hayi, yibani nemihlali, nigcobe nanini yiloo nto ndiyidalayo; ngokuba, yabonani, ndiyayidala iYerusalem ukuba igcobe, nabantu bayo ukuba babe nemihlali.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:19">65:19</a> Ndiya kugcoba ngeYerusalem, ndibe nemihlali ngabantu bam,  lingabi savakala khona ilizwi lokulila nelizwi lokukhala.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:20">65:20</a> Akuyi kuba savela khona usana oluneentsuku, nexhego elingayizalisanga imihla yalo; kuba umfana uya kufa engominyaka ilikhulu ezelwe, atshabhiswe umoni engominyaka ilikhulu ezelwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:21">65:21</a> Baya kwakha izindlu, bazihlale; batyale izidiliya, badle iziqhamo zazo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:22">65:22</a> Abayi kwakha, kuhlale bambi; abayi kutyala, kudle bambi;  kuba iya kuba njengemihla yomthi imihla yabantu bam, badle into esetyenzwe zizandla zabo abanyulwa bam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:23">65:23</a> Abayi kuzixhamla ngokulambathayo, bazalele ukhwankqiso;  ngokuba bayimbewu ayisikeleleyo uYehova, nabaphume ezibilinini zabo banabo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:24">65:24</a> Kuya kuthi bengekabizi, ndisabele; besathetha, ndibe sendivile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:25">65:25</a> Kuya kudla ndawonye ingcuka nemvana, ingonyama idle umququ njengenkomo; inyoka, sibe luthuli isonka sayo. Aziyi kwenza bubi, zonakalise, kuyo yonke intaba yam engcwele; utsho uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:1">66:1</a> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Amazulu ayitrone yam, ihlabathi sisihlalo seenyawo zam. Iyini na le ndlu, niya kundakhela yona?  Iyini na le ndawo yokuphumla kwam?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:2">66:2</a> Zonke ezo zinto sazenza isandla sam, zabakho ke zonke ezo zinto; utsho uYehova; ndibheka kulo, kolusizana, komoya waphukileyo, kogubhayo ngelizwi lam.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:3">66:3</a> Oxhela inkomo unjengesixabela-mntu; obingelela igusha ngumsiki wenja; onyusa umnikelo wokudla ngumnyusi wegazi lehagu; okhumbuza ngoqhumiselo lwentlaka emhlophe ngosikelela into ebubutshinga. Bezinyulele nje iindlela zabo, umphefumlo wabo wawananza amazothe abo:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:4">66:4</a> nam ke ndiya kunyula iimfeketho zokufeketha ngabo,  ndibazisele izinto ezibanxunguphalisayo; ngenxa enokuba ndabizayo, akwabakho usabelayo; ndathetha, abeva; besuka benza ububi emehlweni am, banyula nento endingayinanzileyo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:5">66:5</a> Liveni ilizwi likaYehova, nina nigubhayo ngelizwi lakhe;  uthi, Abazalwana benu abanithiyayo, abanigxothayo kubo ngenxa yegama lam, bathi, Makazizukise uYehova, sibone imivuyo yenu;  baya kudana ke bona.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:6">66:6</a> Phulaphulani isandi esiphuma kuwo umzi; ilizwi eliphuma etempileni; ilizwi likaYehova, ephindezela impatho yeentshaba zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:7">66:7</a> Ingekazibhijabhiji, yazala; ingekezi inimbakuyo, yathi tyibilili umntwana oyinkwenkwe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:8">66:8</a> Ngubani na okhe weva kunjalo? Ngubani na okhe wabona izinto ezinjalo? Kuya kuzalwa ilizwe ngamini-nye na? Kuzalwa uhlanga ngasihlandlo sinye na? Ngokuba isathi ukuthi ukuzibhijabhija,  yabazala onyana bayo iZiyon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:9">66:9</a> Mna ndingavelisisa na, ndingazalisi? utsho uYehova;  ndingathi mna ndizalisayo ndivingce na? utsho uThixo wakho.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:10">66:10</a> Vuyisanani neYerusalem, nigcobe ngayo, nonke bayithandayo;  yenzani imihlali nibe nemihlali, nonke bayenzalayo isijwili;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:11">66:11</a> ukuze nanye nihluthe libele leentuthuzelo zayo, ukuze nishube, nixhamle ukwehlisa kozuko lwayo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:12">66:12</a> Ngokuba uYehova utsho ukuthi, Yabonani, ndisingisa uxolo kuyo njengomlambo, nozuko lweentlanga njengesihlambo esikhukulayo, ukuze nanye; niya kubelekwa ephangweni,  niteketiswe emathangeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:13">66:13</a> Njengomntu othu thuzelwa ngunina, ndiya kwenjenjalo mna ukunithuthuzela, nithuthuzelwe eYerusalem.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:14">66:14</a> Nobona, ibe nemihlali intliziyo yenu, ahlume amathambo enu njengohlaza, sazeke isandla sikaYehova ebakhonzini bakhe,  azibhavumele iintshaba zakhe.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:15">66:15</a> Kuba, yabonani, uYehova uya kuza ngomlilo,  zinjengesaqhwithi iinqwelo zakhe zokulwa, ukuze abuyekeze umsindo wakhe ngobushushu, nokukhalima kwakhe ngamalangatye omlilo.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:16">66:16</a> Kuba uYehova uya kuyigweba ngomlilo nangekrele lakhe inyama yonke, babe baninzi ababuleweyo nguYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:17">66:17</a> Abo bazingcwalisayo, bazihlambululele imiyezo, bexelisa omnye ongaphakathi, badle inyama yehagu, nento enezothe,  nempuku, baya kuphela kunye; utsho uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:18">66:18</a> Mna ke, ndiyazazi izenzo zabo neengcinga zabo. Kobakho ixesha lokuba zihlanganisane zonke iintlanga neelwimi, zize zibubone ubuqaqawuli bam;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:19">66:19</a> ndomisa umqondiso phakathi kwazo, ndithume abasindileyo kuzo, baye ezintlangeni ezingooTarshishe, noPuli, noLudi,  abatyedi besaphetha; ezingooTubhali noYavan, eziqithini ezikude ezingazivanga iindaba zam, ezingabubonanga ubuqaqawuli bam,  babuxele ubuqaqawuli bam ezintlangeni.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:20">66:20</a> Baya kubazisa bonke abazalwana benu, bevela nabo ezintlangeni zonke, bengumnikelo kuYehova, bekhwele emahasheni,  nasezinqwelweni, nasemathaleni, nakoondlebende,  nakwiinkamelakazi, benyuke entabeni yam engcwele eYerusalem,  utsho uYehova; kwanjengokuba oonyana bakaSirayeli bewuzisa umnikelo wokudla ngesitya esihlambulukileyo endlwini kaYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:21">66:21</a> Ndothabatha nakuzo ezo, zibe ngababingeleli nabaLevi;  utsho uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:22">66:22</a> Kuba njengoko amazulu amatsha nehlabathi elitsha endiza kuwenza, amiyo phambi kwam, utsho uYehova, iya kwenjenjalo ukuma imbewu yenu negama lenu;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:23">66:23</a> kuthi kuphikelane nokuthwasa kweenyanga zonke, kuphikelane neesabatha zonke, ukuza kwenyama yonke, ukuba iqubude phambi kwam; utsho uYehova.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:24">66:24</a> Baya kuphuma babone izidumbu zamadoda akreqileyo kum; kuba iimpethu zabo aziyi kufa, nomlilo wabo ungacimi, babe linyumnyezi kuluntu lonke.</p> 
 <p></p><hr>
